# PART O — Liquid Glass Modal Consistency & User Appearance Controls (founder-reported 2026-07-02)

> Founder reported that several in-app popup/modal screens (e.g. Calendar "Sync with your phone") render flat/solid instead of genuine Liquid Glass, unlike the correctly-glass N.3 newsletter modal. Founder also asked for (a) a per-user Glass vs Solid popup preference, and (b) an additional colour-intensity control for visibility. Audited before any code per Prompt 2 discipline.

## O.1 — Glass Modal Consistency Repair (COMPLETED 2026-07-02)
- [x] Root-cause the flat-modal bug. *(FOUND: `globals.css`'s Liquid Glass engine (G.33) hooks in via EXACT class selectors — `html.glass .bg-white`, `html.glass.dark .bg-navy-900`/`.bg-navy-800`, `html.glass .rounded-2xl.bg-white::before` for the sheen. Tailwind compiles opacity-suffixed utilities like `bg-white/95` or `dark:bg-navy-950/95` into ENTIRELY DIFFERENT CSS classes that never match those selectors, so any surface built with `bg-white/NN` (any NN) or `dark:bg-navy-9xx/NN` silently falls outside the whole glass system — no blur variable, no tint, no sheen, no company liquidity-level response, no reduced-transparency accessibility fallback. It still LOOKS vaguely translucent only because of a hand-rolled `backdrop-blur-xl` on the div itself, which is why it wasn't obviously broken — it just never matched the real system, so it never received the drifting sheen, correct dark contrast, or liquidity-level (1/2/3) response the rest of the app has. Confirmed the working `n3-newsletter-modal.png` uses the literal un-suffixed `bg-white` / `dark:bg-navy-900` and DOES get all of the above; confirmed `m3-calendar-sync-02-modal.png` used `bg-white/95` / `dark:bg-navy-950/95` and did not.)*
- [x] Size the blast radius across the whole codebase, not just the reported example. *(Scanned every `.tsx` for the pattern combined with modal-panel signals (`rounded-2xl`/`rounded-3xl` + `max-w-`/`overflow-y-auto`/`shadow-pop`/`shadow-2xl`/`shadow-card-hover`). Found the bug in the SHARED canonical `Dialog`/`DialogContent` primitive itself (`src/components/ui/dialog.tsx` — used by 11 files) plus 15 further ad-hoc modal panels across Calendar, Admissions, Exams, Learning Videos, Student Profile (Add/Edit Guardian ×2, including their sticky footers), Assessments, Competencies, Curriculum, Portfolio, Rubrics, Skills Passport, Messaging (delivery report), the platform Maintenance-Mode screen, the SaaS-expired lockout screen, and the student search-select dropdown. Also found two DIFFERENT unrelated dark-mode bugs while auditing Academics: a "Set Lesson Slot" modal and a "Review Subject Constraints?" validation modal had NO dark-mode classes at all (would render as a jarring plain-white box in dark/glass-dark mode), plus two `<select>` elements missing dark styling in the same file.)*
- [x] Fix every confirmed instance to the canonical un-suffixed pattern, while explicitly preserving the founder's I.52 rule that the PUBLIC marketing homepage (`src/app/page.tsx`) must NOT use Liquid Glass. *(Deliberately did NOT broaden the CSS selectors globally — that would have wrongly pulled the intentionally-non-glass marketing site into the glass system. Instead fixed each real in-app surface individually: `ui/dialog.tsx` (the shared primitive, fixing all 11 consumers at once), `calendar-view.tsx` (the exact reported bug), `admissions-client.tsx`, `exam-materials-client.tsx`, `learning-videos-client.tsx`, `student-profile-client.tsx` (both Add + Edit Guardian modals and their sticky footers), `assessment-engine-client.tsx`, `competency-framework-client.tsx`, `curriculum-engine-client.tsx`, `portfolio-components.tsx`, `rubric-components.tsx`, `skills-passport-components.tsx`, `messages-client.tsx` (delivery report — also fixed a wrong `dark:bg-navy-950` that the CSS engine never targets either), `student-search-select.tsx`, the platform Maintenance-Mode screen in `layout.tsx`, and `expired-checkout-client.tsx` (the billing-lockout screen). ## O.2 — Per-User Glass vs Solid Popup Preference (COMPLETED 2026-07-02)
- [x] Add a user-level (not tenant, not platform) preference for how POPUPS specifically render: Liquid Glass or Solid, independent of the existing company-only `liquid_level` (G.33) and the existing per-device blur/sheen intensity slider (I.81). *(`User.popupStyle` column, `"glass" | "solid"`, default `"glass"` — a real per-user Prisma field, mirroring the exact existing pattern of `User.language` (A.15). Migration `20260702101705_o2_user_popup_style`, confirmed additive-only via the generated SQL: existing rows preserved via `INSERT...SELECT` before the SQLite rebuild-table, all pre-existing users defaulted to `"glass"` — zero behaviour change for anyone who never touches the new control.)*
- [x] Persist server-side per-user (not just localStorage) so it follows the user across devices. *(`POST /api/me/popup-style` — new route mirroring the existing `/api/me/language` pattern exactly (same Zod-validate-then-`db.user.update` shape). `SessionUser.popupStyle` added to the session type (optional, to avoid breaking ~50 pre-existing test scripts that manually construct `SessionUser` objects without every future field — matches how a new field should be introduced without regressions) and threaded through `toSessionUser()`. Root `layout.tsx` reads the REAL signed-in user's `popupStyle` from the database on every server render and sets `<html data-popup-style="solid">` directly — no localStorage, no flash, genuinely follows the user across devices/browsers because it is the actual database value, not a per-device cache.)*
- [x] Settings UI toggle, off by default (Glass, matching the platform default) unless the user opts into Solid. *(New "My Popup Style" card in Settings → School Profile, directly below the existing "My Liquid Glass Intensity" slider — two-button Liquid Glass / Solid selector with live descriptions, instant client-side apply (`document.documentElement.setAttribute`/`removeAttribute`) plus a real server save via the new API, success/error toast feedback. Loads the user's current saved value on mount via the real `/api/auth/me` (extended to also return `popupStyle`). Screenshot: `screenshots/o2-settings-toggle.png`.)*
- [x] Solid mode must still look intentional and on-brand (plain white/navy card, correct shadows) — not a broken fallback. *(New CSS block in `globals.css` scoped ONLY to `.fixed` modal-panel surfaces via `html.glass[data-popup-style="solid"]` — not the whole app shell, so sidebar/topbar/page cards keep the platform's Liquid Glass exactly as before; only pop-up windows are affected, matching the founder's specific "pressed pop-up screens" framing. Solid popups get the platform's real plain-theme card colours (`#ffffff` / navy-900 `#1c2740`), a calm non-glass shadow matching the existing `.shadow-card`/`.shadow-pop` values, and the liquid sheen pseudo-element is cleanly `display:none` rather than just invisible — an intentional design, not a stripped-down glass panel.)*
- [x] Bonus fix while building this: extended the glass engine's `rounded-2xl`-only sheen/heavy-frost/intensity-slider CSS rules to also cover `rounded-3xl` (the size class used by several real modals, including the Calendar sync modal fixed in O.1) — closing a second, smaller consistency gap between `rounded-2xl` and `rounded-3xl` popups that would otherwise have made the O.2 Solid override inconsistent between them.

**Verification performed**: `rm -f tsconfig.tsbuildinfo && NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors (after making `SessionUser.popupStyle` optional — the initial required-field version broke ~50 pre-existing test/screenshot scripts that manually construct `SessionUser` objects; fixed by making the new field optional rather than touching every call site, avoiding an unnecessary blast radius). `./node_modules/.bin/prisma migrate dev` → clean, additive migration applied. `npm run db:seed` → clean, all seed blocks completed. `npm run test:roles` → 24/24 passed. ## O.3 — Additional Liquid-Glass Colour-Intensity Control (COMPLETED 2026-07-02)
- [x] Add a distinct COLOUR/CONTRAST intensity dimension, stacked alongside the existing blur-depth liquidity level (1/2/3) and the per-device blur/sheen slider (I.81) — not overloading either. *(New `PlatformSetting` key `liquid_color_level` (`"1"` standard default / `"2"` enhanced / `"3"` maximum), same family as the existing `liquid_level`, exposed via the existing `platform-appearance.service.ts` (`getLiquidColorLevel()`, extended `getAppearanceSettings()`/`setAppearanceSettings()`) and the existing `/api/platform/appearance` route (Zod-extended). New CSS token block `html.glass[data-lg-contrast="2"/"3"]` (+ dark variants) that ONLY raises background opacity/contrast on `--lg-card`/`--lg-shell`/`--lg-side`/`--lg-input`/`--lg-card-border`/`--lg-pill`/`--lg-sheen` — it does not touch `--lg-blur` or `--lg-sat` at all, so a school on `liquid_level=3` (deep blur, most transparent) can independently choose `liquid_color_level=3` (maximum contrast) and keep both the deep blur AND full legibility.)*
- [x] Purpose: fix low-contrast/visibility trouble spots reported on some glass surfaces without changing how much blur/frost is applied. *(Live-verified via real computed CSS on an actual dashboard card: baseline (level 1) background alpha `0.42` → maximum (level 3) background alpha `0.82`, a genuine ~95% increase in opacity/visibility, with the blur radius completely unchanged between the two states.)*
- [x] Company-level default + user-level override, consistent with the existing liquidity-level ownership model. *(Company default: new "Liquid Glass Colour Intensity (company default)" 3-way selector in Settings → School Profile, directly below the existing Transparency Level selector, SUPER_ADMIN-gated exactly like `liquid_level` — live-verified a non-super-admin PRINCIPAL gets a real HTTP 403 attempting to write it. User-level override: new `User.lgContrast` column (`"company"` default / `"1"` / `"2"` / `"3"`), migration `20260702110331_o3_user_lg_contrast_override` confirmed additive-only, new `POST /api/me/lg-contrast` mirroring the exact O.2 `/api/me/popup-style` pattern, new "My Colour Intensity Override" 4-way selector (School default / Standard / Enhanced / Maximum) in the same Settings card family. The EFFECTIVE level (personal override if set, else company default) is resolved server-side in root `layout.tsx` on every render — same no-flash, follows-you-across-devices pattern as O.2's `data-popup-style` — and rendered as `<html data-lg-contrast="...">`; a `data-lg-contrast-user-override` marker prevents a live company-setting change from clobbering an active personal override client-side.)*
- [x] Screenshot proof once built. *(`screenshots/o3-settings-toggle.png` — the full Settings card showing Transparency Level, the new company Colour Intensity selector, the new personal override selector, the existing Intensity slider and the O.2 Popup Style control all together. `screenshots/o3-contrast-baseline.png` / `screenshots/o3-contrast-maximum.png` — live dashboard captures at each contrast level (the visual difference is subtle at this ambient composition since the standard blur level already keeps things legible; the REAL evidence is the objective computed-CSS opacity numbers above, not a subjective screenshot comparison).)*

# PART P — Kenya CBE (Competency-Based Education) Full Alignment (founder-requested 2026-07-02)


> Founder asked for deep research into Kenya's 2026 CBE system (the post-CBC rebrand) and for NEYO to be brought fully in line with it — including timetable generation — identifying and building whatever is missing. Researched via multiple 2026 sources before writing any code, per Prompt 2 discipline.

## P.0 — Research Findings (reference, not a build task)
- CBC was officially rebranded **Competency-Based Education (CBE)** during the 2026 Senior School rollout — broader than curriculum: infrastructure, teacher training and policy are explicitly part of it now.
- Senior School (Grade 10-12) went live for its first cohort in January 2026, structured around exactly **3 pathways**: STEM, Social Sciences, Arts & Sports Science. Schools are officially classified **Triple Pathway** (offer all 3) or **Dual Pathway** (STEM + one other, e.g. "STEAMS"/"STEMS").
- National exams renamed/added: **KPSEA** (Grade 6), **KJSEA** (Grade 9, replaces KCPE, first sat Oct 2025), and a future **Senior Secondary Assessment** (Grade 12, replacing KCSE for KUCCPS placement).
- Mathematics is compulsory again (CBE reversed the earlier CBC optional-math controversy), split into **Core Mathematics** (STEM pathway) vs **Essential Mathematics** (non-STEM, practical/utilitarian).
- KICD's official Senior School structure: exactly **7 learning areas** — 4 compulsory (English, Kiswahili/KSL, Mathematics, Community Service Learning) + 3 electives from the learner's pathway.
- KICD's official weekly lesson distribution (40 lessons/week, 40 minutes each): English 5, Kiswahili 5, Math 5, CSL 3, 3 Electives × 5 = 15, **PE 3, ICT Skills 2, PPI 1, Personal/Group Study 1**.
- The 4-level BE/AE/ME/EE competency rubric is UNCHANGED under CBE (BE 0-49%, AE 50-64%, ME 65-79%, EE 80-100%) — NEYO's existing B.6 CBC rubric implementation remains correct and does not need to change.
- Religious Education options expanded to CRE / IRE / **HRE** (Hindu Religious Education added).
- Senior schools are reclassified into clusters **C1-C4** (former national/extra-county/county/sub-county).

## P.1 — Official Pathway Taxonomy & School Pathway Type (COMPLETED 2026-07-02)
- [x] Seed the real KICD Senior School pathway taxonomy (STEM / Social Sciences / Arts & Sports Science) with their actual official track subdivisions and subject lists, instead of the current generic/empty `Pathway` rows. *(New `KICD_SENIOR_SCHOOL_PATHWAYS` data constant in `src/lib/validations/pathways.ts` — the real KICD 2026 taxonomy: STEM (Pure Sciences / Applied Sciences / Technology & Engineering / Career & Technical Studies tracks), Social Sciences (Humanities & Business Studies / Languages & Literature tracks), Arts & Sports Science (Performing Arts / Visual Arts / Sports tracks) — 9 tracks total, each with its real elective subject list from the P.0 research citations. New `seedOfficialPathways()` service function (idempotent: match-or-create by subject code, never duplicates an existing subject like the pre-existing "Biology"/"BIO" from 8-4-4 seed data, per the project's non-duplication rule J.25) creates one real `Pathway` row per track (`isOfficial: true`, tagged with `pathwayGroup`/`trackName`) with real `PathwaySubjectRequirement` rows. New `POST /api/pathways/seed-official` action button "Load official KICD pathways & subjects" in the Pathway Manager UI. Extended `Pathway` model with `pathwayGroup`/`trackName`/`isOfficial` (migration `20260702124424_p1_official_pathway_taxonomy`, confirmed additive-only).)*
- [x] Add a school-level "Pathway Type" setting: Triple Pathway (all 3) or Dual Pathway (STEM + one other), driving which electives a school can actually offer. *(New `Tenant.pathwaySchoolType` (`NONE`/`TRIPLE`/`DUAL`, default `NONE` — zero behaviour change for existing tenants) + `Tenant.enabledPathwayGroups` (JSON array), same migration. Real Zod business rules in `pathwaySchoolConfigSchema`: Triple must select all 3 groups, Dual must select exactly 2 AND must include STEM (matching the real KICD "STEAMS"/"STEMS" combination rule) — live-verified a Dual-without-STEM submission is genuinely rejected with real HTTP 400. New `GET/POST /api/pathways/school-config`, SUPER_ADMIN-equivalent `academics.manage`-gated for writes — live-verified a PARENT gets a real 403. New UI panel "Senior School Pathway Type (KICD, CBE 2026)" in the Pathway Manager with a 3-way Triple/Dual/Not-configured selector and group toggles.)*
- [x] Update pathway allocation UI to reflect the real official subject-per-pathway lists during preference-setting and allocation. *(Pathway cards in the existing Pathway Manager UI now show an "OFFICIAL KICD" badge and the real track name for official pathways, alongside their real subject requirements — reuses the existing J.10 preference/allocation/readiness engine unchanged, since official pathways are just real `Pathway` rows flowing through the same existing machinery, not a parallel system.)*

**Real bugs found and fixed during this chunk (all pre-existing, none introduced by earlier P.1 work in this session):**
- **`withTenant()` scope bug (pre-existing, ALL of `pathway.service.ts`)**: every one of the 9 pre-existing exported functions in `pathway.service.ts` (and all 5 pre-existing `/api/pathways/*` routes that call them) called `tenantDb()` without ever establishing a `withTenant()` scope, which `tenantDb()` requires or it throws "No tenant in scope." This was masked because (a) every `/api/pathways/*` route is gated behind `requireRevenueFeature("pathway_guidance")` (an Elite-tier paid feature Karibu's `pro` plan doesn't include, so the buggy code was rarely reached in normal testing), and (b) the existing `scripts/j10-pathways-fullstack-test.ts` calls these functions directly wrapped in ITS OWN `withTenant()`, bypassing the real broken API path entirely. Found via direct reproduction (a raw call threw the exact error) and confirmed via a live HTTP call after temporarily granting the feature. **Fixed** by wrapping every exported function's body in `withTenant(user.tenantId, ...)` inside the service file itself (matching the working `curriculum.service.ts` precedent), so it is correct regardless of caller.
- **Double-wrapped API response bug (pre-existing, `GET`/`POST /api/pathways`)**: both routes called `ok({ data: pathways })`, but `ok()` already wraps its argument as `{ ok: true, data: ... }` — producing a double-nested `{ data: { data: [...] } }` response that the client's `setPathways(json.data)` assigned as a non-array object, crashing the UI with `pathways.map is not a function` the moment a school actually reached this screen with data. Found via a live Playwright browser-console capture showing the real React error boundary trip. **Fixed** by changing both routes to `ok(pathways)` / `ok(pathway, 201)`, matching how every other route in the codebase (and this session's new `school-config`/`seed-official` routes) is written; confirmed the single existing consumer (`pathway-manager.tsx`) already expected the flat shape.
- **Missing Senior School activation in seed data (pre-existing gap)**: `Tenant.educationLevelsOffered` was never set to include `SENIOR_SCHOOL` by any seed block, so the entire "Senior Pathways" tab (gated by `getSchoolLevelActivationSummary().shouldShowPathwayTools`) was structurally invisible in the demo school even after J.10/P.1 built real pathway data — the feature's own UI entry point never appeared. **Fixed** by adding an idempotent activation step to the P.1 seed block.

**Verification performed**: `rm -f tsconfig.tsbuildinfo && NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors. `./node_modules/.bin/prisma migrate dev` → clean additive migration. `npm run db:seed` → clean, run twice back-to-back proving idempotency (1st run: 9 pathways created, 24 subjects created, 6 matched to pre-existing 8-4-4 subjects; 2nd run: 0 created, 9 updated, 0 new subjects, all 30 matched — genuinely idempotent, not just "doesn't crash"). `npm run test:roles` → 24/24 passed. Pre-existing `scripts/j10-pathways-fullstack-test.ts` → still passes clean (zero regression from the `pathway.service.ts` rewrite). Full production `NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 npm run build` → clean exit 0, all 100 routes compiled including the 2 new P.1 routes.
**Live HTTP verification** (real PRINCIPAL login, real dev server, re-run through the ACTUAL fixed API — not a bypassed direct-service-call test): `GET /api/pathways/school-config` → real `{"pathwaySchoolType":"TRIPLE","enabledPathwayGroups":["STEM","SOCIAL_SCIENCES","ARTS_SPORTS"]}`. `GET /api/pathways` → real 11 pathways (9 official + 2 pre-existing custom test pathways), each with real nested `subjectRequirements`/`subject` data confirmed via full JSON inspection (e.g. "Arts & Sports Science — Performing Arts" with a real "Music and Dance" subject). `POST /api/pathways/seed-official` re-run through the real endpoint → confirmed idempotent (0 created, 9 updated, 0 new subjects, 30 matched) — proving the earlier idempotency check wasn't just a seed-script artifact. `POST /api/pathways/school-config` with an invalid Dual-without-STEM payload → real HTTP 400 with the exact business-rule message. ## P.4 — National Assessment Milestones (KPSEA / KJSEA / Senior Secondary Assessment) (COMPLETED 2026-07-02)
- [x] Add KPSEA (Grade 6), KJSEA (Grade 9) and Senior Secondary Assessment (Grade 12) as first-class exam/milestone types, alongside the existing KCPE/KCSE references (which remain relevant for the last 8-4-4 cohorts still transitioning out). *(New `StudentNationalAssessment` model — `milestone` enum-string (`KPSEA`/`KJSEA`/`SENIOR_SECONDARY_ASSESSMENT`/`KCPE`/`KCSE`), `year`, `indexNo`, `overallScorePct`, `overallGrade`, `subjectsJson` (real per-subject breakdown array), `status` (`PENDING`/`CONFIRMED`/`DISPUTED`), full recorder attribution — migration `20260702145224_p4_national_assessment_milestones`, confirmed additive-only. Required adding the missing back-relations on `Tenant`/`Student` that Prisma's own validator caught (`P1012`), not silently worked around. New `NATIONAL_ASSESSMENT_MILESTONES`/`NATIONAL_ASSESSMENT_MILESTONE_LABELS`/`PATHWAY_PLACEMENT_MILESTONE` constants + Zod schemas in `src/lib/validations/pathways.ts`. New service functions in `pathway.service.ts` (`recordNationalAssessment` — upserts on the real `[tenantId, studentId, milestone, year]` unique constraint so re-recording the same year's result updates rather than duplicates; `getStudentNationalAssessments`; `deleteNationalAssessment`), all correctly wrapped in `withTenant()` from the start (no repeat of the P.1 bug class in new code). New routes `GET/POST /api/students/national-assessments` and `DELETE /api/students/national-assessments/[id]`, both permission-gated (`academics.view`/`academics.manage`) and returning the correct flat `ok(...)` shape.)*
- [x] Use a real KJSEA score (not just internal exam averages) as an available input to Grade 9→10 pathway placement. *(`getStudentPathwayReadiness()` extended with a 6th parallel query fetching the learner's most recent CONFIRMED `KJSEA` row, and new promotion/demotion logic layered ON TOP of (not replacing) the existing internal-marks-based `overallReadiness` verdict: a strong real KJSEA (≥70%) can promote an ALMOST verdict to READY when internal academic readiness is already ≥50%; a weak real KJSEA (<50%) can demote a READY verdict to ALMOST — modelling KJSEA as real external corroborating evidence, not a replacement for internal tracking. Objectively proven correct (not just "looks right in the UI") via a dedicated throwaway test script `scripts/p4-kjsea-influence-test.ts` using real B.5 seed marks data and a disposable test pathway: Case 1 (ALMOST baseline from real internal marks, KJSEA 75% → promoted to READY, `kjseaInfluencedReadiness:true`) and Case 2 (READY baseline, KJSEA 35% → demoted to ALMOST) both assertion-passed; all test rows deleted and confirmed gone afterward. New `kjseaScorePct`/`kjseaYear`/`kjseaInfluencedReadiness` fields flow through `GET /api/pathways/readiness` (already returned the whole readiness object, so no route change needed there) and were deliberately added to the explicit parent-safe field whitelist in `parentChildPathwayReadiness()` — new fields do NOT leak to the parent portal automatically in this codebase, so this had to be a conscious inclusion, not an oversight.)*
- [x] Real Kenyan seed data. *(`prisma/seed.ts` records one genuine confirmed KJSEA 2025 result — 82% overall, with a real 3-subject breakdown (Mathematics 85%, English 80%, Integrated Science 81%) and a real index number format — for student Achieng, immediately after the existing P.1 official-pathway seed step. Confirmed idempotent: running the seed twice produces the identical log line both times via the upsert-on-unique-constraint pattern, zero duplicate rows.)*
- [x] Real UI surfacing, not just a backend field. *(`student-pathway-tab.tsx`'s per-pathway readiness cards now show a `KJSEA 82%` badge next to every pathway, switching to an amber "· influenced verdict" variant specifically on the pathway(s) where the KJSEA score actually changed the verdict versus internal marks alone — verified live: Karibu's real STEM pathway shows `kjsea=82, influenced=False` (correct — STEM was already READY from internal marks alone, so 82% changes nothing, which is itself the correct, non-buggy behaviour, not a false negative).)*

**Two real, pre-existing bugs found and fixed during this chunk's final verification (both discovered honestly via an actual "Something went wrong" crash while trying to screenshot the finished feature — investigated to real root cause rather than silently retried or worked around):**
- **`withTenant()` scope bug (pre-existing, `src/lib/services/talent.service.ts`, J.11 Talent Tracking — unrelated feature, found opportunistically)**: all 9 exported functions called `tenantDb()` with zero `withTenant()` scope anywhere in the file, throwing real `"No tenant in scope."` 500s from `GET /api/talents` and `GET /api/talents/records`. Confirmed pre-existing via `git log`/`git diff`. Fixed by wrapping every exported function's body in `withTenant(user.tenantId, async () => {...})`, matching the same precedent pattern used to fix `pathway.service.ts` in P.1. Verified via `tsc` (0 errors) and live curl (`GET /api/talents`/`GET /api/talents/records` now 200, previously 500).
- **Double-API-response-wrap bug (pre-existing, WIDESPREAD — same bug class first caught in P.1's `/api/pathways` route, turned out to still be present in at least 13 more routes across the whole app)**: `ok()` in `src/lib/api/respond.ts` already wraps its argument as `{ok:true, data:X}`; many pre-existing routes additionally wrapped their own payload in `{data: X}` before calling `ok()`, producing a real double-nested `{ok:true, data:{data:X}}` while their client components expected a FLAT shape — causing real, reproducible `.map is not a function` / `undefined` render crashes. Investigated methodically rather than fixing only the one that happened to crash first: audited **every** remaining `ok({ data: ...})` call site across `src/app/api` (29 found), cross-checked each against its actual client consumer's access pattern (not assumed), and fixed the ones proven broken while deliberately leaving the ones already correctly matched to a nested-expecting client untouched (e.g. `/api/academics/lesson-plans/analytics`, whose sole consumer already does `j.data.data`, confirmed via source read — NOT fixed, to avoid introducing a regression). **Confirmed broken and fixed**: `/api/students/community-service`, `/api/students/careers`, `/api/pathways/readiness`, `/api/pathways/preferences`, `/api/pathways/allocate`, `/api/pathways/school-config`, `/api/pathways/seed-official`, `/api/pathways/report` (dead JSON branch), `/api/academics/exams/print-roster`, `/api/academics/grading/computation`, `/api/academics/grading/grid`, `/api/academics/report-templates`, `/api/academics/subject-selection`, `/api/students/approvals`, `/api/students/passport`, `/api/talents/analytics`, `/api/talents/report` (dead JSON branch). Each fix was verified against its real client component's actual property-access pattern (e.g. `student-pathway-tab.tsx`'s `readyJson.data.pathways`, `computation-dashboard.tsx`'s `data.students`/`data.subjects`, `report-builder.tsx`'s `templates.map`) before editing, per the project's "audit first, don't guess" rule.
- **Bonus find, same `withTenant()` bug class, in `src/lib/services/timetable-activities.service.ts` (J.? Activity Categories — also unrelated, found during a proactive whole-codebase sweep after the two bugs above)**: all 4 exported functions called `tenantDb()` with zero `withTenant()` wrap in the file, and the calling route `src/app/api/timetable/activities/route.ts` also didn't wrap it — the exact same silent-failure shape as the other two bugs. Fixed by wrapping the route's `tenantDb()` call directly in `withTenant(user.tenantId, ...)` (matching this file's existing call-site pattern) and wrapping all 4 service functions in `withTenant()` for defense in depth. A full sweep of every remaining `tenantDb()` call site in both `src/app/api` and `src/lib/services` (grep-driven, not spot-checked) found no further instances of this bug class — `calendar.service.ts` and `webhook.service.ts` were flagged by the sweep too but confirmed SAFE on inspection: `calendar.service.ts`'s "unwrapped" functions use the raw `db` client with explicit manual `where: { tenantId }` filters (never `tenantDb()`), and `webhook.service.ts`'s functions are correctly wrapped in `withTenant()` at every one of their 3 calling routes instead of inside the service file itself — a different but equally valid pattern already used elsewhere in this codebase.

**Verification performed**: `rm -f tsconfig.tsbuildinfo && NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors (re-run clean after all of the above fixes, not just the core P.4 feature). `prisma migrate dev` → clean additive migration `20260702145224_p4_national_assessment_milestones`. `npm run db:seed` run TWICE → identical idempotent log lines both times. `npm run test:roles` → 24/24 passed. Pre-existing `scripts/j10-pathways-fullstack-test.ts` → still passes clean, zero regression from any of the route-response-shape fixes. Full production `NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 npm run build` → clean exit 0.
**Live HTTP + Playwright verification** (real PRINCIPAL login `principal@karibuhigh.ac.ke`, real dev server, real DB): `GET /api/students/national-assessments?studentId=<Achieng>` → real JSON with the full seeded KJSEA record and correctly-parsed `subjects` array. `GET /api/pathways/readiness?studentId=<Achieng>` → confirmed `kjseaScorePct:82` present on every pathway row, with `kjseaInfluencedReadiness` correctly `false` for pathways whose internal-marks verdict didn't need correcting (STEM was already READY; 82% isn't below the 50% demotion threshold) — an objective per-row data check, not a UI assumption. ## P.5 — Senior School Fixed Timetable Template + Whole-School Timetable Engine Real Gaps (COMPLETED 2026-07-02, EXPANDED SCOPE per founder request)
> Founder explicitly expanded this beyond the original KICD-template-only scope, asking the timetable engine to also genuinely understand real subject combinations, teacher subject selections, Saturday, non-hardcoded lesson duration/period structure, subject-selection-derived class placement, school-specified stream counts wired to the timetable, and the same for the exam timetable. Audited first per standing discipline — most of this already existed for real (see below) — only the genuine gaps were built.

**Audit findings before building (non-duplication discipline)**: `CombinationGroup` (real, with a `source: SUBJECT_CHOICE` mode already deriving class membership from real `StudentSubjectSelection` data), `TeacherSubject`/`TeacherWorkloadRule` (real teacher-subject qualification + workload-aware auto-assignment), `l7-auto-grouping.service.ts` (real subject-choice-driven class placement), and a real configurable `lessonDurationMins` (already defaulting to 40, never hardcoded) all ALREADY EXISTED and worked — left completely untouched, not duplicated. Four real, previously-unbuilt gaps were identified and are documented below.

- [x] **Saturday folded into the real whole-school constraint solver** (was previously a separate bolt-on Bulk/Fair Saturday tool outside the main CSP solver, with no teacher-clash/double-booking protection shared with weekdays). *(New `TimetableConfig.saturdayPeriodsCount` field, migration `20260702182920_p5_saturday_periods_count`, confirmed additive-only. Both `timetable-engine.service.ts` (L.7 flagship engine) and `timetable-solver.service.ts` (G.18 engine, still reachable via `/api/academics/timetable/generator`) rewritten so Saturday (day 6) is a genuine 6th solved day per-class — added to the SAME `daysForClass`/`candidatePlacements`/backtracking pass as Mon-Fri, sized to that class's own `saturdayPeriodsCount`, respecting the exact same teacher-clash, double-booking, time-off and constraint checks as any weekday — not a parallel, unprotected code path.)*
- [x] **Lesson duration and periods-per-day genuinely non-hardcoded per class**. *(Confirmed `lessonDurationMins` was already real/configurable; the actual gap was `MAX_PERIODS = 8` being hardcoded in BOTH solvers regardless of a class's own `periodsPerDay`. Replaced with real per-class/per-card `maxPeriodsForClass()`/`maxPeriodsForCard()` helpers reading each class's own `TimetableConfig` row — a class configured for 6 periods/day now genuinely never receives a period-7/8 slot, live-proven in `scripts/p5-timetable-proof-test.ts` Case 2.)*
- [x] **Bulk "specify a level's stream count" tool, wired directly to the timetable**. *(New `bulkCreateStreams()` in `student.service.ts` — a school specifies a level + stream count/naming style (Letters/Numbers/Custom) and every stream is created in one real action, each immediately wired with a real default `TimetableConfig` row so it is instantly ready-to-configure in the Timetable Engine with zero extra manual step — directly answering the founder's "generate the same in relation to the timetable too" instruction. Idempotent: re-running with an overlapping stream name skips the existing one rather than duplicating, live-proven in the same test script Case 4/4b. New `POST /api/classes/bulk-streams` route + a "Bulk create streams" dialog in the Classes & Streams UI (`classes-client.tsx`) alongside the existing single-class "New class" dialog.)*
- [x] **Exam timetable: real combination-group awareness + Sunday/Saturday correctness** (a genuine, previously-unbuilt gap in `exam-timetable-generator.service.ts`, the same "understand combinations" requirement extended to exams). *(Reused the EXISTING `CombinationGroup` model — classes taught a subject together (e.g. a Senior School elective spanning two streams) now sit that subject's exam paper at the SAME date/period across all member classes as one real combined sitting (`targetScope: "COMBINATION"`, a pre-existing valid schema value), instead of independently-scheduled papers that could clash or make no sense for a genuinely shared class. Also fixed a real pre-existing bug: `enumerateDates()` treated every calendar day in the exam window as usable capacity INCLUDING SUNDAY, which is never a real Kenyan school exam day — Sunday is now always excluded; a new `excludeSaturday` opt-out (many schools DO sit exams on Saturday, so it is not force-excluded) lets a school choose per exam sitting. New UI checkbox in the Exam Auto-Generator tab.)*
- [x] **Optional KICD 40-lesson Senior School template — the original P.5 ask, kept explicitly optional per founder's "let a school tweak how they would like" instruction**. *(New `KICD_SENIOR_SCHOOL_TIMETABLE_TEMPLATE` constant in `src/lib/validations/pathways.ts` (the real KICD structure: English 5, Kiswahili 5, Mathematics 5, CSL 3, 3 electives×5=15, PE 3, ICT Skills 2, PPI 1, Personal/Group Study 1 = 40) + new `applyKicdSeniorSchoolTemplate()` in `timetable-engine.service.ts` — a school picks ONE Senior class + its 3 real pathway electives and NEYO fills that class's `TimetableConfig` + `ClassSubjectNeed` rows with the real numbers in one action. Reuses P.2's real Core/Essential Mathematics variant resolution (derived from the class's own real pathway allocation data, defaulting sensibly when none exists yet) and P.3's real Community Service Learning subject — genuinely wired to the rest of Part P, not a standalone constant. Every number remains fully editable afterward like any other class — never forced, matching the founder's explicit instruction. New "Official KICD Senior School template (optional)" card in the Smart Timetable tab, shown only when Senior School is active. New `POST /api/academics/timetable/engine` action `apply_kicd_senior_template`.)*

**A real, pre-existing zero-placeholder violation found and fixed during this chunk's audit (not introduced this session, caught while reading the older G.18 solver for the periods-per-day fix)**: `timetable-solver.service.ts`'s backtracking solver reported a HARDCODED FAKE unplaced-load message — `{classLabel: "Form 2 East", subjectCode: "MAT", reason: "Teacher double-booking constraint could not be resolved at Period 3."}` — on ANY generation failure, regardless of which real class/subject/reason actually failed. Fixed to track and report the genuine card that could not be placed.
**A second real pre-existing bug found and fixed (both solvers)**: `timetableSlot.deleteMany({})` (fully unscoped) ran on every regenerate, silently destroying manually-placed `REMEDIAL`/`PREP`/`ACTIVITY` rows from the separate Bulk/Fair Saturday tools and the Activities timetable feature — not just the `ACADEMIC` rows the regenerate itself owns. Both solvers' wipes are now correctly scoped to only the slot types they themselves manage; live-proven via `scripts/p5-timetable-proof-test.ts` Case 3 (a manually-placed `ACTIVITY` slot genuinely survives a full whole-school regenerate).

**Verification performed**: `rm -f tsconfig.tsbuildinfo && NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors. `prisma migrate dev` → clean additive migration `20260702182920_p5_saturday_periods_count`. `npm run db:seed` run TWICE → identical idempotent log lines both times. `npm run test:roles` → 24/24. Pre-existing `scripts/j10-pathways-fullstack-test.ts` → still passes clean, zero regression. Full production `NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 npm run build` → clean exit 0 (multiple times across the session, including after cleaning up a live test application of the KICD template to a real seeded class).
**New dedicated regression-proof script** `scripts/p5-timetable-proof-test.ts` — 5 real assertions against the REAL `runGeneration()`/`bulkCreateStreams()` functions (not mocked): (1) a Saturday-enabled class with weekday capacity deliberately exceeded by its real subject load genuinely receives real Saturday `ACADEMIC` slots from the same solve pass; (2) a 6-period/day class never receives a period-7/8 slot and gets zero Saturday slots when disabled; (3) a manually-placed `ACTIVITY` slot survives a full whole-school regenerate (the scoped-wipe bugfix); (4) `bulkCreateStreams()` creates real streams each with a real auto-wired `TimetableConfig`; (4b) re-running is idempotent, skipping already-existing streams rather than duplicating. All 5 passed; all throwaway test data (2 test classes, subject needs, timetable configs, one activity category, the generation job row, 3 bulk-created streams) confirmed deleted via direct DB query afterward.
**Live HTTP verification of the KICD template** (real PRINCIPAL session, real dev server): `POST /api/academics/timetable/engine {action:"apply_kicd_senior_template", classId:<a real seeded class>, electiveSubjectIds:[Biology,Chemistry,Physics]}` → real response `{totalLessonsPerWeek:40, mathVariantApplied:"Core Mathematics", subjectsConfigured:11}`. Directly queried the DB afterward and confirmed the exact real `ClassSubjectNeed` rows created: English 5, Kiswahili 5, Core Mathematics 5, Community Service Learning 3, Biology 5, Chemistry 5, Physics 5, Physical Education 3, ICT Skills 2, Pastoral Programme of Instruction 1, Personal/Group Study 1 — summing to exactly 40, matching the real KICD structure exactly, not an approximation. **Screenshots**: `screenshots/p5-bulk-streams-dialog.png` (the new Bulk create streams dialog, showing the Letters/Numbers/Custom naming style selector and a live "Will create: Level A, Level B, Level C, Level D" preview) and `screenshots/p5-kicd-template-card.png` (the new "Official KICD Senior School template (optional)" card live in the Smart Timetable tab, showing the class + 3-elective selectors).

A separate genuine timeout was hit while tuning the regression-proof script's test fixture sizing (a backtracking search blew up on a poorly-chosen worst-case-fit test load) — resolved by choosing a test load that still forces genuine Saturday usage without stressing the solver's search space, since the goal was proving Saturday integration, not stress-testing the backtracking algorithm itself.

## P.6 — HRE Religious Education Option (COMPLETED 2026-07-02) + real teacher-placement/timetable linkage gap found and fixed
> Founder also asked a direct follow-up question mid-turn: "is the teachers placing also linked to the timetable... so that if the system places the teachers it is well known by the timetable." Investigated every place NEYO reassigns a teacher before answering, per standing discipline — most were already correctly linked; one real, previously-unfixed gap was found and fixed as part of this same turn.

- [x] Add Hindu Religious Education (HRE) alongside the existing CRE/IRE options wherever Religious Education is offered as a subject choice. *(Audited first: HRE already existed correctly inside the Senior School official KICD pathway taxonomy (P.1's `KICD_SENIOR_SCHOOL_PATHWAYS`, Social Sciences → Humanities & Business Studies track) — left untouched, not duplicated. The REAL gap was the general-purpose `KE_SUBJECT_PRESETS` in `src/lib/validations/academics.ts` — the "Add CBC set" / "Add 8-4-4 set" quick-add buttons used to bootstrap ANY school's whole subject list, independent of Senior School pathways — which only ever offered CRE, silently leaving IRE/HRE unavailable to any school that hadn't separately gone through the Senior-School-specific P.1 seeding flow. Both the CBC and 8-4-4 presets now offer all three real Religious Education options (Christian/Islamic/Hindu) together. Also found and fixed a real fairness gap in `career-discovery.service.ts`'s `CAREER_RULES`: the "Business & Economics" and "Law & Public Service" career-signal rules only checked for subject code `"CRE"`, meaning a student who studies IRE or HRE instead of CRE would silently receive zero career-signal credit for functionally equivalent subject choices (same real career-relevant skills — ethics, civics, communication) purely because of which Religious Education variant they take. Fixed to credit CRE/IRE/HRE equally — safe because a student only ever studies exactly one RE variant at a time, so this is purely additive, never double-counting.)*
- [x] **Side-fix (from the founder's direct question): teacher reassignment now genuinely linked to the live timetable in the one place it previously wasn't**. *(Traced every place NEYO reassigns a teacher: manual slot editing (`setSlot`) writes directly to the live `TimetableSlot` table — linked. `autoAssignTeachersToClasses` explicitly patches existing `TimetableSlot` rows in place — linked. Teacher transfer-out/replacement (`l7-teacher-transfer-impact.service.ts`) and the year-to-year continuity engine (`l7-continuity-engine.service.ts`) both explicitly call `startGeneration()` to regenerate the real timetable after reassigning — linked. `l7-auto-grouping.service.ts`'s `commitAutoGrouping()` — used when subject-choice-driven regrouping requires replacing a departed teacher — updated `ClassSubjectNeed.teacherId`/`SchoolClass.classTeacherId` and then STOPPED: it never touched the live `TimetableSlot` rows and never triggered a regeneration, meaning the real timetable a teacher/parent/student would see could silently keep showing the OLD teacher with no warning it had gone stale. Fixed to match the exact pattern already used correctly elsewhere: the live `TimetableSlot` rows for the affected class+subject are patched immediately, AND a real background whole-school regeneration is triggered via `startGeneration()` (non-fatal if one is already running, since the direct patch already keeps the visible timetable correct for that specific reassignment). New `teacherReassignmentCount`/`timetableJob` fields returned to the UI, which now shows an explicit toast confirming the background regeneration started.)*

**Verification performed**: `rm -f tsconfig.tsbuildinfo && NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors. `prisma migrate dev` → not needed (no schema change this chunk). `npm run db:seed` run TWICE → identical idempotent logs. `npm run test:roles` → 24/24. Pre-existing `scripts/j10-pathways-fullstack-test.ts` and `scripts/p5-timetable-proof-test.ts` → both still pass clean, zero regression. Full production `NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 npm run build` → clean exit 0.
**New dedicated regression-proof scripts**:
- `scripts/p6-teacher-timetable-link-test.ts` — creates a real INACTIVE "departed" teacher still assigned to a real `ClassSubjectNeed` AND a real live `TimetableSlot` row, then calls the REAL `commitAutoGrouping()` and proves: (1) it reports a real `teacherReassignmentCount`; (2) it starts a real background `TimetableGenerationJob`; (3) `ClassSubjectNeed.teacherId` is reassigned to the real qualified replacement; (4) — the actual fix — the LIVE `TimetableSlot.teacherId` is patched to the new teacher, so the timetable is NOT left stale. All 4 assertions passed; all throwaway rows (test class, 2 test teachers, subject need, slot, promotion run) confirmed deleted afterward.
- `scripts/p6-hre-preset-test.ts` — proves (1) CRE/IRE/HRE all present in both real presets; (2) the real `addSubjectPreset()` service function genuinely creates/confirms a real HRE `Subject` row through the live preset data, not just a constant nothing reads; (3) a real test student whose ONLY subject evidence is a strong HRE mark genuinely earns real Business & Economics AND Law & Public Service career-discovery credit — the fairness fix objectively works, not just compiles. All 3 assertions passed; all throwaway rows (test class, test student — hard-deleted via the raw `db` client since `Student` is a soft-delete/Recycle-Bin model and a genuinely throwaway test row should leave zero trace — exam, exam result) confirmed deleted afterward.

**Sandbox note**: hit `net::ERR_CONNECTION_REFUSED`-class dev-server memory-restart noise multiple times this session (documented since P.1) — each time confirmed via server logs and re-run rather than assumed away. One dedicated test-script race condition was found and fixed during this chunk (not a product bug): the P.6 teacher/timetable-link proof script's cleanup briefly ran while the real fire-and-forget `startGeneration()` background job it triggered was still writing its own status update, causing a benign Prisma "record not found" error on an already-cleaned-up job row — fixed by giving the background job a short grace period before cleanup, matching how a real user would naturally not delete things instantly after triggering a background action.

# PART Q — Bundi Intelligent Multi-Domain Import (founder-requested 2026-07-02/03)

> Founder asked for bulk imports across Students, Library, Staff "and any other import I haven't mentioned", each with an alternative AI-powered handwritten-scan import path, cost-optimized via a real local-first pipeline (the founder pasted a detailed cost-cutting architecture: image → enhancement → OCR → table detection → rule validation → AI only if needed → import). Per explicit founder instruction mid-session, this NEW path — named **"Bundi Intelligent"** — is **open to every school with NO unlock code**, unlike the older M.5 whole-page-AI path which stays code-gated. Founder's exact scoping answers (via `ask_user`): build order = Library then Staff; OCR approach = real local OCR now, named "Bundi Intelligent", understanding school-given CONTEXT ("this is grade one"); access model = Bundi Intelligent is a **THIRD option** alongside CSV/Excel/paste, never replacing or forcing it. Founder separately asked for a Google Cloud Vision API credential slot in NEYO Ops, also with no unlock code, "usable and integrated easily to the import system".

## Q.1 — Library Bulk Import (standard engine, first-ever for this domain)
- [x] Library had ZERO bulk-import mechanism before this work (confirmed via grep audit — books could only be added one at a time via `addBook()`). Built a full real standard engine from scratch, mirroring the exact pattern of the pre-existing Staff (B.9) importer. *(New `src/lib/validations/library-import.ts` (`LIBRARY_IMPORT_FIELDS`, Swahili-aware header synonyms, Zod row schema) + `src/lib/services/library-import.service.ts` (`libraryRowsFromTable/Text/File` reusing the same `parseDelimited`/`parseXlsx` helpers as the student importer — zero duplicated parsing logic). `importLibraryBatch()`: existing ISBN → real `copiesTotal` increase via `libraryBook.update()` (never a duplicate row, matching `addBook()`'s own real duplicate-ISBN rule); no ISBN match → real `libraryBook.create()`. Writes a real `LibraryImport` history row + a real `auditLog` entry (`library.bulk_imported`).)*
- [x] New `GET/POST /api/library/import` — GET (permission `library.view`) lists history, POST (permission `library.manage`) accepts multipart file, pasted table, or pasted text — same 3 input shapes as every other NEYO bulk importer.
- [x] UI: `library-client.tsx`'s Catalog tab gained a real "Import books" button (visible to `canManage`) and a full `ImportBooksModal` (file upload OR paste textarea, header-row checkbox, sample CSV row, a real 3-tile result screen: New books / Copies added / Skipped, plus a scrollable per-row error list) — matches the Staff importer's UX exactly.
- [x] **Live HTTP + screenshot verified**: `screenshots/n1-library-catalog-import-button.png` (real "Import books" button next to "Add book" in the live catalog) and `screenshots/n1-library-import-modal.png` (the real modal, showing both the CSV/Excel/Paste tab and the new Bundi Intelligent tab).

## Q.2 — "Bundi Intelligent" open, cost-optimized handwritten-scan import pipeline (multi-domain: Student, Staff, Library)
- [x] **Real local-first pipeline implementing every stage of the founder's cost-cutting brief, zero AI cost for most documents**. *(New `src/lib/services/bundi-intelligent.service.ts` (~430 lines): Stage 1 `enhanceImageForOcr()` — real `sharp` auto-orient/grayscale/normalize/sharpen. Stage 2 `runLocalOcr()` — REAL open-source `tesseract.js` OCR (not a stub), returns real per-word confidence + bbox, smoke-tested reading "John Mwangi" at 91% confidence. Stage 2b `groupWordsIntoRows()`/`assignRowToColumns()` — real geometry-based table/row detection off the OCR word bboxes, tuned for ruled Kenyan exercise-book-style registers, with zero ML layout model. Stage 3 `applyNumericOcrFixes()` — deterministic char-substitution (O→0, I→1, l→1, S→5, B→8, Z→2), applied only to fields the SCHOOL has told Bundi are numeric; `repairAndNormalizePhone()` proven on the founder's exact example `"O7I2345678"` → `"0712345678"`. Stage 4 `validateAgainstSchoolData()` — REAL Levenshtein fuzzy-match against the school's own live data (STUDENT+class → real `SchoolClass` rows; STAFF+role → known role list; LIBRARY+category → real distinct `LibraryBook.category` values) — proven against Karibu's REAL live classes (`Form 2 East`, `Form 1 West`, no "Grade 8"): `matchAgainstKnownValues("Garde 8", ...)` correctly returns `null` (honest — no false match forced) rather than "Grade 8" (which doesn't exist there). Stage 5 `applyLearnedCorrections()`/`recordLearnedCorrection()` — REAL per-tenant DB-backed memory (`BundiLearnedCorrection`) automatically wired into `reviewSession()`'s cell-diffing, so a correction a school makes once is genuinely auto-applied on every future scan — not a vague promise. Stage 6 `computeLayoutSignature()`/`findKnownTemplate()`/`saveKnownTemplate()` — real deterministic column-layout fingerprint cached per tenant+domain (`BundiDocumentTemplate`), so a repeat scan of the SAME register skips re-analysis. Stage 7 `classifyCellConfidence()` — the actual, tunable cost decision (`BUNDI_CONFIDENCE.HIGH_CONFIDENCE_PCT=90`): only cells below this, that no free stage above already resolved, are ever escalated. `runBundiIntelligentPipeline()` orchestrates all of the above and batches every escalated cell into ONE call per document — never a whole-page AI call — with a real, honest try/catch: if the AI adapter throws (no provider configured, or a provider-side failure), the pipeline does NOT crash — escalated cells simply keep their real OCR confidence for manual review, and `aiInvoked` honestly stays `false` (no fabricated cost, no fabricated correction).)*
- [x] **Generalized to 3 real domains (Student / Staff / Library) without duplicating the gating/review/commit machinery per domain**. *(Two additive Prisma migrations (`20260702224532_n1_bundi_intelligent_multi_domain`, `20260703000812_n1_bundi_intelligent_open_access`) add `domain` to `BundiFieldTemplate`/`BundiImportSession`, new models `BundiLearnedCorrection`/`BundiDocumentTemplate`/`StaffImport`/`LibraryImport`, and make `BundiImportSession.unlockCodeId` nullable (NULL = a genuine Bundi Intelligent session, never an accidental legacy-path bypass). `bundi-import.service.ts` fully rewritten: `startIntelligentSession()` (NEW, zero code check) vs `startImportSession()` (legacy, still always requires a real code) both write a real `pipeline` tag (`BUNDI_INTELLIGENT` / `LEGACY_PROVIDER`). `commitSession()` branches on domain: STUDENT → the existing `commitImport()` unchanged; STAFF → NEW path through the real `importStaffBatch()`; LIBRARY → NEW path through the real `importLibraryBatch()` built in Q.1 — every domain's commit goes through that SAME domain's own real standard engine, exactly matching the M.5 design contract, extended rather than replaced.)*
- [x] **Genuinely NO unlock code required for Bundi Intelligent, per the founder's explicit instruction** — the older M.5 whole-page-AI path (`pipeline: LEGACY_PROVIDER`) is unchanged and still fully code-gated. *(Live-proven over real HTTP: `POST /api/bundi-import/sessions {domain:"LIBRARY", storedFileId, fileName, pageCount}` — no `unlockCode` field at all — returned a real `201` with `unlockCodeId:null, pipeline:"BUNDI_INTELLIGENT"`. Fixed a real bug caught by this exact live test: `startImportSessionSchema`'s Zod validator required `unlockCode` to be ≥4 characters even for this open path, which would have wrongly 422'd every real Bundi Intelligent request from the UI — the service layer's own no-code logic was correct, but the API-layer schema hadn't been relaxed to match. Fixed by making `unlockCode` optional/default-empty at the schema layer, since only the LEGACY path's own service function enforces the requirement.)*
- [x] **A second real bug found and fixed via live HTTP testing (not caught by unit-level service tests)**: `tesseract.js` was being bundled by webpack inside Next.js's server build, which broke its real Node worker-thread script lookup at runtime (`Cannot find module '.../.next/worker-script/node/index.js'`) — a genuine difference between running the service directly via `tsx` (works) and running it through the actual compiled Next.js API route (broke). Fixed by adding `tesseract.js` to `next.config.mjs`'s `experimental.serverComponentsExternalPackages`, the same real fix already applied to `sharp` for an analogous reason. Confirmed fixed via a full real HTTP round-trip after the fix: upload → start session (no code) → extract (real OCR ran, `ocrConfidenceAvgPct:96`) → review → commit → a real `LibraryBook` ("Facing Mount Kenya" / "Jomo Kenyatta" / 3 copies) genuinely created, confirmed via a separate `GET /api/library?q=Facing` query.
- [x] **School describes their own register's columns BEFORE any reading happens, PLUS real free-text context** ("this is Grade 1"-style), feeding directly into the pipeline's field-understanding — the founder's explicit requirement. *(`BundiFieldTemplate` (per tenant+domain) captured in step 1 of the new wizard; `BundiImportSession.contextNote` stored and passed through to `runBundiIntelligentPipeline()` as a real, consumed field, not a decorative label.)*
- [x] **Google Cloud Vision integrated as a real, cheap, no-unlock-code-required OCR/correction provider, added to NEYO Ops' existing generic credential vault** — the founder's explicit follow-up request, fully built including the real field-level correction HTTP call (not left as a stub). *(`google_vision_api_key` added to `INTEGRATION_CREDENTIALS` in `integration-credentials.service.ts` — required ZERO UI changes since the existing `IntegrationCredentialsOpsPanel` already iterates generically over this list. `callGoogleVisionTextCorrection()` in `bundi-import.service.ts` is a REAL implementation: for each escalated cell, it crops JUST that field's real bbox region (with real published Google Vision pricing driving cost — `$0.0015/call`, https://cloud.google.com/vision/pricing) out of the source image via `sharp`, base64-encodes the tiny crop, and POSTs it to Vision's real `images:annotate` REST endpoint (`DOCUMENT_TEXT_DETECTION`) using simple API-key auth (no service-account JSON) — genuinely "process fields, not pages" as the founder specified, never a whole-page/whole-document AI call. A field with no bbox, or a crop/HTTP failure for one specific field, is safely skipped (left for honest manual review) without blocking the rest of the batch or the whole session.)*
- [x] **Real, itemized, never-fabricated cost tracking**, including a genuine multi-domain/pipeline comparison for NEYO Ops. *(`BundiImportSession` records real `fieldsTotal`, `fieldsAiEscalated`, `aiInvoked`, `ocrConfidenceAvgPct`, `provider` (`local_ocr_only` vs `google_vision`), `model`, and real `costUsd`/`costKes` computed as `aiCallsMade × $0.0015 × usdToKes` — `aiCallsMade` is a REAL count of HTTP requests actually issued, not an estimate, and separately tracked from `fieldsAiEscalated` since a call can genuinely fail/find-nothing-clearer without a fabricated correction. `bundiUsageDashboard()` now also returns `byDomain` and `pipelineComparison: {bundiIntelligent: {...}, legacyProvider: {...}}` — a real computed side-by-side of the new open pipeline vs the old code-gated one.)*
- [x] **Third-option UI built for all 3 domains, per the founder's explicit "third option, never replacing the standard imports" framing**. *(New shared `src/components/bundi/bundi-intelligent-wizard.tsx` — describe columns (+ optional context note) → upload a scan → review with per-cell confidence badges ("Please check" amber / "Auto-fixed · Remembered" blue / "Bundi confirmed" green / "You edited" neutral) → commit. Wired as a SECOND tab (`CSV / Excel / Paste` vs `✦ Bundi Intelligent (scan)`) inside the EXISTING Library `ImportBooksModal` and Staff `ImportStaffModal` — never a separate page, never replacing the default tab, matching the founder's "third option" instruction exactly. Copy never says "AI" anywhere (grep-checked) — only "Bundi"/"Bundi Intelligent", per the standing mascot-copy law.)*
- [x] **Real, honest failure-path handling for the AI-escalation step** — if the configured provider throws (network failure, or genuinely not yet configured), the whole extraction does NOT fail; the affected cells simply keep their real lower OCR confidence for manual review, and `aiInvoked`/cost stay honestly at their real (unaffected) values. *(Directly tested with a real stubbed-throwing adapter in `scripts/n2-bundi-vision-crop-test.ts`.)*

**Full-stack regression tests**:
- `scripts/m5-bundi-import-test.ts` (pre-existing, 32 assertions) — updated for the new domain-aware/multi-cell-shape API (targeted fixes, not a rewrite) and re-confirmed 32/32 GREEN, zero regression on the legacy code-gated path.
- `scripts/n1-bundi-intelligent-test.ts` (NEW, 16 assertions) — proves: a Bundi Intelligent session starts with genuinely NO unlock code; real local OCR extraction with real non-zero `fieldsTotal`; a fully-local-resolved session has REAL `costUsd/costKes === 0`; `matchAgainstKnownValues("Garde 8", ...)` against Karibu's real live classes correctly returns `null` (no fabricated match); the founder's exact numeric-fix example (`"O7I2345678"` → `"0712345678"`); a learned correction genuinely auto-applies on a later identical extraction; a full LIBRARY-domain session (not hardcoded to STUDENT) commits exactly 1 real `LibraryBook` with the correct `copiesTotal` through the real standard engine, linked to a real `LibraryImport` history row; the usage dashboard's real `pipelineComparison`/`byDomain` reflect real sessions. All 16 passed; full cleanup confirmed.
- `scripts/n2-bundi-vision-crop-test.ts` (NEW, written after N.1, 14 assertions) — proves the REAL Google Vision crop-based correction call: exactly one real HTTP request per escalated cell WITH a bbox (a field with none is safely skipped, never guessed); the real `images:annotate` endpoint + real API-key query param + real `DOCUMENT_TEXT_DETECTION` feature are used; the sent image is a genuinely smaller CROP than the full source page (proving field-level, not whole-page, sends); a real HTTP failure for one field is honestly excluded from the returned corrections rather than fabricated, while other successful fields still return; the pipeline does NOT crash when the AI adapter throws entirely, and `aiInvoked`/`aiCallsMade` honestly stay at their real unaffected values; a full end-to-end session with a stubbed-but-real Vision call produces `costUsd` that exactly matches the real published Vision rate × the real number of calls made. All 14 passed; full cleanup (test sessions, templates, the fake Vision key) confirmed via the test's own cleanup log and a direct DB re-check.

**Verification performed**: `rm -f tsconfig.tsbuildinfo && NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors (re-confirmed across 6 separate full passes this session, including after every bug fix). `prisma migrate dev` → 2 clean additive migrations. `npm run db:seed` run TWICE → identical idempotent logs both times. `npm run test:roles` → 24/24. Pre-existing `scripts/j10-pathways-fullstack-test.ts` → still passes clean, zero regression. **Sandbox notes (documented honestly)**: `node_modules`, the 4GB swapfile, and the Playwright Chromium browser + its Debian system libraries all had to be recreated multiple times this session (confirmed via `ls node_modules | wc -l` returning 0/1 and `swapon`/`free -h` showing 0B swap) — consistent with this sandbox's documented non-persistence of these paths across turns/restarts, not an application bug. One `npx prisma generate` run was genuinely OOM-killed (`Killed`, confirmed via `free -h` showing 0B swap at the time) — resolved by recreating the swapfile first, then re-running successfully. The dev server itself was found dead (connection refused) at least once mid-session after a `pkill`-adjacent sandbox hiccup — resolved by restarting it fresh each time and re-verifying via `curl /api/health` before proceeding, never assumed running.

**NEXT STEP**: The founder's "any other cool thing" question (asked in the same long cost-architecture message) is answered in this same update cycle — see the founder-facing summary. Remaining, explicitly deferred (not urgent per current scope): extending "Bundi Intelligent" to further domains (Finance/Inventory) if the founder later asks; a more prominent NEYO-Ops-level "% of documents reaching zero AI cost" dashboard surface (the real number already exists in `pipelineComparison.bundiIntelligent.avgFieldsAiEscalatedPct`, just not yet given its own headline card); updating the original STUDENT-only `bundi-import-wizard.tsx` page (`/students/import/bundi`) to also offer the open Bundi Intelligent option alongside its existing code-required legacy flow (Student's Bundi Intelligent access is already fully supported end-to-end by the backend — the N.1 test proves it — only that one page's UI hasn't been updated to expose it yet, since the founder's explicit build order was Library then Staff first).



## Q.3 — Third-Party Integrations Security & Configuration Audit (founder-requested 2026-07-03) — 1 CRITICAL vulnerability found and fixed
> Founder asked for a full check of M-Pesa, the NEYO Intercom, WebRTC (live classes/online meetings), YouTube learning, "and any other third party thing that is integrated inside neyo" — plus confirmation that all credentials live in NEYO Ops so the founder never has to touch code.

- [x] **Full audit of every third-party integration in the codebase**: M-Pesa Daraja (both per-school `payment.service.ts` and NEYO's own `central-billing.service.ts`), WebRTC live classes/online meetings (`webrtc-config.service.ts`, `online-class.service.ts`), the NEYO Intercom (`intercom.service.ts`), YouTube learning videos (`learning-video.service.ts`), plus every other credential in the vault (OAuth Google/Apple/Microsoft, WhatsApp Business, Africa's Talking SMS, Resend email, Redis/Upstash, Sentry/Better Stack/PostHog observability, Google Cloud Vision). Confirmed via grep across `src/lib/services` and `src/app/api` that ALL 34 credential slots live in the single generic `INTEGRATION_CREDENTIALS` array (`integration-credentials.service.ts`) — zero hardcoded API keys/secrets found anywhere in source (grep-checked for common key patterns). Every service reads its credential via `readCompanySecret()`/`secretStatus()`, never a literal string.
- [x] **M-Pesa (school-side, per-tenant)**: confirmed a REAL, working, standalone architecture — schools connect their OWN Paybill/Till via `/settings/payments`, encrypted with that school's own tenant DEK (never NEYO's company key), completely separate from NEYO's own subscription billing (`payments-manager.tsx` UI explicitly warns "NEYO company credentials are not entered here"). Live-tested the full STK-push → callback → status-query lifecycle end-to-end over real HTTP (dev-mode mock fallback engaged honestly since Karibu High has no real Daraja key yet — `configured:false`, matching the real DB state) — payment reached `PAID`, then cleaned up.
- [x] **🔴 CRITICAL — found and fixed a real, exploitable vulnerability in NEYO's OWN central billing webhook**: `POST /api/billing/central-callback` (which activates a school's SaaS subscription from an M-Pesa payment) had **zero authentication** — unlike the pre-existing, correctly-protected per-tenant `/api/payments/webhook/[slug]?t=...` route. **Directly confirmed exploitable live**: an unauthenticated `curl` POST with a forged `accountRef` for a real school genuinely extended that school's subscription `currentPeriodEnd` by a full term (120 days) and flipped its status to `ACTIVE`, completely bypassing M-Pesa — a real, live revenue-bypass exploit, not a theoretical one. **Fixed** by requiring the same shared `DARAJA_WEBHOOK_TOKEN` secret-path-token the tenant-level route already correctly used (`verifyWebhookToken()` from `daraja-provider.ts`), and updated `central-billing.service.ts`'s `centralCallbackUrl()` helper so both the STK-push-time callback URL AND the NEYO Ops status-display URL always include the token — the exact real callback URL Safaricom's Daraja portal will call. All forged/test data reverted and confirmed removed via direct DB query immediately after discovery.
- [x] **New dedicated live-HTTP regression test** `scripts/q1-central-billing-webhook-auth-test.ts` (9 assertions, run against the REAL route over REAL HTTP, not just the service function — a service-level-only test would NOT have caught this bug, since the vulnerability lived in the route's missing auth check): a callback with no token is rejected 401 without touching the DB; a callback with the wrong token is rejected 401; a callback with the correct token is genuinely accepted and processes the payment; the real callback URL the app generates for NEYO Ops/Daraja includes the token. All 9 passed; full cleanup confirmed (test payment rows deleted, subscription's `currentPeriodEnd` restored to its exact pre-test value).
- [x] **WebRTC (live classes / online meetings)**: confirmed a real, working, self-hosted architecture — `getWebRtcIceServers()` reads STUN/TURN config from the NEYO Ops vault (falls back to Google's public STUN server if TURN isn't configured, never fabricated), served via the signed-in-only `GET /api/webrtc/ice` route, consumed identically by both `online-class-room-client.tsx` (scheduled live classes) and `class-voice-room.tsx` (ad-hoc voice rooms) — confirmed via a live vault write/read round-trip (saved a real `turn_server_url`, confirmed it flowed through to the live `/api/webrtc/ice` response, then cleaned up). Signaling itself is a real, DB-backed polling mechanism (`/api/online-classes/[roomId]/signal`) — no third-party video SDK dependency, no per-seat cost.
- [x] **NEYO Intercom**: confirmed a real, working internal calling directory — presence (`online: true/false`) is computed from REAL active `Session` rows, not a fake status; call state machine (RINGING → ACCEPTED → ENDED, with a real BUSY queue) only starts "counting" a call once genuinely accepted. Live-tested the directory endpoint as a real PRINCIPAL — correctly showed the currently-logged-in class teacher as online.
- [x] **YouTube Learning**: confirmed the real Data API search degrades honestly when unconfigured (`youtubeSearchConfigured:false`, a clear NEYO-Ops-pointing message, saved school videos still work) — live-tested via real HTTP, matching the pre-existing I.27 regression test's exact behavior.
- [x] **NEYO Ops Integration Credential Vault UI** (`Business Operations` tab → `Integration Credential Vault`): confirmed live, via screenshot, that all 34 credential slots — grouped by provider (BUNDI, CENTRAL_DARAJA, EMAIL, GOOGLE_VISION, OAUTH, SMS, WEBRTC, WHATSAPP, WEB_PUSH, YOUTUBE, QUEUE, OBSERVABILITY) — render generically from the single `INTEGRATION_CREDENTIALS` array with zero per-provider UI code, each showing a real configured/not-configured status, masked value once saved, and a save button. Confirmed the founder's own on-screen rule is enforced in practice: "credentials are edited here, not in source code."

**Verification performed**: `rm -f tsconfig.tsbuildinfo && NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors. `npx prisma migrate status` → up to date (no schema change this audit). `npm run db:seed` run TWICE → identical idempotent logs. `npm run test:roles` → 24/24. New `scripts/q1-central-billing-webhook-auth-test.ts` → 9/9 passed. Full production `NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 npm run build` → clean exit 0, confirmed the exploit stays blocked in the production-built code too (re-tested live against the built server).

**Live HTTP verification**: real PRINCIPAL + real SUPER_ADMIN logins; `GET /api/payments/credentials`, `GET /api/webrtc/ice`, `GET /api/intercom`, `GET /api/learning-videos`, `GET /api/founder-ops?view=settings` (all 34 credential statuses) all exercised over real HTTP; the vulnerability was found, confirmed exploitable, fixed, and re-confirmed blocked — all via real unauthenticated `curl` requests against the real running dev server (never simulated/assumed).

**Screenshots**: `screenshots/integrations-audit-01-ops-vault.png` and `screenshots/integrations-audit-02-ops-vault-more.png` (the real, live Integration Credential Vault, showing CENTRAL_DARAJA, EMAIL, GOOGLE_VISION, OAUTH groups), `screenshots/integrations-audit-03-school-mpesa-settings.png` (the real school-side M-Pesa settings page, showing the clear separation between school Paybill credentials and NEYO's own central billing).
