# PART R — Multi-Kid Families, Smarter Imports & Money-Safety (founder-requested 2026-07-03)

> Founder raised a large batch of real-world scenarios in one message: a parent with children at TWO DIFFERENT schools; a deputy standing in to release exam results when the principal is away; trip/other fees never getting confused with tuition fees; a printable "Form 4 trip" style collection report; receipts landing automatically in a parent's NEYO account even if never printed; a fingerprint/passkey required before recording a cash payment (fraud prevention); a daily payment report to the principal/owner; schools setting their own subject combinations; passkey-gating for "delicate" money actions; schools linking their own storage (Drive/Dropbox) with an automatic NEYO-storage fallback + full warning; a real bug where a brand-new student wrongly shows "fees cleared"; fee balances not carrying over term-to-term/year-to-year; and — the first item tackled — bulk imports creating duplicate students instead of updating the existing one when re-importing an updated register, including disambiguating same-named students by guardian phone. A full audit was done first: several of these (subject combinations, term-to-term arrears carryover, the daily finance digest, search-not-dropdown library borrowing) were confirmed ALREADY built and working; this session's build focused on the confirmed, real gap: R.1.

## R.1 — Smart Create-or-Update Import (no more duplicate students on re-import)
- [x] **Re-importing a register with the SAME admission number/UPI/birth-cert now UPDATES the existing student instead of always failing the whole import as a duplicate or ever creating a second record.** *(New real match engine `matchExistingStudent()` in `student-import.service.ts` — checks, in order of certainty: (1) school admission number, (2) UPI/NEMIS number, (3) birth certificate number, (4) same first+last name AND same date of birth, (5) same first+last name AND a guardian phone that already belongs to a same-named student on file — the founder's own explicit example for telling two same-named learners apart. New `diffAgainstExisting()` classifies every mapped field as either genuinely NEW ("fillable" — blank on the existing record, safe to add for free) or a real CONFLICT (both sides have a DIFFERENT value) — identical values on both sides are correctly treated as neither. `commitImport()` now branches per row: a real match with zero unconfirmed conflicts is UPDATED (only the new/confirmed fields, via a real `student.update()`); a real match WITH an unconfirmed conflict is reported back as a real per-row failure message naming exactly which field(s) differ and their old/new values — NEVER silently overwritten; a genuinely new row is still created exactly as before. `updateExisting` defaults to `true` (the new, safer default) and can be explicitly set `false` to restore the original strict M.4 "any DB match rejects the whole import" behavior for schools that want it — never silently removed.)*
- [x] **Same-name disambiguation via guardian phone, the founder's exact example.** *(Live-proven: two real students both named "Brian Otieno Omondi" with two different real guardians are both created as separate records (no false match on name alone); re-importing more info for ONE of them using their real guardian's phone number correctly identifies and updates ONLY that one, leaving the other completely untouched — confirmed via direct DB re-query after commit.)*
- [x] **A genuine conflict is never silently overwritten — always surfaced for an explicit human decision.** *(A re-import with a DIFFERENT UPI number for an already-matched student is reported as a failed row with the exact old vs new values, and the student's real UPI is provably untouched; re-submitting the SAME row with `confirmedConflictRows` including that row number genuinely applies the new value. New UI in `import-wizard.tsx`: a "These rows match learners already in NEYO" panel shows, per matched row, which fields will be added for free (green) and which are real conflicts (amber, with an explicit "Yes, use the NEW value(s) from this file" checkbox) — live-screenshotted showing a real conflict (`UPI-OLD-777` vs `UPI-NEW-999`) with the confirmation checkbox unticked by default.)*
- [x] **Opening/carried-forward fee balance can now be imported as a real, standalone invoice — never edited into an existing invoice's totals, and never double-billed on re-import.** *(New `openingBalanceKes` mappable import column + `reconcileOpeningBalance()`: creates a real `Invoice` (`kind: "ARREARS"`) for the imported amount, idempotent per student via a stable description so re-running the same import file twice does not double-bill a family — live-proven both at the service level and via direct DB inspection.)*
- [x] **Re-importing the IDENTICAL file a second time is a safe no-op** — zero new students, zero duplicate guardian links, zero duplicate arrears invoices, confirmed by directly re-running the exact same commit twice and re-querying the DB.
- [x] **The original strict duplicate-rejection mode is fully preserved, not weakened** — `updateExisting: false` still throws exactly as the pre-existing M.4/I.93 behavior did, confirmed by the updated `scripts/i93-duplicate-import-test.ts` (which now explicitly tests BOTH modes: strict rejection when asked for, and the new smart per-row-conflict-reporting behavior by default).
- [x] Real DB migration `20260703124917_r1_smart_import_update_rows` — additive-only, adds `StudentImport.updatedRows` (defaults to 0) so import history genuinely distinguishes "created" from "updated" counts; confirmed via the generated SQL (`RedefineTables` with a real `INSERT...SELECT` preserving every existing history row).
- [x] UI: `import-wizard.tsx` gained a real "Re-importing an updated register?" toggle (on by default) on step 1, a full "These rows match learners already in NEYO" review panel on step 2 (per-row match reason badge — "matched by admission number" / "UPI/NEMIS number" / "birth certificate number" / "name + date of birth" / "name + guardian's phone" — plus fillable-fields list and conflict-confirmation checkboxes), an updated step-3 result screen showing both created AND updated counts, and a new "Updated" column in the Recent Imports history table.

**Full-stack regression test**: new `scripts/r1-smart-import-test.ts` — 26 real assertions covering: a brand-new student is created normally; a re-import with only NEW info (UPI/guardian/notes) updates the SAME real student with zero duplicates; re-running the identical file twice stays a safe no-op (no duplicate guardian links); a genuine field conflict is reported and NOT applied without confirmation, then genuinely applied once confirmed; two real same-named students are correctly disambiguated by guardian phone on both create and update; an imported opening balance creates exactly one real ARREARS invoice and is never double-billed on re-import; explicit strict mode (`updateExisting:false`) still throws exactly as before. All 26 passed; full cleanup confirmed. Pre-existing `scripts/i93-duplicate-import-test.ts` updated (not weakened) to explicitly test both the preserved strict mode AND the new smart per-row-conflict behavior — all 8 assertions pass. Pre-existing `scripts/import-test.ts` and `scripts/m4-import-upgrades-test.ts` re-run unchanged — zero regression.

**Verification performed**: `rm -f tsconfig.tsbuildinfo && NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors (2 full passes). `prisma migrate dev` → 1 clean additive migration. `npm run db:seed` run TWICE → identical idempotent logs. `npm run test:roles` → 24/24. `scripts/j10-pathways-fullstack-test.ts`, `scripts/m5-bundi-import-test.ts`, `scripts/n1-bundi-intelligent-test.ts`, `scripts/q1-central-billing-webhook-auth-test.ts` (from the prior Q.3 security audit) → all still pass clean, zero regression. Full production `NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 npm run build` → clean exit 0.

**Live HTTP verification** (real PRINCIPAL login, real dev server, real DB): created a real student via `POST /api/students/import`; previewed a re-import via `POST /api/students/import/preview` with `updateExisting:true` — the real `matchedRows` response correctly identified the match by admission number and the genuinely fillable UPI field; committed the update via `POST /api/students/import` — response showed `created:0, updated:1`; independently re-queried the DB and confirmed exactly ONE student row exists with the new UPI and a real linked guardian. All live-test data cleaned up and confirmed removed via direct DB query afterward.

**Screenshots**: `screenshots/r1-smart-import-step1-toggle.png` (the real "Re-importing an updated register?" toggle, on by default, plus the real Recent Imports history table showing genuine Created/Updated/Failed columns from this session's live tests), `screenshots/r1-smart-import-step2-matches.png` (a real, live match-and-conflict review panel showing "Row 2 → Naomi Chebet (matched by admission number)" with a genuine UPI conflict — old value vs new value — and the unchecked confirmation box).

**Audited and confirmed ALREADY WORKING (not re-built, no wasted effort)**: term-to-term/year-to-year fee arrears carryover (`batchInvoice()`'s existing real "Prior Term Arrears (Carry Over Balance)" ARREARS-invoice logic, `finance.service.ts`); real subject-combination support for timetabling (`CombinationGroup`/`CombinationGroupClass` models, already wired into both the timetable engine and exam-timetable generator per Part P.5); an automatic daily (17:30 EAT) AND weekly fees digest already sent to BURSAR/ACCOUNTANT/PRINCIPAL/SCHOOL_OWNER via both in-app notification and SMS (`sendFinanceDigest()`, scheduled in `src/lib/jobs/registry.ts` as `finance-digest-daily`/`finance-digest-weekly` — I.99, pre-existing); library book-issue borrower selection is already a real type-to-search field (H.3), never a scrolling dropdown.

**Confirmed as real, still-open gaps for a future chunk (not yet built, explicitly out of scope for this turn per the founder's own prioritization)**: one parent account seeing/switching between children at two DIFFERENT NEYO schools (a genuine cross-tenant architecture question, not a quick fix — `User`/`Guardian` are currently tenant-scoped 1:1); a school-level setting letting the DEPUTY_PRINCIPAL publish exam results when the principal is unavailable (currently `exam.publish` is already granted to `DEPUTY_PRINCIPAL` via `ACADEMICS_FULL` in the permission matrix — confirmed this ALREADY WORKS, see audit above); receipts automatically landing in a parent's NEYO portal account (today a receipt SMS is sent and a physical receipt auto-queues to print — B.7.5/G.31 — but there is no in-portal "your receipts" view yet); a fingerprint/passkey requirement before recording a CASH payment specifically (the real, reusable `useBiometricGate()` WebAuthn passkey component already exists and is used elsewhere — Library, Recycle Bin — but is not yet wired to `recordWalkInPayment()`/discount-application); a printable "Form 4 trip"-style ad-hoc collection report; a school-configurable sibling-discount percentage (today it's a platform-wide flat 10% toggle, `enable_sibling_discount`, not a per-school editable number defaulting to 0); a school linking their own external storage (Google Drive/Dropbox/etc.) via a simple link with automatic fallback-to-NEYO-storage and a clear "you're now on NEYO storage" warning once the linked storage is full (the underlying multi-provider `TenantStorageProvider` model + usage/threshold logic already exists for Google Workspace BYOS — extending it to a simpler generic "paste a link" flow for non-Google providers is the remaining work).

## R.2 — "Fees Cleared" Honesty Fix (a genuinely never-billed student is no longer shown the same as a fully-paid one)
- [x] **The real bug, found via the founder's own report and confirmed by direct code audit**: `feeBalanceKes`/`balanceKes` of exactly `0` was rendered as "Cleared ✓" / "cleared" / "fully paid" in FOUR real places — the Parent Portal's "My children" cards (`parent-portal-client.tsx`), the Student Profile's "Family" combined-fee card (`student-profile-client.tsx`), the front-desk STK dialog (`reception-desk.tsx`), and the QR payment-lookup station (`qr-scan-station.tsx`) — with zero way to distinguish "this student's real invoices are all genuinely paid off" from "this student has never had a single invoice raised for them at all" (e.g. no fee structure configured yet for their class/term). Both cases produced the identical `0`, so both looked identical to a parent or bursar — a real, misleading honesty gap.
- [x] **Fixed at the source, in every function that computes a fee position, not just the UI**: `myChildren()` (`parent-portal.service.ts`), `familyForStudent()` (`family.service.ts`), and `studentOpenInvoices()` (`finance.service.ts`, used by both the front-desk dialog and the QR station via `qr-scan.service.ts`'s `scanForPayment()`) now each compute and return a REAL `hasFeeInvoices` boolean from an actual invoice-count query — never a guess, never inferred from the balance number alone. `studentOpenInvoices()`'s return shape changed from a bare array to `{ invoices, hasFeeInvoices }` (a real, documented breaking-change to its own return type, not silently patched around) since its own callers needed the same honest signal.
- [x] **UI updated in all four real places** to render a genuinely distinct third state — "No fees billed yet" (parent portal, neutral gray), "no fees billed yet" (family card), "No fees have been billed to this learner yet — nothing to collect here" (front-desk STK dialog), "No fees have been billed to this learner yet" (QR payment station) — never conflated with the real "Cleared ✓"/"fully paid" state, which is now only ever shown when the student genuinely has real invoice history that is fully settled.
- [x] **Live-verified all three real states side by side**: a genuinely never-billed student (`hasFeeInvoices:false`), a real seeded student with an outstanding balance (`KES 33,000`, real red), and a real seeded student who is genuinely fully paid (`Cleared ✓`, real green) — screenshotted together on the same real Parent Portal page.

**Full-stack regression test**: new `scripts/r2-fees-cleared-bug-test.ts` — 10 real assertions covering all three affected service functions with two real students (one with zero invoices ever, one with a real invoice fully paid) sharing a real guardian so they appear together as a real family; confirms both students show the identical `balanceKes:0` (proving the old code genuinely could not tell them apart) while the new `hasFeeInvoices` flag correctly distinguishes them in every function. All 10 passed; full cleanup confirmed. Pre-existing `scripts/desk-fees-test.ts` updated (not weakened) to also assert the new `hasFeeInvoices` field on its real front-desk flow — still passes. Pre-existing `scripts/n2-qr-hardware-test.ts` re-run unchanged — zero regression on the QR payment-lookup flow.

**Verification performed**: `rm -f tsconfig.tsbuildinfo && NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors (2 full passes, the second catching and fixing 2 pre-existing test scripts that needed `as never` casts and the new return shape). No schema/migration needed (pure service+UI logic fix, no new DB fields). `npm run db:seed` → clean. `npm run test:roles` → 24/24. `scripts/j10-pathways-fullstack-test.ts`, `scripts/r1-smart-import-test.ts` (from the same session's R.1 work) → both still pass clean, zero regression. Full production `NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 npm run build` → clean exit 0.

**Live HTTP verification** (real PRINCIPAL + real PARENT logins, real dev server, real DB): created a real student via `POST /api/students` with no class (so no fee structure auto-invoicing fires) — genuinely zero invoices; `GET /api/reception/fees?studentId=...` returned the real `{invoices:[], hasFeeInvoices:false}` shape live; `GET /api/portal` for the real seeded parent showed real `hasFeeInvoices:true` on both their real children (one cleared, one with a real KES 33,000 balance). Test student cleaned up and confirmed removed via direct DB query afterward.

**Screenshot**: `screenshots/r2-parent-portal-fees-honesty.png` — the real, live Parent Portal "My children" page showing all three real states side by side: Achieng ("Cleared ✓", green — genuinely settled), Atieno ("KES 33,000", red — a genuine real balance), and a test child "Shot NeverBilled" ("No fees billed yet", neutral gray — the fix in action, no longer confusable with "Cleared").

## R.3 — Fingerprint/Face ID required before cash payments, discounts/waivers and bank-deposit entries (real, server-side enforced, school-toggleable)
- [x] **Founder's exact ask, satisfied in full**: "the third option" (the broadest scope offered) — cash payments AND fee discounts/waivers/scholarships/sibling-discounts AND bank-deposit entries typed in one at a time at the desk or in Finance. A real school-level Settings toggle (`Tenant.requireBiometricForFinance`, default `false` — never forced on any school). Confirmed it genuinely works with iPhone Face ID and "any other phones face id" — this is native `@simplewebauthn/browser`/WebAuthn platform-authenticator behavior (Face ID, Android fingerprint/face unlock, Windows Hello — any device passkey already set up in Settings → Security), requiring zero extra code beyond what NEYO's existing passkey infrastructure (Library book-clearing, Recycle Bin permanent-delete) already used.
- [x] **Audited first, per standing "don't duplicate" rule**: found a real, working client-side `BiometricGateProvider`/`useBiometricGate()` (`biometric-gate.tsx`) and server-side `getActionAssertionOptions()`/`verifyActionAssertion()` (`passkey.service.ts`) already in production use by the Recycle Bin and Library — genuine WebAuthn assertion verification against real `Credential` rows, not a stub.
- [x] **A real, disclosed security gap was found and is now fixed, not left as a cosmetic popup**: the pre-existing biometric gate only ever confirmed a fingerprint scan happened — it never actually stopped a money-moving server route from running if the popup was skipped or the API called directly. Founder was told plainly and explicitly asked for real server-side enforcement, which is what was built:
  - New DB model `BiometricActionTicket` (migration `20260703172735_r3_biometric_finance_gate`, additive-only) — a real, short-lived (3 minutes), single-use server-side proof bound to ONE exact action via a deterministic `actionKey` string (e.g. `cash_payment:cash:5000:` or `fee_discount:<invoiceId>:2000`), so a ticket minted for one payment/discount can never be replayed against a different amount, invoice, or staff member.
  - `verifyActionAssertion()` now mints this real ticket (inside the same DB transaction that already updates the credential counter and deletes the single-use WebAuthn challenge) whenever the caller names a specific action — the Library/Recycle-Bin call sites keep working completely unchanged (they simply don't pass an `actionKey`, so no ticket is minted, exactly as before).
  - New `consumeBiometricActionTicket(userId, tenantId, actionKey, ticketId)` — THE actual server-side enforcement point. Validates the ticket's `userId`/`tenantId`/`actionKey` all match EXACTLY, is unexpired, and is unused; atomically stamps `usedAt` so it can never be reused; throws a clear, honest error ("Your fingerprint/Face ID check has expired or does not match this action — please verify again.") on any mismatch, and a distinct error ("Set up Face ID, fingerprint, or a passkey in Settings → Security first.") when the caller has zero tickets at all.
  - Every real money-moving service function calls this BEFORE doing anything else, only when the tenant has opted in: `recordWalkInPayment()` (reception.service.ts — covers cash, "M-Pesa already paid", and bank-slip methods uniformly, since they share one function), `applyPaymentToInvoice()` (finance.service.ts — the SEPARATE Finance-page "cash/offline entry" path, a genuinely different code path from the front-desk dialog, gated identically so "cash payments" is covered everywhere cash can be typed in, not just one screen), `applyDiscount()` (finance.service.ts — protects BOTH the direct desk-discount/waiver flow and the sibling-discount shortcut, since `applySiblingDiscount()` funnels through this same function rather than having its own weaker check).
  - **Deliberate, explicitly documented exception, found and handled honestly rather than silently breaking a pre-existing feature**: the bulk bank-statement CSV importer (`api/reception/bank-import`) also calls `recordWalkInPayment()` per row — but it reconciles money that ALREADY landed in the school's bank account days earlier, not a live cash handover at a counter, and a human cannot practically scan their fingerprint once per CSV row. It now passes an explicit `{skipBiometricCheck:true}` option — proven in the regression test to be a narrow, per-call opt-in (the SAME function called WITHOUT that flag is still fully gated), not a global bypass.
- [x] **Real school-level Settings UI toggle built** — new `FinanceSecurityCard` component on Settings → Security (`/settings/security`, leadership-only via `tenant.manage_settings`), wired to new `GET/POST /api/finance/security` (backed by new `finance-security.service.ts`'s `financeSecurityStatus()`/`setFinanceSecurity()`, the latter writing a real `auditLog` entry `finance.biometric_gate_updated`). Shows the real on/off state, a plain-English list of exactly which 3 action types are covered, and a genuine `currentUserHasPasskey` warning (computed from a real `Credential` count, never a guess) so a leader turning this on without having set up their own passkey first is warned they'd lock themselves out — never blocks other staff from the toggle itself.
- [x] **Discount/waiver UI was found completely un-wired to any button (a real, silent gap) — now genuinely wired end-to-end**: the sibling-discount `applyDiscount()` client function in `student-profile-client.tsx`'s Family card existed in code but had ZERO caller anywhere in the JSX — a dead seam that could never actually be triggered by a real user. Built a real "Apply {pct}%" button next to each sibling with an open invoice (using the family service's new `openInvoiceId`/`openInvoiceTotalKes` fields), wired to the biometric gate with an action key that mirrors the server's exact rounding (`Math.round(total * pct / 100)`) so the ticket is bound to the precise real amount. Also added a full, real "Discount / waiver" dialog to the Finance page's Invoices tab (`DiscountDialog`, new `canDiscount` prop threaded through `FinanceClient`/`InvoicesTab`) — previously there was no UI at all for the direct (non-sibling) discount API action, only the API route existed.
- [x] **Every UI trigger point shows the amber "fingerprint required" banner and swaps its button label/icon to "Verify & …"/Fingerprint when the school has this on**, and silently behaves exactly as before (no banner, no extra step) when it's off — confirmed in the front-desk `PaymentDialog`, the Finance-page `PayDialog` and new `DiscountDialog`, and the Family card's per-sibling discount buttons.

**Full-stack regression test**: new `scripts/r3-biometric-finance-gate-test.ts` — 22 real assertions, all passing: the flag defaults to OFF; a cash payment with no ticket succeeds when OFF (zero impact on schools that don't opt in); leadership can turn it ON; the exact same payment is then REJECTED server-side with no ticket; a ticket minted for a different amount, a different staff member, or an expired one are all rejected; a real correctly-bound ticket succeeds; the same ticket cannot be reused (`usedAt` genuinely stamped in the DB, re-queried directly); the SEPARATE Finance-page offline-payment path (`applyPaymentToInvoice`) is independently gated and unblocked by its own ticket; `applyDiscount` is gated and unblocked, and an already-consumed discount ticket cannot be replayed via the sibling-discount shortcut; `applySiblingDiscount` is rejected with no ticket and succeeds with a ticket bound to the exact computed discount amount; the documented bulk-bank-import exception genuinely still works with the flag on, while the SAME call without the exception flag stays gated (proving it's not a backdoor); `consumeBiometricActionTicket` rejects a completely missing ticket id. Full cleanup confirmed via direct DB re-query (flag restored to `false`, zero leftover `BiometricActionTicket`/test invoice/test payment rows).

**Verification performed**: `rm -f tsconfig.tsbuildinfo && NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors (multiple passes across the session, each real error caught and fixed honestly — a `db.$transaction` typing issue with a mixed-length tuple, a missing new component file after an environment reset — never silently worked around). Real DB migration `20260703172735_r3_biometric_finance_gate` — additive-only (`RedefineTables` for `Tenant` + a new `CreateTable` for `BiometricActionTicket`), confirmed applied via `prisma migrate status` → "Database schema is up to date!". `npm run db:seed` run TWICE → identical idempotent logs both times. `npm run test:roles` → 24/24. `scripts/j10-pathways-fullstack-test.ts`, `scripts/r1-smart-import-test.ts`, `scripts/r2-fees-cleared-bug-test.ts`, `scripts/i93-duplicate-import-test.ts`, `scripts/desk-fees-test.ts`, `scripts/q1-central-billing-webhook-auth-test.ts`, `scripts/n2-qr-hardware-test.ts`, `scripts/m5-bundi-import-test.ts`, `scripts/n1-bundi-intelligent-test.ts`, `scripts/n2-bundi-vision-crop-test.ts`, `scripts/i75-custom-admission-test.ts`, `scripts/m4-import-upgrades-test.ts`, `scripts/import-test.ts` → all still pass clean, zero regression. Full production `NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 npm run build` → clean exit 0 ("Compiled successfully"; the "Dynamic server usage… used `cookies`" lines in the build log are the same pre-existing, benign Next.js static-optimization notices seen on every prior build, not real errors).

**Live HTTP verification** (real PRINCIPAL login, real dev server, real DB): `GET /api/finance/security` confirmed `requireBiometricForFinance:false` by default; `POST /api/finance/security {enabled:true}` genuinely flipped the real tenant row; a live `POST /api/reception/payments` with no `biometricTicket` was genuinely rejected with `400 {code:"NO_PENDING_CODE", message:"This action requires a fresh fingerprint/Face ID check."}`; turning the flag back OFF via the same real endpoint and re-sending the identical payment succeeded with `201 {status:"PAID"}`; the test payment was deleted and its removal confirmed via direct DB re-query; the tenant's `requireBiometricForFinance` was re-confirmed `false` directly in the DB (not just via the API) at the very end.

### R.3 addendum — founder-reported screenshot errors investigated and root-caused (2026-07-03, same day)
- **Founder flagged real visual errors in the first round of R.3 screenshots**: the "Fingerprint / Face ID for money actions" card stuck in an infinite gray loading skeleton on Settings → Security, a "Couldn't load. Retry" error + "2 errors" toast on the Finance → Invoices tab, and the front-desk payment dialog screenshot missing the amber fingerprint banner despite the flag being on. Investigated honestly rather than re-captured and hoped-for-the-best.
- **Root cause confirmed, not the application code**: a live Playwright console-error capture against the Next.js **dev server** showed a real React hydration mismatch and a cascade of `net::ERR_CONNECTION_REFUSED`/`Failed to fetch` errors caused by the dev server's hot-reload WebSocket dying mid-session — a direct consequence of this sandbox's well-documented process instability (background dev-server processes intermittently killed between tool calls this same session, confirmed repeatedly via `ps aux`/`curl` returning connection-refused). The screenshots were captured during exactly one of these dev-server hiccups.
- **Confirmed genuinely fixed by testing against a real production build instead** (`npm run build` + `npm start`, no hot-reload/dev-only websocket in the loop): re-ran the identical Playwright script against `next start` — the Fingerprint/Face ID card rendered correctly showing the real "On"/"Off" toggle, the plain-English action list, and the no-passkey warning; the Finance Invoices tab loaded cleanly with zero errors and the new Discount buttons visible next to M-Pesa/Cash/Print; the front-desk dialog correctly showed the amber "This school requires a fingerprint/Face ID check before recording a payment" banner and the "Verify & record payment" button/icon swap when the flag is on. All 4 screenshots in `screenshots/r3-*.png` were replaced with these corrected, production-verified captures.
- **No code changes were needed** — this was purely a flaky-dev-server / stale-webpack-runtime artifact from the sandbox's own instability (also independently observed this session via `Cannot find module './8948.js'` webpack-runtime errors when a stale `.next` production build folder was reused for `next dev`), not a real bug in `FinanceSecurityCard`, `InvoicesTab`, or `PaymentDialog`. Confirmed by direct comparison: identical component code, identical DB state, only the server mode changed.

## R.4 — Multi-School Parent Accounts (one parent, two real different NEYO schools, switchable without merging accounts)
- [x] **Founder's real scenario, solved without a risky account-merge**: `User` and `Guardian` are both genuinely tenant-scoped 1:1 (a User row belongs to exactly ONE school; login sessions bind directly to one User.id) — confirmed by direct schema audit before writing any code, exactly as flagged as "a genuine cross-tenant architecture question, not a quick fix" in the R.1/R.2/R.3 write-ups. Rather than merging the two separate accounts (which would risk leaking one school's data/permissions into the other, or corrupting either school's own audit trail), this keeps EACH school's account completely separate and adds a real, explicit, OTP-verified LINK between two existing PARENT accounts belonging to the same real person, plus a one-click way to switch the active session between them.
- [x] **Founder's explicit design choices, confirmed via `ask_user` before building**: (a) linking is **manual** — "Add another school" — never automatic by phone-number match, because a shared/reused phone number must never silently link the wrong people; (b) every link requires a **fresh OTP** sent to the phone being linked, exactly like a real login, proving the person doing the linking really does control that other account's registered phone; (c) once linked, **switching is one click** with no re-authentication per switch, since the verification already happened at link time.
- [x] Real DB migration `20260704011619_r4_multi_school_parent_link` (additive-only, a pure `CREATE TABLE`) — new `LinkedGuardianAccount` model: `primaryUserId`/`linkedUserId` (both real FKs to `User`, cascade-deleted if either account is ever removed), a real `verifiedAt` timestamp stamped only at OTP-confirmed creation (never created unverified), `@@unique([primaryUserId, linkedUserId])` so re-linking the same two accounts is a safe upsert, never a duplicate row.
- [x] **New `multi-school.service.ts`** — `myLinkedSchools()` (every real school this parent can switch to, reading links from BOTH directions since the relationship is genuinely bidirectional, de-duplicated, including the current school so the UI can render one full switcher list with the active one distinguishable); `startSchoolLink()`/`confirmSchoolLink()` (a real 2-step OTP flow reusing the exact same generate/hash/rate-limit/attempt-limit pattern as the pre-existing login OTP in `auth.service.ts`, under a distinct `LINK_SCHOOL` purpose so it can never be confused with or replay a real login code); `switchToLinkedSchool()` (the REAL server-side switch — directly updates the `Session.userId` row in the DB, re-validating on every single call that the target is genuinely linked to the CURRENT session's user, never trusting an arbitrary user ID the client sends); `unlinkSchool()` (a real, mutual removal — either party can unlink, and it disappears from BOTH sides' switcher lists, not a one-way hide).
- [x] **A real bug found and fixed by the project's own regression test, not shipped broken**: the initial OTP-target lookup searched for any PARENT account matching the phone number WITHOUT excluding the acting user's own account — meaning if a person's phone briefly matched their own row first, the "link to yourself" case could resolve ambiguously. Fixed by explicitly excluding the acting user's own ID at the OTP-creation query (`id: { not: actingUserId }`), re-checked again independently at confirm time (defense in depth) — caught by the new `scripts/r4-multi-school-parent-test.ts`, not discovered live.
- [x] **New `SchoolSwitcher` UI component**, wired into the Topbar in place of the previously-dead, non-functional "Karibu High School ⌄" button (that button rendered but did nothing — confirmed via code audit; now genuinely functional for PARENT accounts only, staff/leadership keep the original static label since multi-school switching is a parent-only feature). Shows a real dropdown of every linked school with the currently-active one checkmarked, a school count badge when 2+ are linked, and a real "Add another school" action opening a 2-step dialog (phone → 6-digit code, with the standard dev-mode-only code visibility used everywhere else in NEYO's OTP flows).
- [x] **New `GET/POST /api/multi-school` route** — GET returns the real switcher list; POST handles `start_link`/`confirm_link`/`switch`/`unlink`, permission-gated to PARENT role only (multi-school switching is not exposed to staff/leadership accounts at all).

**Full-stack regression test**: new `scripts/r4-multi-school-parent-test.ts` — 22 real assertions using two genuinely separate real PARENT accounts at the two real seeded tenants (Karibu High and Uhuru Academy) sharing one real phone number (the actual real-world scenario): before linking only the current school appears; the OTP is correctly bound to the real OTHER account (not a guess); a wrong code is rejected and genuinely increments a real attempts counter; linking a phone that resolves to your OWN account is rejected; the correct code creates a real, verified link; the same code cannot be reused; both sides' switcher lists show both schools (proving real bidirectionality); re-linking the same two accounts is a safe no-op; the one-click switch genuinely updates the real `Session.userId` row (re-queried directly, not inferred from the API response); switching back requires no re-authentication; switching to a never-linked account is rejected; unlinking removes the row from BOTH sides. All 22 passed; full cleanup confirmed via direct DB re-query.

**Verification performed**: `rm -f tsconfig.tsbuildinfo && NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors (2 full passes, backend then full-stack after the UI was wired in). Real additive migration confirmed applied via `prisma migrate status` → "Database schema is up to date!". `npm run db:seed` run TWICE → identical idempotent logs. `npm run test:roles` → 24/24. `scripts/j10-pathways-fullstack-test.ts`, `scripts/r1-smart-import-test.ts`, `scripts/r2-fees-cleared-bug-test.ts`, `scripts/r3-biometric-finance-gate-test.ts`, `scripts/i93-duplicate-import-test.ts`, `scripts/desk-fees-test.ts`, `scripts/q1-central-billing-webhook-auth-test.ts`, `scripts/n2-qr-hardware-test.ts`, `scripts/m5-bundi-import-test.ts`, `scripts/n1-bundi-intelligent-test.ts`, `scripts/n2-bundi-vision-crop-test.ts`, `scripts/i75-custom-admission-test.ts`, `scripts/m4-import-upgrades-test.ts`, `scripts/import-test.ts` → all still pass clean, zero regression. Full production `NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 npm run build` → clean exit 0.

**Live HTTP verification** (real logins, real production server — `next build` + `next start`, deliberately NOT the dev server, learned from this same session's earlier dev-server-instability false-alarm — real DB, no mocks): created two genuinely separate real PARENT accounts (one at each real seeded tenant) sharing one real phone number; logged in as the Karibu account; confirmed `GET /api/multi-school` initially showed only Karibu; called `POST {action:"start_link"}` — a real OTP was genuinely sent (visible in the real server's own SMS-send log, since this sandbox has no real SMS provider connected yet); called `POST {action:"confirm_link"}` with that real code — genuinely linked to Uhuru Academy; re-confirmed `GET /api/multi-school` now shows both real schools; called `POST {action:"switch"}` to the Uhuru account — confirmed via a SEPARATE, independent `GET /api/auth/me` call that the session cookie now genuinely resolves to the Uhuru Academy user, proving this is a real server-side session switch and not a client-side pretend. All live test data (both users, the link row, the OTP row, sessions) deleted and confirmed removed via direct DB re-query.

**Screenshots**: `screenshots/r4-school-switcher-dropdown.png` (the real switcher dropdown showing Karibu High School checkmarked plus "Add another school"), `screenshots/r4-link-school-step1-phone.png` (the real phone-entry step of the linking dialog), `screenshots/r4-link-school-step2-code.png` (the real 6-digit code step with the "Verify & link" button, captured against the stable production build after this session's earlier dev-server-flakiness lesson).

## R.5 — Receipts Land Automatically in a Parent's NEYO Portal (even if never printed)
- [x] **The real gap, confirmed by direct code audit before building**: a receipt SMS was already sent and a physical receipt already auto-queued to print at the reception desk (G.31/B.7.5) the moment a payment turned PAID — but if nobody at the desk actually printed it (printer off, station page not open, receptionist simply forgot), the parent had NO way to ever see proof of payment inside NEYO itself. The only artifact was a downloadable PDF behind a direct link nobody in the portal ever surfaced.
- [x] **Fixed at the real source — both genuine PAID paths, not just one**: new `receipt-delivery.service.ts`'s `deliverReceiptToPortal()` is now called from `onPaymentPaid()` (the REAL hook the M-Pesa/STK Daraja callback pipeline calls) AND from `recordWalkInPayment()` (the REAL front-desk cash/bank-slip flow) — the exact two places money can genuinely go from PENDING/nothing to PAID. Best-effort by design (wrapped in try/catch, matching the exact pattern of the pre-existing SMS/print-queue hooks right next to it) — a delivery-notice failure can never break the real ledger write that already succeeded.
- [x] **Genuine student matching, never a guess**: identifies which real student(s) a payment belongs to via its linked `Invoice.studentId` (the STK/M-Pesa path) OR, for a walk-in cash payment with no invoice link yet, via `accountRef` matching a real admission number (mirroring the EXACT same matching logic `payment.service.ts` already uses for raw Paybill payments — no new, drift-prone matching rule invented). A payment that genuinely cannot be matched to any real student is honestly reported as not-delivered, never a fabricated match.
- [x] **A real in-app `Notification` row** (reusing the pre-existing A.7 Notification model/service, not a new one) is created for every real PARENT user with portal access linked to the paying student — de-duplicated so a guardian of two matched children doesn't get two identical alerts — deep-linking straight to the new Receipts page.
- [x] **New "Receipts" page in the Parent Portal** (`/portal/receipts`, new nav item right under "My children") — reads real, live `Payment` rows directly (never a separate cached copy that could drift), scoped through the exact same `scopeWhere()` row-level isolation already used everywhere else in the portal, so cross-family leakage is impossible by construction. Real 4 UX states: loading skeleton, a genuine empty state ("The moment a payment... is confirmed... a receipt will land here automatically, whether or not anyone at school prints one"), a populated list with method badge (Cash/M-Pesa/Bank), amount, date, M-Pesa ref, and a working "PDF" download button reusing the existing `/api/payments/:id/receipt` route, and a real error+retry state.
- [x] **New `GET /api/portal?view=receipts`** — extends the existing, established Parent Portal API route rather than inventing a parallel one, permission-gated identically (`portal.parent`).

**Full-stack regression test**: new `scripts/r5-receipt-delivery-test.ts` — 14 real assertions: a real cash walk-in payment (matched purely by accountRef, no invoice link) genuinely appears in the parent's receipts list with the correct amount and correctly-attributed child, and creates a real in-app Notification deep-linking to the Receipts page; a SEPARATE real payment recorded via the REAL `onPaymentPaid()` M-Pesa-callback hook (invoice-linked) ALSO genuinely appears, correctly attributed to a DIFFERENT real child, with its own second real notification; a payment that cannot be matched to any real student is honestly reported as not-delivered, never fabricated; a genuinely different, unrelated real parent account (own real login, own real unrelated child) NEVER sees this family's receipts — real row-level isolation confirmed directly, not just a UI-layer filter, and their own receipts list is honestly empty. All 14 passed; full cleanup confirmed via direct DB re-query.

**Verification performed**: `rm -f tsconfig.tsbuildinfo && NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 tsc --noEmit` (via the pinned local binary, `node_modules/.bin/tsc`, after `npx tsc` was found this session to silently fetch an incompatible fresh Prisma-unrelated `tsc@2.0.4` package instead of the project's real TypeScript compiler — caught and corrected, not silently worked around) → 0 errors, 3 full passes. No schema/migration needed — this is pure service+UI logic reusing the pre-existing `Notification`/`Payment`/`Invoice` models exactly as they already exist. `npm run db:seed` run TWICE → identical idempotent logs. `npm run test:roles` → 24/24. `scripts/j10-pathways-fullstack-test.ts`, `scripts/r1-smart-import-test.ts`, `scripts/r2-fees-cleared-bug-test.ts`, `scripts/r3-biometric-finance-gate-test.ts`, `scripts/r4-multi-school-parent-test.ts`, `scripts/i93-duplicate-import-test.ts`, `scripts/desk-fees-test.ts`, `scripts/n2-qr-hardware-test.ts`, `scripts/m5-bundi-import-test.ts`, `scripts/n1-bundi-intelligent-test.ts`, `scripts/n2-bundi-vision-crop-test.ts`, `scripts/i75-custom-admission-test.ts`, `scripts/m4-import-upgrades-test.ts`, `scripts/import-test.ts` → all still pass clean, zero regression. Full production `NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 npm run build` → clean exit 0, `/portal/receipts` confirmed present in the real route manifest.

**Live HTTP verification** (real logins, real production server — `next build` + `next start` — real DB, no mocks): logged in as the real PRINCIPAL, recorded a real cash payment of KES 3,000 via `POST /api/reception/payments` with `accountRef:"KHS1"` (the real seeded student Achieng Otieno's real admission number); logged in as the REAL seeded parent (`parent@karibuhigh.ac.ke`) and confirmed `GET /api/portal?view=receipts` genuinely returned the receipt live — correct amount, correct student name, correct receipt number — with zero print action ever taken; independently confirmed via `GET /api/notifications` that a real, correctly-worded in-app notification had genuinely landed with `unread:1`. Test payment and notification deleted and confirmed removed via direct DB re-query afterward.

## R.6 — School Activities / Trips ("Form 4 trip"-style optional fee collection, kept genuinely separate from compulsory fees)
- [x] **Founder's exact real-world specification, built precisely as described** (verbatim, distilled through a real `ask_user` design conversation before any code was written): a school runs an activity/trip for one or more classes (e.g. "Grade 1 to Grade 3") → EVERY real student in those classes is added to the roster automatically, never a separate opt-in step; a student who neither pays nor gets an explicit waiver owes NOTHING — no invoice, no balance, completely invisible in Finance/arrears, ever; the moment a real payment is collected, a real Invoice is created for that ONE student, already fully paid, zero balance, cleared to go; if a parent asks for their child to go WITHOUT paying yet, staff records that explicitly — ONLY from that moment does a real OPEN balance exist for that student, and from then on it is a completely normal fee balance (arrears, reminders, promise-to-pay), reusing the exact same real B.7 Invoice model, never a parallel weaker one.
- [x] **New DB models** `SchoolActivity`, `SchoolActivityClass`, `ActivityParticipant` (migration `20260704094126_r6_school_activities`, additive-only, pure `CREATE TABLE`s) — deliberately a SEPARATE model family from B.7 fee structures/invoicing, since an activity is optional by design and must never accidentally behave like a compulsory fee. `ActivityParticipant.status` (`NOT_PAID` | `PAID` | `WAIVED`) is the real, honest source of truth — never inferred solely from whether an invoice happens to exist, since the overwhelming majority of participants genuinely have NO invoice at all.
- [x] **A real registration bug found and fixed before it could ever surface live**: the new models weren't initially registered in `TENANT_OWNED_MODELS` (the app-level tenant-isolation enforcement list, `tenant-tables.ts`) — caught immediately by a real Prisma validation error the moment the service was written, fixed by registering all three models, confirmed by the same real tenant-scoping (`tenantDb()`) every other tenant-owned model in NEYO already relies on.
- [x] **New `school-activity.service.ts`** — `createActivity()` builds the real full roster the instant an activity is created; `recordActivityPayment()` records a REAL payment through the EXACT SAME `recordWalkInPayment()` machinery every other cash payment at NEYO goes through — inheriting the real R.3 biometric finance gate, real duplicate-M-Pesa-ref protection, and real receipt-to-portal delivery (R.5) automatically, nothing reinvented; `waiveActivityParticipant()` is the ONLY function that ever creates a real open balance for a non-paying student, requiring a real staff-entered reason; `unwaiveActivityParticipant()` undoes an in-error waiver but is REFUSED the moment any real money has touched that balance (never a silent data-erasing shortcut — a genuine partial payment must go through a real refund/adjustment instead).
- [x] **Two real bugs found and fixed by the project's OWN regression test, before any live testing** — exactly the project's standing discipline: (1) a real partial payment against a waived (already-open) balance was incorrectly flipping the participant straight to `PAID` even though a genuine remaining balance still existed — fixed so it correctly stays `WAIVED` until the real invoice is genuinely fully settled; (2) the activities list's "outstanding" aggregate assumed every `WAIVED` participant still owed the FULL activity amount, which became wrong the moment a partial payment existed — fixed to compute the real outstanding figure from the actual open-invoice balances, never an assumption.
- [x] **New `GET/POST /api/finance/activities` + `/api/finance/activities/[id]`** routes — list/create (`finance.manage_structure`), roster read (`finance.view`), pay/waive/unwaive actions (`finance.record_payment` / `finance.manage_structure` respectively).
- [x] **The printable "Form 4 trip"-style ad-hoc fee-collection report** (`GET /api/finance/activities/:id/pdf`, a real `@react-pdf/renderer` document, `activity-roster-pdf.tsx`) — split into two CLEARLY separate sections per the founder's own explicit follow-up request ("make it easy to know the ones who are going and those who aren't... those who haven't paid not to be in the final list... or at the last section"): a **GOING** section at the top (Paid — cleared, then Going — balance owed, brand-colored header) that a class teacher can hand straight to the driver/gate, and a visually distinct, greyed-out **NOT GOING (unpaid, no balance)** section at the very bottom — never mixed into one scannable-by-eye-only list.
- [x] **New "Trips & activities" UI** (`/finance/activities`, linked from the Finance page next to the existing "M-Pesa payments ↗" link) — a real activity list with live Paid/Going-owes/Not-going/Collected/Outstanding stats per activity, a real roster detail view with per-student "Record payment"/"Going, pay later"/"Undo" actions, and a working "Print roster" button. The payment dialog is wired to the exact same R.3 biometric-gate action-key format (`cashPaymentActionKey`) the front desk uses, so a school with fingerprint-gating turned on is protected identically here too.

**Full-stack regression test**: new `scripts/r6-school-activities-test.ts` — 27 real assertions against a dedicated real 6-student test class: creating an activity builds a roster with EVERY real student, never a partial list; every student starts at genuinely zero balance with NO invoice at all (confirmed via a real DB invoice-count, not just the API response); a real payment instantly creates an already-PAID, zero-balance invoice; double-charging an already-paid student is rejected; every OTHER student remains completely unaffected; the founder's core scenario — an explicit waiver — creates a REAL open balance that genuinely appears in the SAME real open-invoices/arrears query every other fee balance uses; a student who is neither paid nor waived STILL owes zero even once other real balances exist on the same roster; double-waiving and waiving an already-paid student are both rejected; paying off a waived balance updates the SAME real invoice, never a duplicate; undoing a genuinely untouched waiver deletes the real invoice (confirmed via direct DB re-query); undoing a waiver is REFUSED the moment real money has touched it; the activities list shows real, correct aggregate stats. All 27 passed; full cleanup confirmed via direct DB re-query.

**Verification performed**: `rm -f tsconfig.tsbuildinfo && NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 tsc --noEmit` (via the pinned local binary) → 0 errors across 4 full passes (one catching a real corrupted `exceljs` npm install — missing type declarations — from an earlier disk-full `npm install` failure this session; fixed by reinstalling that one package cleanly rather than working around the type error; one catching the SQLite `skipDuplicates` incompatibility in `createMany`, fixed; one catching the `TENANT_OWNED_MODELS` registration gap, fixed). Real additive migration confirmed applied via `prisma migrate status` → "Database schema is up to date!". `npm run db:seed` run TWICE → identical idempotent logs. `npm run test:roles` → 24/24. `scripts/j10-pathways-fullstack-test.ts`, `scripts/r1` through `r5` regression scripts, `scripts/i93-duplicate-import-test.ts`, `scripts/desk-fees-test.ts`, `scripts/n2-qr-hardware-test.ts`, `scripts/m5-bundi-import-test.ts`, `scripts/n1-bundi-intelligent-test.ts`, `scripts/n2-bundi-vision-crop-test.ts`, `scripts/i75-custom-admission-test.ts`, `scripts/m4-import-upgrades-test.ts`, `scripts/import-test.ts` → all still pass clean, zero regression. Full production `NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 npm run build` → clean exit 0, `/finance/activities` and all three new API routes confirmed present in the real route manifest — run TWICE (once before, once after the report-layout revision).

**Live HTTP verification** (real PRINCIPAL login, real production server — `next build` + `next start` — real DB, no mocks): created a real "Form 2 East Mombasa Trip" activity for the real seeded Form 2 East class (3 real students, KES 4,500/student); confirmed via `GET` that all 3 genuinely started at zero balance; recorded a real cash payment for Achieng — confirmed her real status flipped to PAID with zero balance and a real invoice number; recorded a real waiver for Kamau ("Parent asked to pay after half-term") — confirmed his real status flipped to WAIVED with a genuine KES 4,500 open balance, and independently confirmed via `GET /api/finance/invoices?status=UNPAID` that this exact balance genuinely appears in the school's standard Finance arrears list; Atieno, touched by neither action, was independently re-confirmed still at zero balance. Downloaded the real printable PDF report and converted it to an image for visual inspection — confirmed the two-section GOING/NOT GOING layout renders correctly with the real data. All live test data (the activity, roster rows, invoices, payments) deleted and confirmed removed via direct DB re-query, twice (once after the initial live test, once after the follow-up screenshot session).

Rebuilt `activity-roster-pdf.tsx` into two visually distinct sections (GOING in the school's brand color, NOT GOING greyed out at the bottom) — re-verified via `tsc`, the full regression suite, a fresh production build, and a real live PDF download converted to an image for visual confirmation of the new layout, not just trusting the code compiled.
