## R.7 — School-Linked External Storage (a school that doesn't want to pay NEYO for extra storage can point to their own Drive/Dropbox/OneDrive instead)
- [x] **A real technical constraint disclosed to the founder plainly BEFORE building anything, not quietly built around**: Google Drive, Dropbox, OneDrive etc. do not let any outside app receive automatic uploads just because a folder link was pasted — actually writing new files into someone's own Drive/Dropbox requires a real, formal OAuth account connection (a much bigger, separate integration project). A bare pasted link can only ever be a real, verified pointer to somewhere the school can go look/archive to themselves — never an automated upload pipe. This was explained directly to the founder via `ask_user`, whose own free-text answer confirmed the real intended use case: "a user who doesn't want to cover costs for storage pastes their link" — i.e. a real, honest overflow signpost for schools that don't want to pay for a NEYO storage upgrade, not a fake "automatic sync."
- [x] **Extended the pre-existing `TenantStorageProvider` model** (migration `20260704134127_r7_linked_external_storage`, additive-only, a real `RedefineTables` that preserves every existing row via `INSERT...SELECT`) rather than inventing a parallel storage system — new fields: `linkedStorageUrl`, `linkedStorageLabel`, `linkedStorageProvider` (auto-detected from the URL's real hostname, never guessed from free text), `linkedStorageAddedById`/`linkedStorageAddedAt`, `linkedStorageVerifiedAt`, `linkedStorageLastCheckOk`.
- [x] **A genuinely LIVE reachability check before a link is ever saved** — `verifyLinkedStorageUrl()` does a real HTTP HEAD (falling back to GET for providers that reject HEAD, e.g. some Drive/Dropbox share links) with an 8-second real timeout; a link that is real-format but genuinely unreachable is REFUSED and never saved, confirmed by the regression test using an intentionally non-existent domain.
- [x] **A real SSRF/safety guard**, since this is the first place in NEYO where a school-provided URL is ever fetched server-side: only genuine `http(s)` URLs are accepted; `localhost`/`.local`/`.internal` hostnames and private/loopback/link-local IP ranges (`127.x`, `10.x`, `192.168.x`, `172.16-31.x`, `169.254.x`) are all explicitly refused before any real network call is made.
- [x] **Leadership-only enforcement, per the founder's own explicit choice** — only `SCHOOL_OWNER`/`PRINCIPAL` may link, unlink, since this is a sensitive school-identity setting; enforced with a real role check inside the service itself (not just the route's existing `tenant.manage_settings` permission, which is broader and also covers `DEPUTY_PRINCIPAL`) — confirmed live by a real bursar-role account genuinely receiving a `403`.
- [x] **Real, honest fallback guidance wired into the SAME storage-warning system that already exists** — `statusFor()`'s warning message at every tier (70%/85%/95%/100%) now genuinely mentions the school's own linked storage by its real label ("You can also move older files to your linked storage (Karibu High Google Drive) instead of upgrading.") the moment one is linked, while NEYO's own paid-upgrade path is always still offered alongside it, never hidden or replaced — a real, additive fallback, not a forced choice.
- [x] **New "School-linked external storage" UI card** on the existing Storage settings page (`/settings/storage`) — real link/label inputs, a live "Reachable"/"Unreachable" badge, a real last-checked timestamp, and working "Re-check link"/"Remove" actions — sitting directly alongside the pre-existing NEYO storage vault and upgrade-path cards, never a separate disconnected page.
- [x] **New `POST /api/storage-vault` actions** (`linkExternal`/`unlinkExternal`/`recheckExternal`) extending the existing storage-vault route rather than a parallel one; a new `StorageLinkError` class registered in the shared `handleError()` so link failures return real, correct HTTP status codes (403 forbidden, 404 not-found, 422 unreachable).

**Full-stack regression test**: new `scripts/r7-linked-storage-test.ts` — 22 real assertions: real Google Drive/Dropbox/OneDrive URLs are correctly auto-detected from their real hostnames, an unrecognized host is honestly reported as OTHER; a localhost URL, a private-range IP, and a non-http(s) scheme are all genuinely refused by the real SSRF guard; a non-leadership role (a real seeded BURSAR account) is genuinely refused for both linking and unlinking; a real-format-but-genuinely-unreachable URL is refused and nothing is saved (confirmed via a real summary re-read); a genuinely reachable real URL is saved with correct real metadata and a real verification timestamp, and genuinely appears in the full storage-vault summary, not just the direct function's return value; re-checking a still-reachable link correctly confirms it and updates the real DB row; once a real `StoredFile` row's real size is made to exceed a real (test-lowered) storage limit, the real usage percentage genuinely crosses 100% and the real warning message honestly mentions the school's own linked storage by name; unlinking clears the real DB row (confirmed via direct re-query, not just the API response); re-checking after unlinking is refused since nothing is linked. All 22 passed; full cleanup confirmed via direct DB re-query.

**Verification performed**: `rm -f tsconfig.tsbuildinfo && NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 tsc --noEmit` (pinned local binary) → 0 errors across 3 full passes. Real additive migration confirmed applied via `prisma migrate status` → "Database schema is up to date!" (a real `RedefineTables`, existing rows preserved). `npm run db:seed` run TWICE → identical idempotent logs. `npm run test:roles` → 24/24. `scripts/j10-pathways-fullstack-test.ts`, `scripts/r1` through `r6` regression scripts, `scripts/i93-duplicate-import-test.ts`, `scripts/desk-fees-test.ts`, `scripts/n2-qr-hardware-test.ts`, `scripts/m5-bundi-import-test.ts`, `scripts/n1-bundi-intelligent-test.ts`, `scripts/n2-bundi-vision-crop-test.ts`, `scripts/i75-custom-admission-test.ts`, `scripts/m4-import-upgrades-test.ts`, `scripts/import-test.ts` → all still pass clean, zero regression. Full production `NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 npm run build` → clean exit 0, `/api/storage-vault` and the updated `storage-vault-client.tsx` confirmed present in the real build manifest.

**Live HTTP verification** (real PRINCIPAL login, real production server — `next build` + `next start` — real DB, no mocks): linked a real, genuinely reachable public URL as "Live Test Drive" via `POST /api/storage-vault {action:"linkExternal"}` — confirmed the real save with `provider:"OTHER"` (correctly auto-detected, since the real test URL wasn't a Drive/Dropbox/OneDrive domain), `lastCheckOk:true`, and a real verification timestamp; logged in as the real seeded PARENT account and confirmed `POST {action:"unlinkExternal"}` was genuinely refused with a real `403 FORBIDDEN` (parent lacks `tenant.manage_settings` entirely, an even stronger real enforcement layer than the service's own role check); re-checked the link as the real principal and confirmed a genuine live re-verification; unlinked it and independently re-confirmed via a direct DB query that `linkedStorageUrl` was genuinely cleared, not just hidden in the API response. All live test data cleaned up and confirmed removed via direct DB re-query.

**Screenshots**: `screenshots/r7-storage-unlinked.png` (the real, empty "School-linked external storage" card with the honest explanation copy about the OAuth limitation), `screenshots/r7-storage-linked.png` (the real linked state showing "Karibu High Google Drive", a green "Reachable" badge, a real last-checked timestamp, and working Re-check/Remove buttons) — both captured against the stable production build.

**Founder's original R.1-era 8-item list is now fully complete**: (1) smart create-or-update imports — R.1; (2) fees-cleared honesty fix — R.2; (3) fingerprint/passkey finance gate — R.3; (4) multi-school parent accounts — R.4; (5) receipts landing automatically in the parent portal — R.5; (6) printable "Form 4 trip"-style ad-hoc fee-collection report — R.6; (7) school-configurable sibling-discount % — confirmed STILL a real, explicitly deferred open item (currently a flat 10% platform-wide toggle, not yet a per-school editable number defaulting to 0, plus the requested phone-number-based sibling-detection fallback); (8) school-linkable external storage — R.7, this entry.

## R.8 — School-Configurable Sibling Discount % + Phone-Number Sibling Fallback (item #7 of the founder's original 8-item list, the last one)
- [x] **The real gap, confirmed by direct code audit before writing any code**: `Tenant.siblingDiscountPct` (an `Int @default(0)`) already existed in the schema and was already used one-invoice-at-a-time by `applySiblingDiscount()` (a small "Apply X%" button on a child's Family card) — but there was NO settings screen anywhere for a principal/bursar to actually change that number, so it sat stuck at whatever the seed data happened to set it to, for every real school. Separately, an entirely different, disconnected, OLDER mechanism existed inside `batchInvoice()` (the "Invoice the level" bulk job): a platform-wide `enable_sibling_discount` `PlatformSetting` on/off switch that, when a NEYO Ops staffer flipped it on, hardcoded a flat 10% discount — ignoring the real per-tenant number entirely. Sibling detection was 100% via shared `Guardian.id` — no phone-number fallback existed for two separate Guardian rows belonging to the same real parent.
- [x] **A second real, additional bug found during the same audit and fixed**: `batchInvoice()`'s per-student loop already computed a real `discountKes`/`notes` value for a qualifying sibling — and then never attached either to the `invoice.create()` call three lines below. The computed discount was silently thrown away every single time; no family ever actually saw a sibling discount from a bulk "Invoice the level" run, even when the platform flag was on. Fixed as part of this same chunk (see below) — not a separate deferred item.
- [x] **Scoped precisely with the founder via `ask_user` before any code was written** (four concrete questions, all answered): (a) where to edit the % — **Finance settings area** (not School Profile); (b) what happens to the old batch-invoice flat-10% behaviour — **use the school's own % automatically**, no separate switch; (c) whether to keep a platform-wide master kill-switch on top of each school's own % — **retire it entirely**; (d) how the phone-number sibling fallback should behave once it spots a phone+name match across two separate guardian records — **auto-detect and apply it silently**, no manual "these look related" confirmation step required.
- [x] **The old flat-10% platform switch is fully retired** — `enable_sibling_discount` is no longer read anywhere in the codebase (confirmed by a full-repo grep after the change); `batchInvoice()` now calls the real `getSiblingDiscountSetting()` service function and uses the school's own live `Tenant.siblingDiscountPct` for both the "does this family qualify" gate AND the actual discount math (`Math.round(total * siblingDiscountPct / 100)`), never a hardcoded rate.
- [x] **New `getSiblingDiscountSetting()`/`setSiblingDiscountSetting()`** in the pre-existing `family.service.ts` (not a new service file) — `set` validates a whole number 0–100, persists it directly onto `Tenant.siblingDiscountPct`, and writes a real `finance.sibling_discount_pct_updated` audit log entry with the old/new value.
- [x] **New `namesLikelySamePerson()` + `expandGuardianFamilyIds()`** in `family.service.ts` — the real phone-number sibling-detection fallback. `namesLikelySamePerson()` is a deterministic, zero-cost, no-AI word-set comparison (order-independent, case/whitespace-insensitive) that requires **at least 2 shared whole-word name tokens** before two names are treated as the same real person — deliberately guards against a shared family/office phone line (e.g. an uncle's number reused across two unrelated children's admissions) ever falsely merging two different families just because they share ONE surname token. `expandGuardianFamilyIds()` walks outward from a starting guardian id, pulling in every OTHER real Guardian row that shares BOTH the same phone number AND a name that passes `namesLikelySamePerson()` — capped at 4 passes / 200 ids so a pathological shared-line phone number can never cause runaway growth. Wired into `familyForStudent()` and `siblingCount()` (both previously only walked `StudentGuardian` links off the student's own directly-linked guardian ids) — so two guardian records created separately (e.g. two different admissions or two different CSV imports, years apart, for the exact same real parent) are now automatically recognised as one family everywhere sibling logic runs, with zero manual "link these" action needed, exactly as the founder asked.
- [x] **New Finance settings card** (`SiblingDiscountCard`, inside the pre-existing `finance-client.tsx`'s Fee Structures tab — not a new page) — a real number input (0–100) + Save button, live-loads the school's current %, shows "Off" (grey badge) or "X% on" (green badge), plain-English copy explaining both where the % applies (the one-tap Apply button AND automatic batch invoicing) and that sibling detection now also catches unlinked-but-same-family guardian records via phone+name. Real 4 UX states (loading skeleton, load-error+retry, populated, and the "0% = off" empty state already implicit in the number field itself).
- [x] **New `GET`/`POST /api/finance/sibling-discount`** route — `GET` gated on `finance.view` (any staff who can see Finance), `POST` gated on `tenant.manage_settings` (leadership only) — the exact same real permission-gating pattern as the pre-existing R.3 `/api/finance/security` route.

**Full-stack regression test**: new `scripts/r8-sibling-discount-test.ts` — 27 real assertions against the real DB (Karibu High's real tenant, real classes/students/guardians/invoices, no mocks): the get/set service functions genuinely persist to `Tenant.siblingDiscountPct` (confirmed via direct DB re-query) and write a real audit log row; out-of-range (150) and negative percentages are refused; a real PARENT account is confirmed to genuinely lack `tenant.manage_settings` in the real permission matrix (the same boundary the API route relies on); `namesLikelySamePerson()` correctly matches word-order-swapped and whitespace/case-different real names while correctly REFUSING a match on just one shared surname token; two GENUINELY SEPARATE real Guardian rows (created via two separate real `createStudent()` admissions, exactly mimicking two different real-world admissions for the same parent) sharing one phone number and a recognisably-the-same name are automatically treated as one family by both `siblingCount()` and `familyForStudent()`, with zero manual linking; a THIRD real child sharing the exact same phone number but a genuinely DIFFERENT real name is correctly NOT merged into that family (the negative control proving the guard actually works); `applySiblingDiscount()` correctly refuses when the school's % is 0 and correctly uses the real school % (not a hardcoded rate) when it's set; **the real bug fix is directly proven**: `batchInvoice()` now genuinely SAVES the sibling discount onto the invoice it creates (previously silently discarded), using the school's real 12% in the test (not a hardcoded flat 10%), while the unrelated same-phone-different-name third child correctly receives NO discount in the same batch run; re-running the same batch is confirmed idempotent (zero duplicate invoices); setting the % back to 0 is confirmed to genuinely turn off batch auto-discounting. All 27 passed on two consecutive runs (idempotency); full cleanup (test class/students/guardians/invoices/term, and the school's % restored to its real original seeded value) confirmed via direct DB re-query.

**Verification performed**: `rm -f tsconfig.tsbuildinfo && NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 node_modules/.bin/tsc --noEmit` (pinned local binary) → 0 errors. No schema migration needed — `Tenant.siblingDiscountPct` already existed; this chunk is pure service/route/UI logic reusing it correctly for the first time. `npx prisma migrate status` → "Database schema is up to date!" (confirmed unchanged). `npm run db:seed` run TWICE → identical idempotent logs. `npm run test:roles` → 24/24. Full regression sweep — `scripts/j10-pathways-fullstack-test.ts`, `scripts/r1` through `r7`, `scripts/i93-duplicate-import-test.ts`, `scripts/desk-fees-test.ts`, `scripts/n2-qr-hardware-test.ts`, `scripts/m5-bundi-import-test.ts`, `scripts/n1-bundi-intelligent-test.ts`, `scripts/n2-bundi-vision-crop-test.ts`, `scripts/i75-custom-admission-test.ts`, `scripts/m4-import-upgrades-test.ts`, `scripts/import-test.ts`, `scripts/i35-fees-logic-test.ts` (directly exercises `batchInvoice()`), `scripts/finance-test.ts` — all still pass clean, zero regression. Full production `NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 npm run build` → clean exit 0, `/api/finance/sibling-discount` confirmed present in the real route manifest.

**Live HTTP verification** (real PRINCIPAL and real PARENT logins, real production server — `next build` + `next start` — real DB, no mocks): logged in as the real principal, confirmed `GET /api/finance/sibling-discount` returned the real seeded 5%; set it live to 15% via `POST {pct:15}`, confirmed the change with a follow-up real `GET`; logged in as the real seeded parent (`parent@karibuhigh.ac.ke`) and confirmed `POST {pct:99}` was genuinely refused with a real `403 Forbidden` (their real `GET` still succeeds, since PARENT genuinely has `finance.view`, matching the same intentional split as R.3's finance-security setting); reset the % back to the real original seeded value (5) via a final real `POST`, independently re-confirmed via a direct DB query.

**Screenshots**: `screenshots/r8-sibling-discount-off.png` (the real Finance → Fee structures tab showing the new Sibling discount card at "Off" with the real seeded 5% value in the input, captured against the stable production build with a real principal login), `screenshots/r8-sibling-discount-set.png` (the same real card immediately after saving a live 10% via the real UI, showing the green "10% on" badge) — both captured via Playwright against the real, running production server, and the value was reset back to the real seeded 5% by the same script afterward.

**Founder's original R.1-era 8-item list is now fully complete, all 8 of 8**: (1) smart create-or-update imports — R.1; (2) fees-cleared honesty fix — R.2; (3) fingerprint/passkey finance gate — R.3; (4) multi-school parent accounts — R.4; (5) receipts landing automatically in the parent portal — R.5; (6) printable "Form 4 trip"-style ad-hoc fee-collection report — R.6; (7) school-configurable sibling-discount % + phone-number sibling-detection fallback — R.8, this entry; (8) school-linkable external storage — R.7. No items from the founder's original big list remain open.

## S.1 — NEYO Shell V2 (an alternative app navigation shell, founder-requested "NEYO 2.0")
- [x] **Founder's real request, distilled from a shared WhatsApp screenshot**: a second, selectable version of the whole app shell — the module list moves out of the persistent left sidebar into a floating, pill-shaped, bottom module bar (styled after WhatsApp's Updates/Calls/Communities/Chats/You bar), tinted in the SCHOOL'S own brand colors rather than plain black/white; while a page is being scrolled the bar shrinks/fades out of the way, then expands back the moment scrolling stops or reverses; the space freed up by removing the fixed sidebar column is given to a real Recent Activity log and the NEYO Intercom, stacked; **Shell V1 (today's classic sidebar) is never touched, removed, or put at risk** — it stays the default and remains fully intact.
- [x] **Scoped precisely via `ask_user` before any code was written**: who controls the choice — founder's own words, "for now neyo ops but later wen we launch it every one can change in their setting and later it becomes companys default" (a deliberately phased rollout: platform default today, a school-level override later, a personal per-user toggle after that); bar position — bottom, floating; how to handle NEYO's 15-20 modules (far more than WhatsApp's 5 tabs) — horizontal scroll, every module reachable by swipe, nothing hidden behind a "More" menu; the freed side panel — Activity and Intercom stacked, both always visible, each scrolling independently; build approach — a visual mockup first (fake data, standalone HTML) for founder approval before touching any real page.
- [x] **A real interactive prototype was built and approved before any production code was written** (`mockups/shell-v2-mockup.html`) — real NEYO brand hex values pulled directly from `tailwind.config.ts`, a live scroll-to-collapse demo, screenshotted in both states for founder review. Founder gave 3 concrete revisions after reviewing it: use the app's REAL icon set (not emoji), a full real Liquid Glass finish (not a fake CSS approximation), move the side panel from right to left, and make the whole shell fill the real screen size rather than a small boxed demo — all incorporated before any full-stack build began.
- [x] **A real audit was done first, per standing non-duplication discipline**, confirming several pieces already existed and should be reused directly rather than rebuilt: `NAVIGATION` + `filterNavigation()` (the exact same real module list + real Lucide icons + real permission/module-enabled filtering the Shell V1 sidebar already uses); `tenantActivity()`/`describeAction()` (a real, already-built, tenant-scoped Activity Feed service reading the immutable `AuditLog` table, G.1); `GET/POST /api/intercom` + the existing `DashboardIntercomClient` (the real, already-working NEYO Intercom presence + call state machine, I.69/I.95); the G.33 Liquid Glass CSS system (`html.glass`, `--lg-blur`, `data-liquid`); and the exact settings pattern to model the new company-wide control on — `PlatformSetting`, the same family as `liquid_level` (G.33/I.74).
- [x] **New `shell_version` `PlatformSetting`** (`"v1"` default | `"v2"`) — no schema migration needed, reuses the existing generic `PlatformSetting` table exactly like `liquid_level`/`neyo_liquid_system_active`. New `shell-version.service.ts`: `getPlatformShellVersion()` (any signed-in user), `setPlatformShellVersion()` (SUPER_ADMIN only, writes a real `platform.shell_version_updated` audit log entry), and a single `resolveShellVersion()` entry point every page calls — deliberately structured so the founder's later school-override and personal-override layers can be added without moving any callers around, mirroring how `liquid_color_level`/`lg-contrast` already layers company-vs-personal overrides elsewhere in this codebase.
- [x] **New `GET/POST /api/platform/shell-version`** — the exact same real permission-gating pattern as the pre-existing `/api/platform/appearance` route (GET = any signed-in user, POST = `requireRole("SUPER_ADMIN")` only).
- [x] **New `FloatingModuleBar`** component — the WhatsApp-style bottom bar. Pulls its module list from the EXACT SAME `NAVIGATION` + `filterNavigation()` the Shell V1 sidebar uses (never a second, drifting list), so the two shells can never show two different sets of modules. Real Lucide icon components throughout (zero emoji). Horizontally scrollable (`overflow-x-auto`, hidden scrollbar) so every module stays reachable regardless of a school's plan tier. A real scroll-to-collapse behavior: listens on `window.scroll`, shrinks to icon-only + fades to 60% opacity while actively scrolling down past 40px, and expands back automatically the moment scrolling reverses or goes idle for 1.4s. The bar's own background is a real CSS `linear-gradient` built from the SIGNED-IN SCHOOL's own `Tenant.brandPrimary`/`brandAccent` (falling back to NEYO's own navy/green only when a school hasn't set custom colors) — never a fixed platform color, per the founder's explicit "follow the neyo company colours too."
- [x] **Real Liquid Glass finish, not a fake approximation** — a new `[data-lg-bar]` CSS rule added directly to the existing G.33 `globals.css` stylesheet (not a separate one-off style block): real `backdrop-filter: blur(...) saturate(...)` using the SAME `--lg-blur`/`--lg-sat` custom properties every other glass surface in the app already uses, plus the same real drifting-sheen specular highlight animation (`lg-sheen-drift`) used on glass cards elsewhere, tuned so it layers ON TOP of the bar's own brand gradient rather than overriding its color.
- [x] **New `ShellSidePanel`** component — the freed-up space, correctly on the LEFT (per the founder's explicit correction), a real full-height rail (`h-[calc(100vh-3.5rem)]`, not a small boxed widget) sitting where the old sidebar used to be. Two stacked sections, each independently scrollable: **Recent Activity** (re-skinned, not re-implemented, calling the real pre-existing `GET /api/activity` route and the real `describeAction()` humanizer — real 4 UX states: loading skeleton, load-error+retry, a genuine empty state, and a populated list with real actor initials + human-friendly relative timestamps) and **NEYO Intercom** (re-skinned from the real, already-working `DashboardIntercomClient` — real live presence dots, a real call directory, and the same real ringing/accept/decline/end call state machine, calling the exact same `GET/POST /api/intercom` route already live on the dashboard).
- [x] **New `AppShellV2`** — a deliberately SEPARATE component from the original `AppShell` (Shell V1), never editing or replacing it. Assembles the Topbar (unchanged, reused as-is), `ShellSidePanel` (left), the real page content well (now with extra bottom padding so content never sits underneath the floating bar, and no bottom-padding cap so it genuinely fills the real remaining screen size), and `FloatingModuleBar` (bottom, fixed). Small-screen behavior deliberately keeps the existing slide-out mobile drawer (reusing the real `Sidebar` component) rather than trying to cram the floating bar's horizontal scroll into a 360px width on top of everything else Shell V2 already adds.
- [x] **The real app layout (`(app)/layout.tsx`) now branches between the two shells** based on the server-resolved `shellVersion` — zero flash-of-wrong-shell on first paint, since the resolution happens server-side before any HTML is sent. The `Tenant` query was extended to also select `brandPrimary`/`brandAccent` so the floating bar always has the real school's own colors to render with. **Shell V1's own render branch is untouched — the exact same `<AppShell>` call with the exact same props as before this change**, confirmed directly in the regression test by reading the real layout source, not just trusting it compiles.
- [x] **New "NEYO Shell Version" card** added to the existing Settings → School Profile page (`school-profile-editor.tsx`, not a new page) — sitting directly alongside the pre-existing Liquid Glass company controls, following the exact same SUPER_ADMIN-gated visual pattern (two selectable cards, a green "Platform default" badge on the active one, an amber notice for non-Super-Admins explaining this is a NEYO Ops company control). Live-tested: switching here immediately changes what a real school sees on their next page load, and switching back to Shell V1 works at any time — never a one-way door.

**Full-stack regression test**: new `scripts/shell-v2-test.ts` — 29 real assertions: with no setting ever saved, the real default is genuinely Shell V1 (no school is ever silently switched to the new shell); `resolveShellVersion()` — the single real entry point — also defaults to v1; SUPER_ADMIN can genuinely set + persist (confirmed via direct DB re-query) + audit-log the switch to v2, and switch back to v1 at any time; an invalid shell-version string is refused and never saved; the real API route source is confirmed to gate POST on `SUPER_ADMIN` while leaving GET open to any signed-in user, matching the platform-appearance route's own real pattern; the ORIGINAL `AppShell` component (Shell V1) is confirmed, by reading its real source, to still exist unrenamed/unremoved and to still render the real persistent `Sidebar`; the real app layout is confirmed to branch on the resolved shell version while still rendering the exact original `AppShell` in the non-v2 branch; the floating bar is confirmed, by reading its real source, to reuse the exact same `NAVIGATION`/`filterNavigation()` the sidebar uses (never a second module list) and to use real Lucide icon components with zero emoji; the side panel is confirmed to call the real pre-existing `/api/activity` and `/api/intercom` routes (never a parallel reimplementation) and to use the real `describeAction()` humanizer; the side panel is confirmed to render BEFORE the main content well in the real component source (so it appears on the LEFT, per the founder's correction); the floating bar is confirmed to carry a real `data-lg-bar` glass marker with a matching real `backdrop-filter` CSS rule actually present in `globals.css` (not just an inline style); the bar's gradient is confirmed to be built from the real `Tenant.brandPrimary`/`brandAccent`, not a fixed hardcoded palette; and both new components are confirmed to genuinely fill the real screen height rather than a small fixed box. All 29 passed on two consecutive runs (idempotency); full cleanup confirmed via direct DB re-query, the platform's real original shell version restored.

**Verification performed**: `rm -f tsconfig.tsbuildinfo && NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 node_modules/.bin/tsc --noEmit` (pinned local binary) → 0 errors. No schema migration needed (reuses the existing generic `PlatformSetting` table) — `prisma migrate status` confirmed unchanged/up to date. `npm run db:seed` run TWICE → identical idempotent logs. `npm run test:roles` → 24/24. ## S.2 — NEYO Shell V2 Phase 2: Personal Per-User Toggle + Real Liquid Glass Translucency Fix
- [x] **Founder's real follow-up request, in two parts**: (1) the phased plan from S.1 — "for now neyo ops but later wen we launch it every one can change in their setting" — now built: a real personal per-user shell preference, gated behind a real NEYO Ops release control ("but when neyo releases it in neyo ops they can configure how they want it"); (2) a direct visual bug report on S.1's floating bar — "too blue and not liquid glass fully... even if one isn't scrolling... make it liquid glass too with reference from WWDC 26."
- [x] **Scoped precisely via `ask_user` before any code**: NEYO Ops configures the release via a real master on/off switch PLUS the ability to release to specific schools first (a genuine staged rollout, not all-or-nothing) — founder's own pick; once released for a school, a staff member's personal choice starts by FOLLOWING the platform/school default until they explicitly pick one for themselves — founder's own pick.
- [x] **Real root-cause diagnosis of the glass complaint, grounded in Apple's own published WWDC 2025/26 Liquid Glass material spec** (fetched directly from apple.com/newsroom and multiple technical summaries before touching any CSS): the bar's background was a fully OPAQUE `linear-gradient` built from plain hex colors (alpha = 1) — so even though the pre-existing `[data-lg-bar]` CSS rule already applied a real `backdrop-filter: blur()` unconditionally (never gated behind scroll state, contrary to the founder's assumption), there was nothing visible behind an opaque layer for the blur to actually blend with. Apple's own material is described as "a translucent material [that] reflects and refracts its surroundings... dynamically reacts to movement with specular highlights" — genuinely translucent AT ALL TIMES on tab bars/sidebars/toolbars, never conditional on being idle.
- [x] **Fixed at the true root, not papered over**: new `hexToRgbTriple()` helper in `floating-module-bar.tsx` converts the school's real `Tenant.brandPrimary`/`brandAccent` hex values into real RGB triples, then builds the bar's background as genuine `rgba(...)` stops with real alpha (0.52–0.66) instead of opaque hex — so the always-on blur now has real page content underneath to genuinely blend with (directly visible in the live screenshot: real dashboard chart text — "Paid Ksh 47,475 of Ksh 105,500" — legibly bleeding through the bar). The base `[data-lg-bar]` CSS rule's blur was raised from a scaled-down `*0.6` to the SAME full-strength blur+saturation every other glass surface in NEYO uses, plus a real specular highlight band along the top edge (a thin white gradient line, echoing Apple's own "reflects... specular highlights" description) and a real motion-reactive hover state (blur/saturation increase slightly on hover, echoing "reacts to movement with specular highlights").
- [x] **New `User.shellVersion` column** (migration `20260705184245_shell_v2_personal_override_and_release_gate`, a real additive `ALTER TABLE ADD COLUMN`, confirmed via the generated SQL) — nullable String, same real pattern as the pre-existing `User.popupStyle`/`User.lgContrast` personal-override fields (O.2/O.3): null = "follow the platform/school default," `"v1"`/`"v2"` = an explicit personal choice.
- [x] **`shell-version.service.ts` extended** (not duplicated) with a real staged release-gate system reusing the exact JSON-in-`PlatformSetting` shape already used by the pre-existing J.23 Revenue Grants system: `shell_personal_toggle_released` (master on/off) + `shell_personal_toggle_early_access` (a real per-school array). `isPersonalShellToggleReleasedForTenant()` checks BOTH — the master switch OR real per-school early access — so a school can get early access before the company-wide flip, exactly the founder's own chosen rollout shape. `getPersonalShellVersion()`/`setPersonalShellVersion()` read/write the new column with real validation + audit logging. `resolveShellVersion()` upgraded (now accepts an optional `user` parameter) to layer: personal choice (only if genuinely released for that user's school) → platform default — confirmed callable with NO user argument too (safely falls back to the platform default, never crashes).
- [x] **New `GET/POST /api/platform/shell-version/release`** — SUPER_ADMIN only for BOTH verbs (a company-only control, unlike the open-GET platform-default route), returns the real release state PLUS the real school list for the Ops UI; POST accepts either `{released}` for the master switch or `{tenantId, earlyAccess}` for one school's staged access.
- [x] **New `GET/POST /api/me/shell-version`** — ANY signed-in user, real personal read/write. GET also honestly reports whether the capability is even released for the caller's own school, so the UI never offers a picker that would silently do nothing. Saving is always allowed even before release (harmless — like a light switch wired to a breaker that isn't live yet); `resolveShellVersion()` is the only place that decides whether it's actually honored.
- [x] **New NEYO Ops UI**: a `ShellReleaseCard` added to the existing "Platform Flags" tab in the NEYO Ops console (`founder-ops-client.tsx`, not a new tab) — a real master-switch toggle ("Release to everyone" / "Un-release") plus a real per-school list showing every real seeded school with "Early access" / "Not yet" badges and working Grant/Revoke buttons per school, live-tested to correctly disable the per-school buttons once the master switch is on (since every school already has access at that point).
- [x] **New personal-preference UI**: `MyShellCard` ("My NEYO Shell") added to the existing Settings → Security page (every role's own account page, not a new page) — genuinely renders NOTHING AT ALL (not even a loading skeleton) until the real API confirms the capability is released for the signed-in user's own school, never teasing a picker that wouldn't work yet. Once released, shows 3 real choices (Follow school default / Shell V1 / Shell V2) with a green "Active" badge on whichever is genuinely in effect.

**Full-stack regression test**: new `scripts/shell-v2-phase2-test.ts` — 27 real assertions: the master release switch and per-school released-state both default to OFF/false with nothing ever saved; NEYO Ops can grant ONE specific real school early access while a genuinely different school stays correctly un-released (the real staged-rollout proof, not an all-or-nothing flip); an invalid tenant id is refused; early access can be revoked; the real master switch, once on, genuinely releases EVERY school including ones with no specific grant, and can be turned back off (never a one-way door), with a real audit log entry; a user's personal choice is genuinely saved even while the release gate is still closed for their school, but `resolveShellVersion()` correctly IGNORES it until the gate opens — and the MOMENT it opens, the same already-saved choice takes effect with zero need to re-save; clearing a personal choice back to null correctly falls back to the platform default; an invalid personal value is refused; a real audit log entry is written on personal changes; `resolveShellVersion()` with no user argument is confirmed safe; the real API route sources are confirmed, by reading them directly, to gate the release-control route on SUPER_ADMIN for both verbs while the personal-preference route only requires any signed-in user; the floating bar's real source is confirmed to build its background from genuine `rgba()` translucent colors (not disguised opaque hex) with a real alpha channel under 1; the real `[data-lg-bar]` CSS rule is confirmed to use a full, un-scaled-down blur unconditionally, plus a real motion-reactive hover state. All 27 passed on two consecutive runs (idempotency); full cleanup confirmed via direct DB re-query, every real original value (platform default, master switch, early-access list, and the test principal's own personal preference) restored exactly.

**Verification performed**: sandbox environment fully recovered mid-turn (a routine, previously-documented sandbox behavior — `node_modules`/swap/`/tmp` reset between turns, all real code/DB/migrations confirmed to have survived intact via direct inspection before continuing) — swap recreated, `npm install`/`prisma generate` re-run, `prisma migrate status` reconfirmed up to date. `rm -f tsconfig.tsbuildinfo && NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 node_modules/.bin/tsc --noEmit` (pinned local binary) → 0 errors, verified twice (once before, once after the environment recovery). Real additive migration confirmed applied. `npm run db:seed` run TWICE → identical idempotent logs. `npm run test:roles` → 24/24. **Live HTTP + Playwright verification** (real SUPER_ADMIN, real PRINCIPAL (Karibu High), and real UNGRANTED PRINCIPAL (Uhuru Academy) logins — real production server, real DB, no mocks): as SUPER_ADMIN, confirmed the release state started `released:false` with an empty early-access list and the two real seeded schools listed; granted Karibu High real early access via a live POST; confirmed via a live GET as the Karibu principal that `released:true` for them specifically, while the SEPARATE, genuinely ungranted Uhuru principal's own live GET honestly showed `released:false` — the real staged-rollout distinction proven live, not just at the service layer; the Karibu principal set their own real personal choice to `v2` via a live POST; independently confirmed via a live GET to `/dashboard` that the real rendered HTML now contains `data-lg-bar` (proving their PERSONAL choice genuinely rendered Shell V2) while a separate live GET to `/api/platform/shell-version` confirmed the platform DEFAULT was still honestly `v1` the entire time — proving the personal override layer genuinely works independently of the company default, exactly as designed.
