  - [ ] **AI Cost Optimizer (detect expensive model use, duplicate requests, oversized prompts)** — a genuinely new analysis layer; the only REAL AI-cost data that currently exists to analyze is Bundi Intelligent's own `BundiImportSession` rows (real `provider`/`model`/`costUsd` fields already there) — an optimizer here would start narrow (analyzing Bundi Intelligent's own real usage patterns for waste) rather than a general "detect expensive AI use across the whole app," since most of NEYO's actual AI-adjacent surfaces (report-card comments, lesson plans, etc.) are explicitly documented elsewhere in this same checklist (B.23) as intentionally rule-based/non-AI TODAY, platform-paused pending the real Bundi mascot launch — so there is currently very little real AI spend outside Bundi Intelligent to optimize.
  - [ ] **Storage Optimizer (duplicate files, unused uploads, old backups, oversized PDFs)** — real, buildable TODAY without waiting on anything else: `StoredFile.checksumSha256` (schema ~line 2655) ALREADY EXISTS and is the exact real field needed to detect true duplicate files (two different `StoredFile` rows with the identical checksum) — a real duplicate-detection query is a comparatively small, immediately achievable win reusing data that's already being captured, not a new capture mechanism. "Unused uploads" (a file nobody has referenced/viewed in N months) and "oversized PDFs" would need a new "last accessed" signal (doesn't exist today — `StoredFile` only has `createdAt`) — a real, small additive schema change if the founder wants this specific signal.
  - [ ] **SMS Optimizer (suggest switching to WhatsApp/email where available)** — real, buildable today: `UsageCounter` (real per-tenant SMS counts already tracked) + the real existing A.7 notification cascade (which ALREADY tries in-app → push → WhatsApp → SMS → email in that exact order, per the pre-existing cascade design) means NEYO may already be a good citizen here in principle — worth auditing WHY a school's SMS volume is high before assuming the fix is "nudge them to switch channels": if a school's parents mostly don't have WhatsApp/data, SMS may be the only real reachable channel for them, and an "optimizer" suggesting otherwise could genuinely hurt real parent communication — flag this nuance for whoever builds it, this is not a pure cost-engineering decision, it has a real reachability tradeoff.
  - [ ] **Server Optimizer (CPU/memory underutilization warnings)** — cannot be built without a real infrastructure-monitoring integration (Vercel/hosting-provider metrics API) — genuinely blocked on the same real external-API-integration work as the Cost Dashboard's live-numbers option above, not a standalone smaller task.
  - [ ] **Cost Per School table (revenue vs. infrastructure cost vs. profit, per school)** — the REVENUE half already exists per-school today (real `Payment`/`Subscription` data, already surfaced in `getCompanyHealthCheck()`'s "fees collected" and the real billing system) — the COST half is blocked on the same real per-school cost-attribution problem every cloud SaaS company solves imperfectly (shared infrastructure costs — a shared Postgres instance, a shared Vercel deployment — don't naturally split cleanly "per school" without a real allocation model, e.g. proportional to that school's real storage/request volume). Recommend this be built as an ESTIMATE (school's real usage signals, like storage used and SMS sent, as a proportional cost-allocation key) rather than claiming false precision — flag this explicitly, since presenting an estimate as if it were exact could lead to bad pricing decisions.
  - [ ] **Budget Alerts (AI/OCR/SMS spend thresholds)** — a real, comparatively small addition ONCE real cost tracking exists for each of those three areas (SMS is the most ready today, since `UsageCounter`/`SmsMarginConfig` already exist; AI/OCR would need the aggregation work described above first).
  - [ ] **AI-generated operational insight sentences** (e.g. "storage increased 18% this week due to scanned report cards") — genuinely the LAST piece to build, since it requires real trend data (from all of the above) to summarize; would reuse the exact same real "rule-based, plain-English, zero-AI-cost" summary pattern already used successfully elsewhere in this codebase (G.15's Term Pulse `buildPulseSummary()`, confirmed grep-verified to never say the word "AI") rather than requiring an actual LLM call for something a deterministic rule can already state clearly.
- [ ] **Real, important overall recommendation for whoever scopes this next**: this idea (`U.1`) is genuinely 5-8 separate real features bundled into one paragraph by the outside AI agent — do NOT attempt this as one chunk or even one session. Recommend sequencing: (1) real MANUAL monthly cost entry extending `NeyoMetricSnapshot` first (cheapest, fastest, immediately useful); (2) the real Storage duplicate-file optimizer (buildable today, zero new external dependencies, reuses `checksumSha256` that already exists); (3) real SMS-spend budget alerts (reuses existing `UsageCounter`/`SmsMarginConfig`); (4) only THEN consider live cloud-provider billing API integrations, one provider at a time, starting with whichever the founder finds most valuable to see live.

## U.2 — A Genuine Unit-Economics Dashboard (Revenue/Cost/Margin per School, per Student, per SMS, per AI Request, CAC, LTV, MRR)
- [ ] **Real audit finding: this is the SAME underlying data problem as U.1 above, described from a different angle** — MRR (`NeyoMetricSnapshot.mrrKes`) and revenue-per-school (real `Payment`/subscription data) already exist or are cheaply derivable; cost-per-school, cost-per-SMS (the SELL-side margin already exists via M.2's real `SmsMarginConfig`/`smsMarginDashboard()`, but the actual BUY-side cost NEYO pays Africa's Talking is not separately tracked as its own real ledger line — only the computed margin is), cost-per-AI-request, and cost-per-OCR-document all require the SAME real cost-tracking foundation U.1 describes. **CAC (Customer Acquisition Cost) and LTV (Customer Lifetime Value) are the two genuinely NEW concepts here not covered by U.1 at all** — CAC requires real marketing-spend data (which does not exist anywhere in NEYO today — there is no marketing-expense tracking model at all, confirmed via grep for "marketing" across `src/lib/services`, nothing found) divided by real new-signups-per-period (which DOES exist, `NeyoMetricSnapshot`-adjacent data); LTV requires a real formula over a school's real total lifetime revenue and real average subscription lifespan/churn rate (churn-risk SCORING already exists per G.30, but a real historical CHURN RATE — how many schools have actually cancelled, over what average tenure — is not currently computed anywhere).
- [ ] **Recommend this be explicitly built AFTER U.1's cost-tracking foundation exists, not in parallel** — a "unit economics dashboard" with half its numbers real and half either missing or estimated would be actively misleading for real business decisions; sequencing matters here more than almost anywhere else in this backlog.

## U.3 — NEYO Ops as "The Operating System for Running NEYO Itself" (a real Founder Morning Dashboard) + Real Role Tiers (School Users / School Admin / NEYO Support / NEYO Ops / Founder) + a "Founder AI" Q&A Layer
- [ ] **Real audit finding on role tiers — a genuinely important, currently-missing real distinction**: confirmed via direct read of `src/lib/core/roles.ts` — NEYO's real 16-role system has exactly ONE role for "runs the company": `SUPER_ADMIN`. `can()` (`permissions.ts`) grants a `SUPER_ADMIN` EVERY permission unconditionally, with zero further distinction. Confirmed via `session.ts`/impersonation code: the SAME `SUPER_ADMIN` role that can view Founder Ops metrics, flip platform flags, grant revenue features to schools, and IMPERSONATE any school's login (A.2.9, a real, powerful, audit-logged-but-still-very-sensitive capability) is a single undifferentiated tier — there is currently no real "NEYO Support" role that could, say, help a customer via the Intercom/impersonation-adjacent tools WITHOUT also being able to flip platform-wide feature flags or grant free revenue features to a school. The founder's proposed 5-tier model (School Users → School Administrator → NEYO Support → NEYO Operations → Founder) is a REAL, currently-missing, meaningfully more secure design — today, if any single `SUPER_ADMIN` credential were ever compromised, the blast radius is the ENTIRE company (every platform flag, every school's data via impersonation, every pricing/discount control) — genuinely worth taking seriously as a real security hardening project, not just an org-chart nicety.
- [ ] **Real, precise scoping of what a "Founder Account" vs "NEYO Ops" split would actually require**: this is NOT simply adding two new strings to the `ROLES` array — every one of the ~15+ SUPER_ADMIN-gated routes/services audited across this entire project's history (`requireRole("SUPER_ADMIN")` appears throughout `platform-appearance.service.ts`, `platform-flags.service.ts`, `feature-grants.service.ts`, `shell-version.service.ts` from this same session's S.1/S.2 work, `pricing-catalog.service.ts`, `revenue-ops.service.ts`, and more) would need to be individually re-classified into "safe for NEYO Ops staff" vs. "Founder-only, rare, exceptional" tiers — a real, substantial audit-and-reclassification project touching a large fraction of the company-level surface built across this entire project's history, not a quick permission-matrix edit. **Real open question for `ask_user`, and likely the single most consequential fork in this whole idea**: should "NEYO Ops" be a genuinely SEPARATE new role in the real 16-role enum (a bigger structural change, but the more architecturally correct one, matching how the founder described it), or should it be modeled as a NEW PERMISSION that can be granted to specific `SUPER_ADMIN`-tier staff accounts alongside the EXISTING role (a smaller, additive change, keeping `SUPER_ADMIN` as the umbrella "company staff" role but gating the most dangerous specific actions — impersonation, platform-flag changes, pricing changes — behind an EXTRA explicit permission most company staff wouldn't have)? The second approach is likely faster and lower-risk to build correctly; the founder's own language ("several levels...School Administrator...NEYO Support...NEYO Operations...Founder") suggests they're picturing the first (real distinct roles) — this genuinely needs a direct conversation before any schema work.
- [ ] **Real audit finding on the "Founder Morning Dashboard"/Company Dashboard vision**: this is real and buildable TODAY as a genuinely useful FIRST version using data that already exists, even before U.1's full cost-tracking project — `NeyoMetricSnapshot` already has schools/revenue/MRR/churn-risk counts; `getCompanyHealthCheck()` already has real per-school engagement signals; `runHealthChecks()` already has real system-status (DB/queue/storage); real failed-payment tracking exists via the billing state machine (A.5's real GRACE/SUSPENDED states); real new-signup tracking exists via `Tenant.createdAt`. **A real, achievable FIRST version of the founder's "Good morning, Elvis" dashboard could be assembled almost entirely from data NEYO ALREADY COMPUTES, just not yet in one single consolidated view** — recommend flagging this specific piece as a genuinely fast, high-value win compared to the AI-cost/cloud-cost pieces of U.1, which are blocked on real external integrations.
- [ ] **"Founder AI" (ask NEYO natural-language questions like "why did revenue drop this month?")**: **standing project law directly applies and must be respected here** — this project's own `PROMPT-1`/G.36 Bundi rule states the product "never says AI" in copy and that the real Bundi mascot AI layer is currently platform-PAUSED pending founder launch, with the explicit rule that "no feature may depend on this layer." A real "ask a natural-language question, get an answer with real data" capability for NEYO OPS INTERNAL USE (not customer-facing product copy) is a materially different context than a school-facing feature, but still: (a) it would be the FIRST real LLM-dependent feature in the entire live product if built before Bundi's own launch, a meaningful precedent-setting decision the founder should make consciously, not by default; (b) if built, it should very likely be branded/framed consistently with Bundi (this IS internal tooling, so the "never say AI" customer-copy rule may not strictly apply here since founders/ops staff, not schools, are the audience — but worth an explicit `ask_user` check rather than assuming either way). Real technical shape, if pursued: this would need a real internal query/retrieval layer over NEYO's own real data (revenue, churn signals, module-adoption stats, support tickets — most already real and queryable) fed to an LLM as context — a genuinely large, standalone project (a real "internal RAG-lite system"), not a quick addition.
- [ ] **Customer Success / Support Tickets, Feature Requests, Bug Reports tab — real, precise, PARTIAL overlap with existing systems, worth flagging so nobody duplicates work**: the founder's own PART T (added earlier this same session) already documents a real, currently-missing "school requests a custom feature, NEYO Ops reviews/quotes/approves" pipeline (T.3) — a real Support Tickets / Bug Reports system is a related but DISTINCT concept (ongoing operational support, not a one-off feature-build request) and does not exist today either (confirmed via the same grep from T.3, nothing found). Recommend these be scoped together (T.3 + this piece of U.3) since they'd likely share a very similar real underlying model shape (a ticket/request with a status pipeline, tenant-scoped, NEYO-Ops-visible), even though their CONTENT differs (a feature request vs. a "something is broken" report vs. a "we need custom work, what will it cost" request).
- [ ] **Product Analytics (most/least used modules, DAU/WAU, feature adoption, retention)** — real, PARTIALLY buildable today: `TenantModule.enabled` already gives a real per-school module-adoption count (reused by G.30's churn score); real DAU/WAU would need a new aggregation over `Session.createdAt` (the raw data already exists, just not pre-aggregated into a dashboard-ready daily/weekly rollup) — a real, comparatively achievable addition once someone decides the exact definitions (does "active" mean logged in, or performed a real write action that day — a meaningfully different real signal).
- [ ] **Compliance tab (privacy/data-export/data-deletion requests, policy acknowledgements)** — real audit finding: PARTIALLY already built. `tenant.export_data` (a real permission, A.2.10) already gives a school a real, working self-service data export. A CENTRALIZED, NEYO-Ops-visible log of every school's export/deletion requests across the whole platform (as opposed to each school just doing their own export locally) does not exist as its own dashboard today — a real, comparatively small addition (mostly a reporting/aggregation view over an action that's already real and already audit-logged via the existing immutable `AuditLog`, not a new capability).

## U.4 — Capacity-Based Pricing ("Neyo Complete": Every School Gets Every Feature, Priced by School-Size Score, Not by Module Tier) — a REAL ARCHITECTURAL FORK from how NEYO is priced TODAY, flagged prominently
- [ ] **CRITICAL, must-read-first finding: this idea directly CONTRADICTS the real, live pricing architecture NEYO has today** — confirmed by direct code read of `src/lib/core/plans.ts` (G.23, the founder's OWN prior explicit request, quoted verbatim in the file's own header comment: "THE BILLING SYSTEM SHOULD BE AS DETAILED SO THAT NEYO THE COMPANY CAN HAVE DIFFERENT PACKAGES") — NEYO's live plans (`Free Karibu`/`Msingi`/`Pro`/`Elite`) EACH carry their own real `includedModules: string[]` (which module keys that specific tier unlocks) and a real à-la-carte `ADD_ONS` array (Hostel module KES 2,500/term, Transport module KES 2,500/term, Inventory & Cafeteria KES 2,000/term, Priority Support KES 3,000/term, etc. — real, live, currently-sellable add-on modules). This is EXACTLY the "Report cards require Pro, Timetable requires Enterprise, Inventory is another upgrade" model the outside AI agent explicitly argues AGAINST in the founder's pasted conversation. **This is not a small gap to fill in — it is a genuine, explicit business-model pivot the founder would need to consciously decide on, since it means UNDOING/replacing a real system the founder themselves previously asked to be built this way (per G.23's own founder-quote header).** Flagging this prominently and explicitly rather than quietly treating it as "just another feature to add," since building U.4 without first resolving this contradiction with the founder would mean building something that actively conflicts with a real, live, already-monetized system.
- [ ] **Real precedent the codebase ALREADY has for exactly this "usage-based, not tier-based" alternative shape, worth reusing rather than inventing from scratch**: `PlanDef.perStudentPerTerm` (already a real field on every plan, `plans.ts`) is PRECISELY the "price scales with school size" mechanism the founder/outside-AI are describing — it already exists as an optional PER-STUDENT charge layered on top of a plan's flat base price. The real gap is not "build a size-based pricing concept from nothing," it's "decide whether to RETIRE the tiered `includedModules`/à-la-carte-add-on system entirely and make `perStudentPerTerm`-style scaling (extended to also weigh staff count, campuses, boarding, etc. — the founder's own proposed "School Size Score" formula) the ONLY pricing lever, with every school getting every module regardless of size." A real, computed "School Size Score" (students + teachers + staff + campuses + boarding, explicitly EXCLUDING parent-account count per the outside AI's own reasoning — charging per parent could perversely discourage a school from inviting parents onto the platform, undermining real parent engagement, a genuinely good real insight worth preserving) does not exist as a formula anywhere today and would be a real, new, comparatively contained calculation to build ONCE the founder decides to pursue this direction.
- [ ] **Real, substantial technical/business work needed if the founder does choose this direction (not enumerated by the outside AI, but real and necessary)**: (a) a real migration path for EXISTING paying schools already grandfathered onto the old tiered pricing (`Tenant.grandfatheredPrice`, A.5's real price-locking mechanism) — do existing customers get moved to the new capacity-based model, or do they stay on their old plan forever (a real, and likely contentious, customer-facing decision); (b) the real internal "pricing engine" the founder/outside-AI describe (`Monthly Cost = Infrastructure + Storage + AI + OCR + Support estimate + margin`) is itself blocked on U.1's real cost-tracking foundation — you cannot build an accurate internal cost-based pricing formula without first having real cost data to feed it, reinforcing that U.1 should likely be sequenced BEFORE U.4's "internal pricing engine" half, even if the founder decides to pursue the "every school gets every feature" marketing/UX change sooner.
- [ ] **Real, comparatively SMALL and immediately actionable sub-piece, if the founder wants to test the WATERS before committing to the full pivot**: keep the existing tiered plans/add-ons system fully intact (zero risk to current revenue/customers), but add a NEW, parallel "Neyo Complete" plan option (a genuinely new `PlanDef` entry in the existing real `plans.ts` array — `includedModules` set to literally every real module key, priced via a real, newly-computed School Size Score instead of a flat base price) that new signups could choose ALONGSIDE the existing tiers, rather than replacing them outright — a real, low-risk way to test the founder's instinct in the live market before a full pivot. Recommend `ask_user` explicitly present this "test it as a new option first" path as an alternative to "replace everything immediately," since the founder may not have considered a middle ground.
- [ ] **Real, precise flag on the founder's own explicit correction regarding profit targets**: the founder has, in prior sessions (visible in this file's own B.24 Owner Dashboard section), already built a REAL "collection target %"/profitability concept for SCHOOLS (a school's OWN fee-collection rate vs their own target) — the outside AI's advice about NEYO's OWN company profit margin (95% vs. "healthy gross margin") is a SEPARATE, company-level concern, not to be confused with the schools' own collection-rate feature that already exists; worth being precise about this distinction so a future session doesn't conflate "NEYO's own margin" with "a school's fee-collection %," which are two completely different real numbers in two completely different real dashboards (Founder Ops vs. a school's own Owner Dashboard, B.24).

## U.5 — Storage Economics for a New School (Onboarding Estimation, Never-Auto-Delete Real Records, Fair Use Policy, Video Compression)
- [ ] **Real audit finding: NEYO's onboarding flow already asks for close to the RIGHT inputs, but doesn't yet use them for a real storage/cost ESTIMATE** — `onboarding.service.ts`'s `signupSchool()` (G.3) already collects student/staff counts and curriculum choice at signup time (confirmed via the real onboarding wizard steps documented in this file's own G.3 section) — the real gap is that this data is not currently fed into any real storage-usage ESTIMATE or shown back to the school as "here's roughly what to expect," matching the outside AI's exact recommendation ("ask questions they already know the answers to... Neyo can then estimate infrastructure requirements internally... the principal never needs to think about gigabytes"). **This is a real, comparatively small, additive feature**: a new estimation function (e.g. `estimateStorageForSchool(studentCount, staffCount, hasBoardingSection, ...)` — a real formula using AVERAGE real per-student/per-staff storage figures NEYO could derive from its OWN real existing schools' actual `StoredFile`/`TenantStorageProvider.storageUsedBytes` data, refining the formula over time exactly as the outside AI suggests) feeding into the EXISTING real `TenantStorageProvider` model (already has `storageLimitBytes` — R.7's real per-school storage-limit system already exists and already has real usage-threshold warning logic, per `statusFor()` in `storage-vault.service.ts`) rather than a new storage system.
- [ ] **Real, IMPORTANT confirmation the founder should hear directly: NEYO's real behavior TODAY already matches the outside AI's "never auto-delete important records" recommendation** — confirmed via a full grep across `src/lib/jobs/registry.ts` and every service file for any automatic hard-deletion of student/fee/attendance/exam data: the ONLY automatic cleanup job that exists is G.8's real "data-retention/auto-archive scheduler," and confirmed via direct reading of its own real behavior (this file's own G.8 entry) — it clears EXPIRED READ NOTIFICATIONS and old ARCHIVE LOGS specifically, never real academic/financial/attendance records. G.6's real Recycle Bin / soft-delete pattern (`deletedAt` fields, `tenantDb()`'s own real soft-delete enforcement) means even a STAFF-INITIATED delete of a real record (e.g. a student profile) is a real, RECOVERABLE soft-delete by default, not a true hard-delete — this is already the safe, correct behavior the outside AI recommended, and NEYO already does it. **Recommend explicitly telling the founder this is a non-issue on the current system** — there is no real risk of NEYO silently destroying academic/fee/attendance history to save storage costs, that protection already exists structurally.
- [ ] **What genuinely IS a real, currently-missing opportunity, matching the outside AI's more precise framing ("clean up temporary/abandoned items, never permanent records")**: a real audit of what counts as truly "temporary" in NEYO today — Bundi Intelligent's own `StoredFile` rows created mid-pipeline for OCR processing (uploaded scan images that are only ever needed transiently during import, not as a permanent record once the import is committed) are a real, concrete, identifiable candidate for a genuinely safe real cleanup job, since they are explicitly NOT the kind of permanent record (marks/fees/attendance/report cards) the outside AI warns against deleting. This would be a real, new, narrowly-scoped job — distinct from G.8's existing retention job, which doesn't currently touch these files at all (confirmed via the same grep) — and should explicitly whitelist ONLY genuinely-transient upload categories, never anything resembling a permanent academic/financial record.
- [ ] **A real Fair Use Policy for storage — genuinely new, does not exist today**: `TenantStorageProvider` already has real usage tracking and real upgrade-prompt logic (R.7), but no real "this usage pattern is clearly outside normal school use" DETECTION exists (e.g. a school suddenly storing thousands of unrelated large video files) — a real, buildable addition once basic usage-pattern analysis exists (average file size/category mix compared against the school's own historical baseline, or against other real schools of similar size), flagged as a genuinely new detection capability, not an extension of anything that exists today.
- [ ] **Video compression/duration limits — genuinely new, confirmed via the same grep as Part T's earlier audit: zero video-handling code exists anywhere in NEYO today** (only real image resize/EXIF-strip via `sharp`, A.9). Building real server-side video compression/transcoding is a materially bigger real technical undertaking than image processing (would likely need a real transcoding service/library, e.g. `ffmpeg`-based, which is not currently a dependency anywhere in this codebase) — flag this explicitly as one of the larger individual technical asks buried inside this batch of ideas, not a quick addition alongside the existing image pipeline.

## U.6 — Optional, School/Parent-Payable Add-Ons: Student Digital Portfolio Storage Fee + CBC/CBE Video/Photo Evidence Capture — ⚠️ MOSTLY ALREADY BUILT, read this before doing anything
- [ ] **🔴 CRITICAL FLAG, read first**: **the "Student Digital Portfolio" feature the founder is describing here — including project photos/videos, teacher assessment, CBC/CBE evidence, and a portfolio that follows a learner through their years at school — is ALREADY FULLY BUILT in this exact codebase, as `J.7 — Student Portfolio System`** (confirmed COMPLETE and re-verified 2026-06-29, per this file's own J.7 section, real full-stack test `scripts/j7-student-portfolio-fullstack-test.ts`, 11 real checks, currently green). The real, live `PortfolioItem` model already supports: project/video/photo/art/coding-work/certificate/teacher-observation/community-activity entries; real encrypted `StoredFile`-backed uploads (never a placeholder); a real teacher-approval workflow before a parent/public can see an item; real parent/student timeline viewing; real linking to competencies/subjects/clubs/awards (a DIRECT real match for "CBC/CBE evidence," since J.4's real Competency Framework + J.5's real Rubrics & Evidence systems are exactly what CBC/CBE assessment evidence needs, and J.7 already links to them); real media-size limits (50MB hard cap, 10MB warning) WITH real storage-usage warnings surfaced in the UI; and a real full export/transfer pack (so a portfolio genuinely follows a learner, matching the founder's own "by the time they finish Grade 9, their portfolio contains..." vision almost exactly, including the transfer/continuity aspect via J.14's real Transfer Passport feature working alongside it).
- [ ] **What is genuinely NEW here, on top of the already-complete J.7 system — a comparatively small, well-scoped set of real additions, NOT a new feature from scratch**:
  - [ ] **Mobile-capture-from-home framing** — J.7's real upload mechanism already accepts photo/video files via the existing real `FileUpload` component; the founder's specific new framing ("a student at home finishes a practical activity, opens Neyo, takes a photo or uploads a short video, the teacher receives it") is really just confirming the EXISTING J.7 submission flow already works this way for a student with portal access — worth a real UX/copy pass (make the "add evidence from home" framing more prominent/discoverable) rather than new backend work, though worth confirming this flow is genuinely mobile-camera-friendly (a real device-camera capture prompt on the upload input, not just a file picker) — a small, real, verifiable UI detail to check, not a structural gap.
  - [ ] **"For a boarding school, teachers can add evidence on behalf of students"** — real, precise, genuinely NEW gap: confirmed via direct read of `portfolio.service.ts`'s real submission logic that a `PortfolioItem` is created by/for a specific student; whether a TEACHER can currently submit an item ON BEHALF OF a student (as opposed to only approving a student's own self-submitted item) needs direct re-confirmation by whoever picks this up (a real, small, precisely-answerable code question, not a guess) — if this "staff submits for a student" path doesn't exist, it's a small, well-scoped real addition to an already-complete system, not a new one.
  - [ ] **Real billing/payment framing — "the school can choose to enable it... covered by the school or parents"**: THIS is the genuinely new, currently-missing piece. J.7 is currently either fully on or off per the platform-wide Part-J feature toggle (`assertJFeatureEnabled("J.7")`, default ON, company-controlled via the same real `jfeature:` `PlatformFlag` mechanism P.6/every other Part-J feature uses) — there is no PER-SCHOOL opt-in toggle for portfolios specifically, and there is definitely no real BILLING mechanism attached to it (no "portfolio storage add-on" charged to the school, and no mechanism at all for a school to pass a portfolio-storage cost through to PARENTS specifically, which would be a genuinely new kind of charge — every other real parent-facing payment in NEYO today is a fee/invoice/activity payment for the STUDENT's own account, never a platform-feature subscription fee charged directly to a parent). **Real open questions for `ask_user`**: should this be modeled as a new J.23-style Revenue Add-on (the existing real `ADD_ONS`/`REVENUE_FEATURE_KEYS` pattern, e.g. `extra_storage` already exists as a real per-term add-on a SCHOOL pays for) — likely the more natural fit for "the school pays," reusing a real existing mechanism; but "parents pay directly for a platform feature" has no real precedent anywhere in this codebase today and would need real new billing plumbing (who does NEYO actually collect the parent payment through — an M-Pesa charge outside the school's own Paybill, or does the school still collect it and NEYO just prices the add-on into what the school charges the family?) — this is a real, non-trivial new billing relationship, not just a checkbox.
- [ ] **Real recommendation for whoever picks this up next**: read J.7's own full existing write-up in this file CAREFULLY before writing a single line of code — the actual net-new work here is almost entirely about SCHOOL-LEVEL OPT-IN + BILLING, not about the portfolio/evidence-capture mechanism itself, which is real, live, and already thoroughly tested.

## U.7 — Cloudflare R2 Cost Model Confirmation + "Unlimited Storage Under Fair Use" Messaging (never expose raw GB numbers to a school)
- [ ] **Real audit finding: NEYO's storage architecture is ALREADY built the way the outside AI recommends, confirmed by direct code read** — `src/lib/storage/provider.ts` (A.9) already uses Cloudflare R2 in production (confirmed via the codebase's own real R2Provider/S3-compatible implementation, with a local-dev fallback provider when R2 credentials aren't configured) — this is not a proposal, it is the REAL, already-built, already-live storage backend. `TenantStorageProvider.storageLimitBytes`/`storageUsedBytes` (R.7) already gives NEYO real internal per-school usage tracking without requiring the SCHOOL to think about gigabytes — the school-facing UI (per R.7's own documented UX) already shows warnings/upgrade-prompt language, not a raw byte-count-first interface. **Whether the school-facing copy specifically uses the outside AI's exact recommended phrasing ("Unlimited storage under our Fair Use Policy") is a real, small, verifiable copy question** — worth a direct re-read of the live `storage-vault-client.tsx` UI copy to confirm it doesn't currently show a literal "X GB of Y GB used" style number prominently (a small, easy, real copy audit, not a structural change) — flag this as a possible quick win if the current copy IS too gigabyte-literal today.
- [ ] **The real "Fair Use Policy" ENFORCEMENT mechanism itself (detecting genuinely abusive/outside-intended-use storage patterns) is the same real, currently-missing capability already flagged under U.5 above** — do not treat U.5 and U.7 as two separate features to build; they are the same real gap described twice from slightly different angles in the founder's two pasted conversations. Merge these when scoping.


# PART V — NEYO Capacity-Based Pricing System 2.0 (founder-confirmed pivot, 2026-07-06) — FULLY BUILT, TESTED & VERIFIED (2026-07-06)

> **Founder's own words, confirmed real decisions (do not re-litigate these — they are settled)**: "neyo and i the founder would like to change the pricing system... schools onboarding data will be used to detect the price... according to the number the price is set... when an increase is noticed by either a certain percentage that the company puts a new price is introduced cause the users have increased a decrease is never considered in the company at all." This Part supersedes U.4's more tentative "should we pivot?" framing — **the founder has confirmed YES, pivot, and has answered the load-bearing design questions via a real `ask_user` session** (captured verbatim below). This is now a real, scoped, ready-to-build project — but per the founder's own explicit request ("start over the pricing section right away... brainstorm as more as possible... a very well designed system"), this turn is SPEC ONLY, exhaustively brainstormed and written down, so the actual CHUNK-by-CHUNK build (a large, multi-session project) starts from a complete blueprint rather than being designed as it's coded.

## V.0 — Founder's Confirmed Real Answers (the load-bearing decisions, verbatim + interpreted)
- [x] **Existing customers**: "migrate everyone now" — every real school, including the two currently-live seeded tenants already on the old tiered plans (Karibu High, Uhuru Academy), moves onto the new usage-based system. **Real implication**: there is no long-term dual-system support to build — the OLD `PlanDef.includedModules`/à-la-carte-add-on system (`plans.ts`, G.23) becomes fully retired for PRICING purposes once V is live (though the underlying MODULE-ENABLEMENT mechanism, `TenantModule`, stays — see V.1, "every feature" doesn't mean every module is force-enabled, it means none are PRICE-gated).
- [x] **What counts toward the price**: students + staff + storage used, confirmed. Parent accounts DO count — but the founder's own precise correction: "i wouldnt count the actual live parents just all parents either live or dormant" — meaning EVERY real `Guardian`/parent `User` row linked to the school counts toward the size score, regardless of whether that parent has ever logged in or is currently active — a deliberately simple, gameable-resistant rule (a school can't reduce their score by having inactive parents, since inactive ones count the same as active ones; this also removes any perverse incentive to under-invite parents, which was the outside AI's own original concern in the earlier ideas batch — the founder's answer solves that concern differently but just as effectively).
- [x] **First-launch pricing needs to be known immediately, before real usage exists**: "after they put their data eg parents students staff and any other thing they get their price in their first launch so that they know the amount of money they would pay" — a real, precise requirement: at the END of onboarding (`signupSchool()`), before the school has uploaded a single real file, NEYO must show a real, computed price based on the school's OWN entered numbers (expected/current student count, staff count, parent count) — meaning the pricing engine must work from DECLARED numbers at signup, then later reconcile against REAL measured numbers (storage actually used, actual enrolled counts) once the school is live.
- [x] **Storage must be estimated, not measured from real uploads, for pricing purposes — and must NEVER be shown to the school as a number**: "in storage the system can guess the documents uploads downloads... but the schools should never realize that the storage is calculated they just get a statement with free storage per fair policy." **This is a real, deliberate, important design choice — NOT the same as R.7/R.7-era real storage TRACKING (`TenantStorageProvider.storageUsedBytes`, which is real, measured, byte-accurate today)**: the founder wants pricing to be driven by a real ESTIMATE (a formula from student/staff/parent counts and typical document/photo/report-card volume) rather than the school's actual measured bytes — likely so the number is stable/predictable rather than fluctuating with real day-to-day upload activity, and so it can be computed instantly at signup before any real files exist. The REAL measured storage (already tracked) still matters for the Fair Use safety net (catching genuine abuse) but is never the PRIMARY pricing input, and the school-facing copy must always read like a free-storage/Fair-Use-Policy statement, never "you are paying for storage" or "you have used X GB."
- [x] **Reprice trigger**: "both" — confirmed the founder wants BOTH a real overall/company-wide threshold AND the ability to set different thresholds per factor (e.g. students growing 15% triggers a reprice, storage/estimated-storage needing a materially bigger jump like 40% before IT alone triggers one, since storage is the "crucial" factor the founder explicitly flagged as needing extra care). **Real implication**: NEYO Ops needs a real settings panel with (a) one overall/default threshold percentage, AND (b) the ability to override it per factor (students/staff/parents/storage each get their own optional threshold, falling back to the overall default when not set).
- [x] **Timing + a very specific, deliberate communication strategy**: the founder's own precise words are the single richest, most important part of this whole answer and must be followed exactly, not paraphrased loosely: **"the system tells them due to the new users and the extra storage facilities you use in neyo and above the fair policy threshold you will be required to add a certain amount to your next billing"** — meaning REAL, HONEST disclosure of WHY the price is increasing (new users, extra storage above the fair policy threshold) IS given to the school, framed around SPECIFIC REAL CAUSES rather than a bald percentage — **BUT** — **"i would suggest you hide the users increase cause they may request a price drop if their users decrease but if it drastic it can be heard maybe the same decrease percentage maybe"** — meaning: (1) do NOT show the school the exact real number of new students/staff/parents that triggered the increase (a school seeing "you went from 200 to 240 students" might reasonably ask "well now we're back to 210, can our price go down?" — the founder has already ruled out decreases entirely, and doesn't want to invite that argument by exposing the exact trigger numbers); (2) if the usage DROP is genuinely drastic (a real, large real-world event — a school closing a campus, a mass withdrawal), the founder is open to a REAL, DISCRETIONARY reduction ("it can be heard," "the same decrease percentage maybe") — but this is explicitly NOT an automatic system behavior; it's a real, human, NEYO-Ops-reviewed exception process, never a formula the school can predict or rely on. **Real implication for the notice copy**: the school-facing repricing notice should say something like "Due to your growing NEYO usage — more staff/parent accounts and additional storage beyond the standard Fair Use allowance — your next billing will include an additional KES X" — real and honest about the CATEGORY of cause, without exposing the literal before/after headcounts.
- [x] **Timing mechanics**: "option [immediate, with a top-up]... you will be required to add a certain amount to your NEXT billing" — the founder's own words land specifically on "next billing," which is actually closer to the FIRST option (apply at next renewal) than a mid-period top-up demand — **real clarification needed and flagged for a quick follow-up `ask_user` at build time**: does "next billing" mean the school's NEXT SCHEDULED renewal payment (the real, already-existing `Subscription.currentPeriodEnd` cycle, A.5) simply comes with a higher amount due, with NO extra collection mid-term (the safer, less disruptive real interpretation, and the one this spec recommends as the default design) — or does it mean a genuinely NEW, immediate top-up invoice is raised as soon as the threshold is crossed, separate from the real renewal cycle? This spec proceeds on the RECOMMENDED interpretation (next real renewal absorbs the new price, no separate mid-term collection) since it's simpler, less disruptive to real schools, and matches "next billing" literally — but this exact mechanic should be re-confirmed with the founder in one quick clarifying question at the start of the real build, since it's a materially different real billing-job design either way.
- [x] **Quote-to-live flow**: "option 2 [self-serve once quote is accepted] but they can be assisted in importation of data and staff training too and any other thing maybe and i would guess a guide into the neyo systems" — a real, precise, hybrid answer: the ACCOUNT activation itself is self-serve/automatic the moment a school accepts a real quotation (no NEYO Ops manual approval gate blocking go-live) — but NEYO still offers real, optional HUMAN assistance alongside that automatic activation: data-import help, staff training, and "a guide into the NEYO systems" (a real onboarding/walkthrough experience, not just a bare empty dashboard). **Real implication**: the "go live" button itself triggers real automatic account activation (reusing the real, already-built `signupSchool()`/`ensureSubscription()` machinery), while a SEPARATE, parallel real request (e.g. "Request onboarding help" — data import assistance, a training session, a site visit) is offered as a real, optional, NEYO-Ops-visible follow-up ticket, not a blocker.

## V.1 — Core Philosophy: "Neyo Complete" — Every Real Feature Included, Priced by a Real School Size + Usage Score
- [x] **What "every feature" really means, precisely, so nobody misreads this**: it does NOT mean every `TenantModule` is force-enabled for every school regardless of whether they want it (a school with no boarding section should obviously still be able to leave the Hostel module off in their own Settings — the REAL, existing `TenantModule.enabled` mechanism, A.2.6, stays exactly as-is for a school's own preference). It means NO module is ever PRICE-LOCKED behind a plan tier — a school on the new system can turn ANY real module on for themselves at zero incremental license cost, with their subscription price driven purely by their real size/usage score, never by which modules they've chosen to enable. **Real implication**: `PlanDef.includedModules` (the current tier-gating field) is retired for pricing purposes; `MODULE_KEYS`/`TenantModule` (the actual on/off mechanism) is untouched and still fully real and necessary — this is a licensing-model change, not a module-system change.
- [x] **What's explicitly kept SEPARATE and usage-billed, per the founder's own earlier-confirmed T.2/U.4-era instincts, reconfirmed consistent with this new answer**: SMS remains a real, separate, usage-based charge — NOT rolled into the size score (M.2's real `SmsMarginConfig`/margin-ledger system already handles this correctly and needs no change). AI/OCR costs (Bundi Intelligent's real per-session `costUsd`/`costKes`) likewise stay a real, separate, pass-through-or-fair-use-governed cost, not baked into the core size score, at least initially — flagged as a real open question for whether AI/OCR usage should ALSO feed into a school's size score over time, similar to storage, once real usage patterns are better understood (recommend starting WITHOUT this, adding it later only if real data shows it's needed, per the founder's own "keep it simple, hide the mechanics" instinct).

## V.2 — The Real "School Size + Usage Score" Formula (the actual pricing engine)
- [x] **Real, concrete proposed formula** (a starting point for NEYO Ops to tune via real, live-editable weights — never hardcoded in a way that requires a code change to adjust, reusing the exact real `PlatformSetting`-JSON-config pattern this entire codebase already uses everywhere for company-tunable numbers — G.23's pricing catalog, M.1/M.2's referral/SMS-margin config, R.8's sibling %, S.1/S.2's shell-version release gate — ALL already follow this real, proven "NEYO Ops edits a live JSON config, the app reads it live" pattern, and V's own pricing weights should be the same, not a new pattern):
  ```
  RawScore =
      (studentCount   × WEIGHT_STUDENT)
    + (staffCount      × WEIGHT_STAFF)
    + (parentCount     × WEIGHT_PARENT)     // ALL parents, live or dormant, per the founder's own answer
    + (estimatedStorageGb × WEIGHT_STORAGE_GB)   // the ESTIMATE, never the real measured bytes, for pricing
  
  MonthlyPriceKes = BASE_FLOOR_KES + (RawScore × KES_PER_SCORE_POINT)
  ```
  Every one of `WEIGHT_STUDENT`, `WEIGHT_STAFF`, `WEIGHT_PARENT`, `WEIGHT_STORAGE_GB`, `BASE_FLOOR_KES`, and `KES_PER_SCORE_POINT` is a real, live-editable NEYO Ops number (a new `pricing_engine_v2` `PlatformSetting`-JSON key, following the exact established real pattern) — NOT hardcoded, so NEYO Ops can genuinely tune the whole pricing model over time as real cost data comes in (directly reusable in the future with U.1's real cost-tracking project, once built, to sanity-check these weights against NEYO's actual real infrastructure spend — but the pricing FORMULA itself does not need to wait for U.1 to exist; it can launch with founder-estimated starting weights and be refined later, exactly matching the founder's own "as you gather real data, you can improve these estimates" framing from the earlier ideas conversation).
  - [x] `BASE_FLOOR_KES` — a real minimum floor price so even a tiny school (a handful of students) always pays something real and non-zero, avoiding a "free forever" loophole for genuinely small paying customers (the actual FREE tier, if the founder wants one, should be a deliberate, separate, explicitly-chosen real state — see V.3 below — not an accidental byproduct of a small school's score rounding to zero).
- [x] **Storage estimate formula — the founder's own explicitly-flagged "crucial" piece, deserves its own real sub-formula**, e.g.:
  ```
  estimatedStorageGb =
      (studentCount × AVG_GB_PER_STUDENT)      // profile photo, report cards, receipts, portfolio items (J.7), OCR scans
    + (staffCount    × AVG_GB_PER_STAFF)        // profile photo, notes, uploaded documents
    + FLAT_SCHOOL_OVERHEAD_GB                    // school logo, public-site assets, shared documents
  ```
    `AVG_GB_PER_STUDENT`/`AVG_GB_PER_STAFF`/`FLAT_SCHOOL_OVERHEAD_GB` are, again, real live-editable NEYO Ops numbers — the founder's own real starting point can literally be derived from the REAL, ALREADY-MEASURED `StoredFile`/`TenantStorageProvider.storageUsedBytes` data across NEYO's own existing real seeded schools (Karibu High, Uhuru Academy) — a real, live, non-hypothetical dataset already sitting in the database RIGHT NOW that could seed these initial constants sensibly rather than guessing from nothing. **Recommend, as part of the real build, a one-time real analysis script (in the spirit of this project's existing `scripts/*-test.ts` real-data-driven verification culture) that computes real average GB-per-student/per-staff from the existing real tenants' actual measured storage, to set sensible v1 defaults for these constants** — a genuinely evidence-based starting point, not an arbitrary guess, fully in keeping with how rigorously this whole codebase already verifies everything against real data.
- [x] **The Fair Use threshold, separately from the base estimate**: a school whose REAL measured storage (the existing, already-accurate `TenantStorageProvider.storageUsedBytes`) exceeds their ESTIMATED allowance by more than a real, NEYO-Ops-configured Fair Use margin (e.g. "actual usage more than 150% of the estimate") is the trigger for the real "extra storage facilities... above the fair policy threshold" repricing cause the founder described — this is DELIBERATELY a two-layer system: layer 1 (the estimate) sets the price a school is TOLD about and never sees fluctuate with routine use; layer 2 (the real measured bytes vs. that estimate) is the silent, real safety-net check that triggers a repricing conversation ONLY when a school's real behavior meaningfully exceeds what was estimated for their size — exactly matching the founder's own two real, distinct mentions of storage ("guess the documents... never realize storage is calculated" for the PRICE, vs. "extra storage facilities... above the fair policy threshold" for the REPRICING CAUSE) as two genuinely different real mechanisms, not one.

## V.3 — Where the "Free Karibu" Tier Fits Now (a real open question, not yet resolved by the founder's own answers)
- [x] **Real gap in the founder's own answers, flagged explicitly rather than assumed**: the founder's confirmed answers describe how a PAYING school's price is set and grows — they do not explicitly say whether NEYO keeps a genuine FREE tier (today's real `free_karibu` plan, `DEFAULT_PLAN_KEY`, the plan every new signup defaults to before choosing to pay) under the new system, or whether "Neyo Complete" pricing applies from the very first real student. **Real options to present via `ask_user` at the start of the real build** (do not assume): (a) keep a genuine, real, permanently-free tier for schools under some real small size threshold (e.g. under 30 students) — likely the safer choice for continued goodwill/market entry, and consistent with the product's own name ("Free Karibu" = "Free Welcome" in Swahili, a deliberate brand choice already made); (b) retire the free tier entirely — EVERY real school pays from day one, per the new size-based formula, with `BASE_FLOOR_KES` simply being low enough for a tiny school to feel affordable; (c) keep a real, time-boxed FREE TRIAL (not a permanent tier) — e.g. the first real N days free regardless of size, then the real size-based price kicks in. This is a real, consequential decision the founder should make explicitly before the pricing engine's `BASE_FLOOR_KES`/tier logic is finalized, since it changes what `ensureSubscription()`'s real default behavior should be for a brand-new signup.

## V.4 — Real DB/Schema Design (a full CHUNK 1 blueprint, not yet migrated)
- [x] **New `PricingEngineConfig`-style `PlatformSetting` key** (e.g. `pricing_engine_v2`, JSON blob) — holds every real live-editable weight/constant from V.2 above (`WEIGHT_STUDENT`, `WEIGHT_STAFF`, `WEIGHT_PARENT`, `WEIGHT_STORAGE_GB`, `AVG_GB_PER_STUDENT`, `AVG_GB_PER_STAFF`, `FLAT_SCHOOL_OVERHEAD_GB`, `BASE_FLOOR_KES`, `KES_PER_SCORE_POINT`, `FAIR_USE_STORAGE_MULTIPLIER`, `DEFAULT_REPRICE_THRESHOLD_PCT`, and optional PER-FACTOR override thresholds `STUDENT_REPRICE_THRESHOLD_PCT`/`STAFF_REPRICE_THRESHOLD_PCT`/`PARENT_REPRICE_THRESHOLD_PCT`/`STORAGE_REPRICE_THRESHOLD_PCT`) — reusing the exact established real config-JSON-in-`PlatformSetting` pattern, zero new infra needed for this piece.
- [x] **New real `Tenant`-linked model, e.g. `TenantPricingSnapshot`** — a real, persisted row per school recording: the real `studentCount`/`staffCount`/`parentCount`/`estimatedStorageGb` figures the CURRENT active price was actually calculated from (the "baseline" a future reprice-trigger compares real current numbers against — this is the real mechanism that makes "usage grew by X% since last priced" possible; without a real stored baseline snapshot, there's nothing to compare growth against), the real computed `RawScore`/`monthlyPriceKes` that resulted, a real `calculatedAt` timestamp, and a real `reason` field (`"INITIAL_SIGNUP"` | `"REPRICE_THRESHOLD_CROSSED"` | `"MANUAL_OPS_OVERRIDE"` | `"DISCRETIONARY_DECREASE"` — the founder's own explicitly-allowed rare exception case from V.0, real and auditable, never silently automatic). A real history of these rows per school gives NEYO Ops a genuine, real audit trail of every price change and why — directly useful for U.2's future unit-economics work too.
- [x] **New real fields on `Subscription`** (or a real, cleanly-separated new one-to-one model if the founder/engineer building this prefers not to touch the existing, already-battle-tested `Subscription` model directly — flag this as a real implementation choice, not a fixed requirement): a real `pricingMode` field (`"LEGACY_TIER"` | `"SIZE_BASED_V2"`) so the real migration (V.0's "migrate everyone now" instruction) can be applied as a real, tracked, one-time data migration rather than an ambiguous silent switch — even though EVERY school ends up on `SIZE_BASED_V2` per the founder's instruction, having the real field lets NEYO Ops confirm the migration actually completed for every real tenant, and gives a real audit trail if anything needs to be investigated later.
- [x] **New real model for quotation requests, e.g. `SchoolQuoteRequest`** (V.6 below) — tenantId (or, for a NOT-YET-ONBOARDED prospective school, no tenantId yet — a real pre-tenant lead capture, since a school requesting a quote may not have signed up at all yet, only tried the real demo, G.14), real declared `studentCount`/`staffCount`/`parentCount` (or "unsure, please estimate"), a real computed `quotedPriceKes` once NEYO Ops (or the automatic engine) responds, a real status pipeline (`REQUESTED → QUOTED → ACCEPTED/DECLINED → LIVE`), and a real optional `onboardingAssistanceRequested` flag + free-text note (data-import help / staff training / "a guide into the NEYO systems," per the founder's own V.0 answer) — feeding a real, NEYO-Ops-visible follow-up task, not a blocker to going live.

## V.5 — Real Service Layer Design (CHUNK 3 blueprint)
- [x] **New `pricing-engine.service.ts`** (a new file, not an extension of the existing `pricing-catalog.service.ts`, which is the OLD tiered-plan config and should likely be left alone/eventually deprecated rather than overloaded with unrelated new logic): `computeSizeScore(studentCount, staffCount, parentCount, estimatedStorageGb, weights)` — a pure, real, easily-unit-testable function (no DB access, just real math — the kind of function this project's own regression-test culture is especially good at proving correct with simple, deterministic assertions); `estimateStorageForSchool(studentCount, staffCount, weights)` — the real storage-estimate sub-formula from V.2; `quotePriceForNewSchool(declaredCounts)` — used at real onboarding-time (V.0's "they get their price in their first launch" requirement) and by the real quote-request flow (V.6), calling the two pure functions above and persisting a real `TenantPricingSnapshot` row with `reason: "INITIAL_SIGNUP"`.
- [x] **New real repricing-check job function, e.g. `checkForRepriceTriggers()`** — scheduled via the EXISTING real `src/lib/jobs/registry.ts` cron system (no new job infrastructure needed, this project already has real, working scheduled jobs for exactly this kind of periodic check — fee reminders, term pulse, data retention, demo-purge, all real precedents). For every real active school: computes their CURRENT real `studentCount`/`staffCount`/`parentCount` (real, live counts — no estimation needed here, these are exact real numbers from `Student`/`User`/`Guardian` tables) and their current real MEASURED storage (`TenantStorageProvider.storageUsedBytes`, already tracked); compares each against the school's real stored `TenantPricingSnapshot` baseline; if ANY factor's real % growth exceeds either the real overall default threshold OR that specific factor's real per-factor override threshold (V.0's "both" answer), computes a real new price via the same `computeSizeScore()` function, and — per the founder's exact "next billing" instruction — updates the school's `Subscription`'s price to apply at the school's own real NEXT `currentPeriodEnd` renewal (never mid-cycle), creates a NEW real `TenantPricingSnapshot` row (`reason: "REPRICE_THRESHOLD_CROSSED"`) recording the new baseline, and sends a real notice via the EXISTING real `sendBillingNotice()` function in `billing.service.ts` (already real, already wired to in-app + SMS, zero new notification infrastructure needed) — with copy following the founder's own EXACT prescribed honesty level (category of cause named, exact headcount numbers never shown, per V.0).
- [x] **Real, explicit non-automatic decrease path**: per the founder's own words ("a decrease is never considered... but if it drastic it can be heard... same decrease percentage maybe"), there should be NO automatic decrease logic in `checkForRepriceTriggers()` at all — only a real, separate, NEYO-Ops-initiated manual action (e.g. `applyDiscretionaryDecrease(tenantId, newPriceKes, reason)`, real audit-logged, `TenantPricingSnapshot.reason: "DISCRETIONARY_DECREASE"`) for the rare, human-reviewed exception case — never a formula a school could predict or demand.

## V.6 — Real "Demo → Quote → Accept → Self-Serve Live + Optional Human Onboarding Help" Flow (CHUNK 4-6 blueprint)
- [x] **Real entry point, reusing what already exists**: a school tries the REAL, already-built G.14 demo (`createDemoSchool()`) — the demo experience itself needs no changes. A new real "Request a quote" call-to-action (on the demo banner/expiry screen, and/or a real public marketing page) starts the NEW real flow: a school enters their real declared student/staff/(optionally)parent counts (or the school can choose "estimate for me based on typical schools this size," a real, honest fallback for a prospect who genuinely doesn't know their exact numbers yet) → `quotePriceForNewSchool()` computes and shows a REAL, immediate price, matching the founder's own explicit "so that they know the amount of money they would pay" requirement — no waiting for a human at this step, since the whole point of the new pricing model is that it's a real, transparent FORMULA, not a negotiated one-off quote.
- [x] **Real, distinct "does the school want a human-reviewed quotation anyway" branch** — since the founder's own language explicitly describes "once the company confirms to send the quotations they get to see it," implying there IS a real human-in-the-loop review step for the formal quotation document itself (even though the underlying PRICE is computed automatically) — likely because a formal "quotation" as a real business document (something a school's board/PTA can review, matching how Kenyan institutional procurement often works) is a different real artifact than an instant on-screen price estimate. **Real proposed shape**: the instant computed price is shown immediately (satisfies "so that they know the amount"); a real "Send me a formal quotation" button creates the real `SchoolQuoteRequest` row and notifies NEYO Ops (reusing the exact real notification-cascade pattern used everywhere else in this codebase) — NEYO Ops reviews (can adjust the computed price if there's a real, justified reason — e.g. a genuine special circumstance — via a real override field, always audit-logged) and sends a real, generated PDF quotation (reusing the EXISTING real `@react-pdf/renderer` document-generation system already used for every other NEYO document — receipts, admission letters, report cards — never a new document system) to the school.
- [x] **Real "Accept & go live" step, self-serve per the founder's own confirmed answer**: once a school accepts a real quotation (a real button click, real audit-logged consent event — worth a real timestamp + IP/device capture for a genuine business-record trail, matching this project's own consistent audit-everything discipline), the REAL, ALREADY-BUILT `signupSchool()`/`ensureSubscription()` onboarding machinery runs automatically — no NEYO Ops manual gate. The school's real declared counts from the quote request seed their REAL `TenantPricingSnapshot` baseline (`reason: "INITIAL_SIGNUP"`) at go-live.
- [x] **Real, separate, non-blocking "Request onboarding help" capability**, per the founder's own explicit "assisted in importation of data and staff training too... a guide into the neyo systems": a real, optional checkbox/request at the same "accept & go live" moment (or any time after) creates a real, NEYO-Ops-visible follow-up task (could reuse T.3's own proposed real support-ticket-style model if that gets built around the same time, or a simpler standalone real flag on the `SchoolQuoteRequest`/a new lightweight model if T.3 hasn't been built yet — flag this dependency for whoever sequences the real build) — NEVER a blocker to the account actually going live, exactly matching "option 2 but they can be assisted," i.e., self-serve activation FIRST, human help OFFERED alongside it, never gating it.
- [x] **The real "a guide into the neyo systems" piece** — likely the most reusable, lowest-effort part of this whole flow: a real, structured first-login onboarding walkthrough/checklist (a genuinely new, small UI addition — a "Welcome to NEYO, here's how to get started" real guided tour or checklist screen shown once at first login for a school that just went live via this new flow) — distinct from a human-assisted session, this is a real, self-serve product feature that could exist independent of whether a school also requests human help.

## V.7 — Real NEYO Ops UI Needed (CHUNK 5 blueprint)
- [x] **A new "Pricing Engine" tab/section in `founder-ops-client.tsx`** (following the exact same established real card-based, list-based UI patterns already used by `RevenueGrantsOpsTab`/`ShellReleaseCard`/the Platform Flags tab — zero new UI paradigm needed) showing: the real live-editable weights/constants from V.4's `pricing_engine_v2` config (a real form, SUPER_ADMIN-gated exactly like every other company-level control in this codebase); the real overall + per-factor reprice-threshold percentages; a real, live "test this formula" calculator (enter hypothetical student/staff/parent/storage numbers, see the real resulting price instantly — a genuinely useful real tool for NEYO Ops to sanity-check the formula before/after any weight change, reusing the exact same pure `computeSizeScore()` function the real production code path uses, so the preview is never out of sync with reality).
- [x] **A real "Schools & Their Current Pricing" list** — every real tenant, their current real `TenantPricingSnapshot` baseline numbers, their current real price, and a real "repriced N times, last on [date]" history link — giving NEYO Ops genuine visibility into the whole real pricing landscape across the company, a natural real companion to U.2's future unit-economics dashboard.
- [x] **A real "Quote Requests" queue** (`SchoolQuoteRequest` rows, status-pipeline UI, matching the exact same real list-with-status-badges-and-actions pattern this codebase already uses repeatedly) — NEYO Ops reviews/sends formal quotations, sees onboarding-assistance requests, and can track a prospective school from "requested" through "live."

## V.8 — Real Open Questions — RESOLVED via `ask_user` on 2026-07-06 (kept here for the historical record; V.9 below is now the live, current design)
- [x] "Next billing" mechanic — **RESOLVED: wait until their next renewal.** Confirmed by the founder: a school keeps paying their current price through the rest of the period they already paid for; the new, higher price only starts applying from their NEXT real payment/renewal. Nothing is ever collected mid-term. This is the design V.9/the real build below implements.
- [x] Free tier fate — **RESOLVED: NEYO Ops decides, live, never hardcoded.** Founder's exact words: "i think you shouldnt hard code it just put it be the two options and the company can change what they would like to change in the neyo ops so the last two options" — meaning a real, NEYO-Ops-editable choice between "time-boxed free trial for everyone" and "every school pays from day one via a low floor price" (the founder explicitly ruled OUT hardcoding either into the app; a genuine permanent free tier as a THIRD option was not selected — only the "trial" and "everyone pays" options remain live choices). **Real implication for the build**: a new NEYO-Ops-editable setting, e.g. `freeTierMode: "TRIAL" | "EVERYONE_PAYS"` plus a `freeTrialDays` number when in `TRIAL` mode, inside the same real `pricing_engine_v2` config — never a fixed, code-level decision.
- [x] AI/OCR in the score — **RESOLVED: yes, folded in, but marketed as a free setup fee.** Founder's exact words: "let it be in too so that neyo can say free setup fee for all schools but behind the seen it is calculated as well" — a real, deliberate PUBLIC-FACING FRAMING decision: NEYO tells every school "no setup fee," while INTERNALLY the real formula still accounts for real AI/OCR usage cost (e.g. a real one-time or recurring AI/OCR-cost estimate folded into the same size-score calculation, exactly like storage is estimated-and-hidden today) — never shown to the school as a literal "AI/OCR charge" line item, matching the exact same "the school never realizes X is calculated" pattern already established for storage in V.0/V.2. **Real implication for the build**: `computeSizeScore()` gains a real `estimatedAiOcrUsageComponent` term (a new NEYO-Ops-editable weight, same `pricing_engine_v2` config family), and the real onboarding/marketing copy explicitly and honestly says "no setup fee" (true, since there IS no separate, additional line item the school ever sees or pays) while the number itself is already absorbed into the one real monthly price from day one.
- [x] Who grants a discretionary decrease — **RESOLVED: the CEO/top NEYO Ops account by default, but delegable.** Founder's exact words: "option 1 but when the ceo allows a staff to do so no issue eg the ceo of neyo" — meaning the REAL default is SUPER_ADMIN/founder-tier only, but the founder (as CEO) can explicitly authorize a specific staff member to also do this — a real, explicit, revocable per-person delegation, not a blanket role change. **Real implication for the build**: `applyDiscretionaryDecrease()` should real-check either `role === "SUPER_ADMIN"` OR a new, narrow, explicitly-grantable real permission/flag (e.g. a `canApplyDiscretionaryDecrease` boolean on a staff User, settable only by SUPER_ADMIN, audit-logged both when granted and when used) — never opened up to a whole role tier by default.
- [x] The literal repricing-notice wording — still to be reviewed by the founder directly once the real notice copy is drafted during the build (a small, low-risk, easy-to-revise UI-copy detail, not a blocker to starting the DB/service work).

## V.9 — Real Build Completion (2026-07-06): CHUNKS 1–8, fully built, tested, and live-verified

**Status: DONE, not a spec anymore.** Every checkbox above (V.0–V.8) reflects the actual shipped system, not the original brainstorm. This section is the real, exhaustive build evidence.

- [x] **CHUNK 1 (DB)** — Migration `20260706104826_pricing_v2_capacity_based` applied and confirmed via `prisma migrate status` ("Database schema is up to date!") repeatedly across multiple environment recoveries this session. Real schema additions: `User.canApplyDiscretionaryDecrease Boolean @default(false)`; `Subscription.pricingMode String @default("SIZE_BASED_V2")` + `Subscription.sizeBasedPriceKes Int @default(0)`; new model `TenantPricingSnapshot` (real per-school pricing history — `studentCount`/`staffCount`/`parentCount`/`estimatedStorageGb`/`estimatedAiOcrUsage`/`rawScore`/`monthlyPriceKes`/`reason`/`triggeredById`/`triggeredByName`/`note`/`calculatedAt`, indexed on `tenantId` and `[tenantId, calculatedAt]`); new model `SchoolQuoteRequest` (real quote-to-live lifecycle — `tenantId` nullable via `SetNull` since a prospect may not have a tenant yet, `declaredStudentCount`/`StaffCount`/`ParentCount`, `requestedEstimate`, `instantQuotedPriceKes`, `formalQuoteRequested`, `finalQuotedPriceKes`, `quotedById`/`quotedByName`/`quotedAt`, `status` enum `REQUESTED|QUOTED|ACCEPTED|DECLINED|LIVE`, `onboardingAssistanceRequested`/`Note`/`DoneAt`, `acceptedAt`). `src/lib/core/tenant-tables.ts` correctly registers `tenantPricingSnapshot` as tenant-owned and explicitly documents `schoolQuoteRequest` as NOT tenant-owned (queried via raw `db`, never `tenantDb()`).
- [x] **CHUNK 2 (Zod)** — `src/lib/validations/pricing-engine.ts`: `pricingEngineConfigSchema` (every weight/constant real and NEYO-Ops-editable), `defaultPricingEngineConfig()`, `quotePriceInputSchema`, `createQuoteRequestSchema`, `sendFormalQuoteSchema`, `discretionaryDecreaseSchema`, `setDiscretionaryDecreaseDelegateSchema`.
- [x] **CHUNK 3 (Service layer)** — `src/lib/services/pricing-engine.service.ts` (the real engine: `getPricingEngineConfig()`/`savePricingEngineConfig()` via the proven `PlatformSetting`-JSON pattern, audit-logged; pure functions `estimateStorageForSchool()`, `estimateAiOcrUsageForSchool()`, `estimateParentCountForSchool()` (added this session — see the parent-count privacy fix below), `computeSizeScore()`, `quotePriceForCounts()`; `getRealCurrentCounts()` for live repricing checks; `checkFairUseStorageBreach()`; `migrateTenantToSizeBasedPricing()`/`migrateAllTenantsToSizeBasedPricing()`; `checkTenantForReprice()`/`checkAllTenantsForReprice()` — the real per-factor threshold check, honest cause-only notice copy, explicit refusal to ever auto-decrease; `canUserApplyDiscretionaryDecrease()`/`applyDiscretionaryDecrease()`/`setDiscretionaryDecreaseDelegate()`; `listSchoolsWithPricing()`/`getPricingHistoryForTenant()` (added for the Ops UI)). `src/lib/services/school-quote.service.ts` (the real quote lifecycle: `instantQuote()`, `createQuoteRequest()` with real SUPER_ADMIN notification cascade, `listQuoteRequests()`/`getQuoteRequest()`, `sendFormalQuote()`, `acceptQuote()`, `markQuoteRequestLive()`, `markOnboardingAssistanceDone()`). `billing.service.ts`'s `sendBillingNotice` exported; `ensureSubscription()` sets `pricingMode: "SIZE_BASED_V2"` on new rows. `onboarding.service.ts` computes a real initial quote from declared/estimated counts at signup, creates the real `TenantPricingSnapshot` (`reason: "INITIAL_SIGNUP"`). `jobs/registry.ts` wired with a real daily `pricing-reprice-check` cron job (05:00 EAT). `api/respond.ts` handles `PricingEngineError`/`SchoolQuoteError`.
- [x] **CRITICAL correctness fix — `tier-gating.service.ts`** (flagged during this session as a direct contradiction of "every feature included"): `hasEntitlement()` now returns `true` immediately for any tenant whose `Subscription.pricingMode === "SIZE_BASED_V2"`, bypassing the old plan/add-on/grant lookup entirely — live-verified via a real script call: `hasEntitlement(tenantId, "skills_passport")` / `"advanced_analytics"` / `"custom_reports"` all returned `true` for a real freshly-signed-up SIZE_BASED_V2 tenant. The old plan/add-on/grant logic is kept intact for any hypothetical non-migrated legacy subscription.
- [x] **CHUNK 4 (API routes)** — 11 real routes, all confirmed present in the production build manifest: `GET/POST /api/platform/pricing-engine` (SUPER_ADMIN), `POST /api/quotes/instant` (PUBLIC, rate-limited 30/hr/IP), `POST /api/quotes` (PUBLIC, rate-limited 10/hr/IP), `POST /api/quotes/[id]/accept` (PUBLIC), `GET /api/ops/quotes` (SUPER_ADMIN), `POST /api/ops/quotes/[id]/formal-quote` (SUPER_ADMIN), `POST /api/ops/quotes/[id]/onboarding-assistance-done` (SUPER_ADMIN), `POST /api/ops/pricing-migration` (SUPER_ADMIN), `POST /api/ops/pricing-decrease` (any signed-in user, real authorization enforced inside the service), `GET/POST /api/ops/pricing-decrease-delegate` (SUPER_ADMIN; GET added this session to list real staff + their delegate flag), `GET /api/ops/pricing-schools` (SUPER_ADMIN; added this session for the Ops "Schools & pricing" list).
- [x] **CHUNK 5/6 (UI)** — `src/components/founder/pricing-engine-ops-tab.tsx` (new, 576 lines): live-editable weights/thresholds/free-tier form; a live client-side "test this formula" calculator mirroring the exact real server formula; "Schools & their current pricing" real list with a "Migrate everyone now" button; "Quote requests" queue with inline formal-quote-price entry + "mark onboarding assistance done"; "Discretionary-decrease delegates" list with grant/revoke. Wired into `founder-ops-client.tsx`'s `TABS` array as a new "Pricing Engine" tab. New public page `src/app/(auth)/quote/page.tsx` + `src/components/quote/quote-request-form.tsx` (the real "see your price → request a quotation → accept & go live" flow). `get-started-wizard.tsx` (the real onboarding wizard) extended with a real live instant-price preview debounced against `/api/quotes/instant`. `onboarding/signup` route links an accepted quote request to the new real tenant via `markQuoteRequestLive()`.

### Post-build correctness fixes (founder-reported, 2026-07-06, same session)

- [x] **Parent count removed from every school-facing surface — now NEYO-Ops-only, per the founder's explicit follow-up instruction.** The founder correctly caught that the public quote page and onboarding wizard were asking a school to enter its own parent count, directly contradicting V.0's own resolved answer ("the schools should never realize that [certain inputs] are calculated... they just get a statement"). **Real fix**: `src/lib/services/pricing-engine.service.ts` gained a new pure function `estimateParentCountForSchool(studentCount)` (a real, honest typical-ratio estimate — 1.3 parents per student, floor of 1 — silently computed server-side, never surfaced to a school). `school-quote.service.ts`'s `instantQuote()` and `onboarding.service.ts`'s signup-time pricing now both call this helper whenever a real declared parent count isn't supplied (which is now always, from any school-facing caller). `src/components/quote/quote-request-form.tsx` and `src/components/onboarding/get-started-wizard.tsx` both had their "Parents" input field, state, and API payload field fully removed — each now sends only `studentCount`/`staffCount` to `/api/quotes/instant`, clearly labeled "Number of students" / "Number of staff" (previously bare, ambiguous placeholder-only fields — also fixed per the founder's "which box for which number" note). The real NEYO Ops Pricing Engine tab (`pricing-engine-ops-tab.tsx`) correctly KEEPS its own "Parents (all, live or dormant)" weight field and "test this formula" calculator input — this is the one place it's meant to live, per the founder's explicit "the dormant or live parents should be only in neyo ops" instruction. **Live-verified**: `POST /api/quotes/instant` with only `studentCount`/`staffCount` in the body now returns the exact same real, correct price as before (parent count is silently estimated identically under the hood) with zero `parentCount` field in the request; Playwright screenshots confirm the public quote page and onboarding wizard now show exactly two fields ("Number of students," "Number of staff"), while the NEYO Ops tab screenshot in the same session confirms "Per parent (all, live or dormant)" is still present and untouched there.
- [x] **Curriculum renamed CBC → CBE in every real user-facing surface, founder-confirmed "full rename" scope.** Real-world context: Kenya's Ministry of Education officially rebranded "Competency-Based Curriculum (CBC)" to "Competency-Based Education (CBE)" in April 2025 (confirmed via live web search — KICD still technically develops what it internally calls "CBC" content, but the Ministry-facing brand is now CBE). **Real, deliberate implementation choice**: the internal/stored value stays `"CBC"` everywhere in the DB (enum values, `Tenant.curriculum`, `Subject.curriculum`, `Class.curriculum`, `Rubric.category`, `AssessmentDefinition.sourceModule`, seed data) — this is a real, zero-risk choice: it means ZERO data migration, ZERO schema change, and full backward compatibility with every existing row across every seeded/live tenant, while every place a human actually READS the word gets the current, correct "CBE" label. A new shared helper `curriculumLabel()` was added to `src/lib/utils.ts` (`"CBC"` → `"CBE"`, `"BOTH"` → `"CBE & 8-4-4"`, else passthrough) and wired into the two data-table badges that render a raw stored curriculum value (`academics-client.tsx`'s subject list, `classes-client.tsx`'s class list). Every other user-facing occurrence of the literal word "CBC" across the whole app was individually located and fixed to read "CBE" instead, confirmed via an exhaustive `grep -rn "\bCBC\b"` sweep of `src/**/*.{ts,tsx}` before and after, with every remaining hit manually reviewed and confirmed to be either (a) an internal file/route/service name (`/cbc` route, `cbc.service.ts`, `cbcStrandId`, `sourceModule: "CBC"`), (b) an internal state default/DB enum literal (`curriculum: "CBC"`), or (c) a code comment — never a real string a user would see. **Real files touched** (~35 distinct user-facing strings across 22 files): the onboarding wizard's curriculum picker (`CBC`/`8-4-4`/`BOTH` buttons — the literal complaint that triggered this fix), the admissions public apply-form's curriculum dropdown, reception desk's inquiry curriculum dropdown, the classes manager's curriculum dropdowns + badge, the academics subject manager's "Add CBC set" button/preset/badge/dropdown, the sidebar navigation label, the command palette (⌘K) "Go to CBC Management" entry, the help overlay shortcut label, the CBC module page's own `<h1>`, the competencies/assessments/rubrics module descriptions, the curriculum engine's onboarding copy and version-manager placeholders, the report builder's template type/placeholder, the founder ops curriculum-template-creation form, the ecosystem trends dashboard's "CBC Competency Health" card, the public marketing homepage's "CBC and 8-4-4 pathways" section, the printed report-card PDF's "(CBC ASSESSMENT REPORT)" heading, the KICD-format competency-report PDF's internal document title metadata, the default seeded "CBC Comprehensive Rubric" name/description (category value itself stays `"CBC"`, rendered as CBE by the fixed badge), and multiple seed-data strings (Karibu High's public-site hero copy, subject name "English (CBC)" → "English (CBE)", landing-page feature bullets). **NOT changed** (explicitly out of scope per the "internal code stays CBC" design choice): route paths (`/cbc`), file/component/service names, the stored DB enum value itself, `ASSESSMENT_SOURCE_MODULES`/`KE_SUBJECT_PRESETS` internal keys, code comments.
