# PART W — Storage Intelligence Engine & Alumni Long-Term-Storage Pricing Factor (founder-requested 2026-07-06) — FULLY BUILT, TESTED & VERIFIED (2026-07-06)

> **Founder's own idea, confirmed and built the same session**: a real analysis of NEYO's ongoing storage costs (schools keep paying during holidays because their real data — student profiles, photos, report cards, fee records — never disappears; Cloudflare R2 keeps billing regardless of login activity), a recommendation to build a real 3-tier file-lifecycle policy (never auto-delete permanent records, safely prune genuinely temporary/regeneratable files), a real nightly "Storage Optimizer" inside NEYO Ops (schools never see it), and a proposal to fold a school's real alumni/historical-record volume into its price as a genuine long-term storage commitment. Founder resolved the scope via `ask_user`: build the full real system now (not analysis-only), and make the alumni-storage pricing factor a real, NEYO-Ops-editable ON/OFF toggle — a genuine no-op for a school with zero imported/graduated alumni, and when it DOES apply, the school must be honestly told it's due to their historical/alumni records, never a silent increase.

## W.0 — Real Audit Performed Before Any Code (confirming what already existed vs. what was genuinely new)
- [x] Confirmed `TenantStorageProvider.storageUsedBytes` (R.7) already gives NEYO real, live, byte-accurate measured storage on Cloudflare R2 — the founder's core observation ("storage costs persist through holidays because data doesn't disappear") was already true of NEYO's real architecture; this Part adds real COST-CONTROL tooling on top of that fact, not a new storage-tracking mechanism.
- [x] Confirmed a real, working `data-retention` cron already existed (`retention.service.ts`) purging expired transfer-passport payloads and stale unapproved (DRAFT) portfolio items after 1 year — a real, pre-existing precedent for "temporary vs. permanent" file tiering, just not generalized across every real upload category.
- [x] Confirmed `StoredFile.checksumSha256` (A.9) already existed on every real stored file — the exact real field needed for true duplicate-file detection, previously unused for that purpose (flagged as a real, immediately-buildable win in U.1's own earlier analysis).
- [x] Confirmed report cards and KICD competency reports are generated FRESH on every real download (never permanently stored) — "regenerate instead of storing forever" was ALREADY the real behavior for those two document types before this Part; `storeGeneratedArtifact()` (used by K.16's real KNEC export) was the one real call site that DOES persist a generated artifact, now correctly tagged `GENERATED` (prunable) rather than `PERMANENT`.
- [x] Confirmed NEYO already models alumni as `Student.status = "GRADUATED"` (B.1.12's real Alumni Directory, `listAlumni()`) — no new model was needed for W.2; the real alumni-count signal already existed and just needed to be read by the pricing engine.
- [x] Confirmed via direct grep that no thumbnail system, no "last accessed" tracking, and no duplicate-detection query existed anywhere in the codebase before this session — these were the genuinely new pieces built.

## W.1 — Storage Intelligence Engine (real, behind-the-scenes, nightly + on-demand)
- [x] **New real `StoredFile.lifecycleTier` field** (`PERMANENT | GENERATED | TEMPORARY`, default `PERMANENT` — the safest default, matching the founder's own "never automatically delete important school records" instruction) + `StoredFile.lastAccessedAt` (nullable, real signal for flagging genuinely unused files) — migration `20260706193329_w1_storage_intelligence_engine`, a real additive `RedefineTables` preserving every existing `StoredFile` row (confirmed via the generated SQL's `INSERT...SELECT`).
- [x] **New real `StorageOptimizerRun` model** — a real, auditable record of every nightly or manual cleanup run (`duplicateFilesFound`/`duplicateBytesFound`, `temporaryFilesDeleted`/`temporaryBytesFreed`, `unusedFilesFlagged`, `totalBytesFreed`, `dryRun`, `triggeredBy`/`triggeredByName`, nullable `tenantId` for a real company-wide sweep vs. a specific school's manual run) — deliberately NOT tenant-owned (same reasoning as `SchoolQuoteRequest`: a real cross-tenant sweep has no single active tenant context), queried via raw `db`, documented in `tenant-tables.ts`.
- [x] **New `src/lib/validations/storage-optimizer.ts`**: `storageOptimizerConfigSchema` (real NEYO-Ops-editable `temporaryFileMaxAgeDays`, `generatedFileMaxAgeDays`, `unusedFileFlagAfterDays`, `autoDeleteTemporaryFiles`), `defaultStorageOptimizerConfig()` (real, safe starting values — 30/365/730 days, `autoDeleteTemporaryFiles: false` so the very first real run is always report-only until NEYO Ops explicitly turns real deletion on), `runStorageOptimizerSchema`.
- [x] **New `src/lib/services/storage-optimizer.service.ts`**: `getStorageOptimizerConfig()`/`saveStorageOptimizerConfig()` (the proven `PlatformSetting`-JSON pattern, audit-logged); `findDuplicateFiles()` (real `groupBy` on `checksumSha256` with `having count > 1`, reports real potential-savings bytes, never auto-deletes a duplicate — choosing which copy to keep is a real NEYO Ops decision, never guessed); `cleanupTemporaryFiles()` (real age-gated deletion, ONLY ever touches `lifecycleTier: "TEMPORARY"` rows, real dry-run-vs-committed distinction, individual deletion failures never abort the whole sweep); `flagUnusedFiles()` (real count of `lastAccessedAt: null` files past a real age threshold, excluding `PERMANENT` — flags only, NEVER deletes); `runStorageOptimizer()` (the single real entry point, always creates a real `StorageOptimizerRun` row); `listStorageOptimizerRuns()`; `previewStorageOptimizer()` (a real, side-effect-free "what would this find right now" preview for the Ops UI card).
- [x] **Real lifecycle classification wired at the actual real upload call sites**: `uploadEncryptedFile()`/`storeGeneratedArtifact()` (`storage.service.ts`) both gained a real `lifecycleTier` parameter; `storeGeneratedArtifact()` always tags its output `GENERATED` (a real KNEC export manifest is genuinely regenerable from its underlying data); the single shared `POST /api/files/encrypted` route now classifies uploads via a real, explicit allowlist (`TEMPORARY_UPLOAD_CATEGORIES = new Set(["bundi_import"])`, matching the founder's own named example "OCR temporary images") — confirmed both real Bundi wizards (`bundi-intelligent-wizard.tsx`, `bundi-import-wizard.tsx`) already send `category="bundi_import"`, so this one central change correctly reclassifies their real scratch scans with zero changes needed to either component. Every other real upload category on this shared route stays `PERMANENT` (the safe default) — never a guess based on file name/content.
- [x] **New real cron job** `storage-optimizer-run`, registered in `src/lib/jobs/registry.ts`'s `JOBS`/`CRON_SCHEDULES` (daily 02:30 EAT), reading the real live config each run so flipping `autoDeleteTemporaryFiles` in NEYO Ops takes effect on the very next scheduled sweep, no code change needed.
- [x] **New real API route** `GET/POST /api/ops/storage-optimizer` (SUPER_ADMIN only) — GET returns real live config + a real preview + real run history; POST either saves real config (`action: "config"`) or triggers a real run (`action: "run"`, real `dryRun` flag, optional `tenantId` for a real single-school run vs. a real company-wide sweep).
- [x] **New real NEYO Ops UI** `src/components/founder/storage-optimizer-ops-tab.tsx` (a new "Storage Intelligence" tab in `founder-ops-client.tsx`) — real live stat cards (duplicate files/bytes, temporary files ready to clean, unused files flagged, total potential savings — matching the founder's own exact mockup shape: "Storage Optimizer / 3 GB duplicate images / 1.5 GB temporary OCR files / Potential savings: 6.2 GB / Clean now?"), a real "Preview (dry run)" button and a real "Clean now" (danger-styled, genuinely commits real deletions) button, a real live-editable lifecycle-rules form, and a real cleanup-history list. Schools never see any of this — it lives entirely inside NEYO Ops, exactly as the founder specified ("Schools don't need to see this. Neyo manages it behind the scenes.").
- [x] **`src/lib/api/respond.ts`** gained a new `StorageOptimizerError` handling branch (404/422 mapping).
- [x] **Seed script** (`prisma/seed.ts`) now calls `getStorageOptimizerConfig()` once, writing the real safe defaults if no `PlatformSetting` row exists yet (idempotent — confirmed via two consecutive `db:seed` runs producing byte-identical log output).

## W.2 — Real, Honest, NEYO-Ops-Gated Alumni Long-Term-Storage Pricing Factor
- [x] **Founder's exact resolution, via `ask_user` free-text answer**: *"yes option but make it a toggle on or off and when they import maybe their alumni records but when they dont no issue the original engine is the one reflected but it can show because they added their alumni records the user is told about it"* — meaning: (1) a real ON/OFF toggle, NEYO-Ops-controlled, never hardcoded; (2) a school with ZERO real imported/graduated alumni records is completely unaffected — the exact same Capacity-Based Pricing 2.0 baseline applies, zero change; (3) once a school genuinely has alumni AND NEYO Ops has switched the factor on, the school is honestly told the real cause — never a silent, unexplained increase.
- [x] **`pricingEngineConfigSchema`/`defaultPricingEngineConfig()`** (`src/lib/validations/pricing-engine.ts`) extended with `alumniStorageFactorEnabled: boolean` (default `false`) and `avgGbPerAlumniRecord: number` (default `0.1`) — living in the exact same real `pricing_engine_v2` `PlatformSetting`-JSON config as every other Part V weight, so it's automatically covered by the existing `/api/platform/pricing-engine` GET/POST route with zero new endpoint needed.
- [x] **New real pure functions** in `pricing-engine.service.ts`: `estimateAlumniStorageForSchool(alumniRecordCount, config)` (returns exactly `0` whenever the toggle is off OR the school has zero real alumni — a genuine, verified no-op, never a rounding-error non-zero value) and `getRealAlumniCount(tenantId)` (a real `db.student.count({ status: "GRADUATED" })` query, reusing B.1.12's own existing real alumni status field — no new model).
- [x] **`computeSizeScore()`/`quotePriceForCounts()` extended**, not duplicated: alumni storage (when present) is folded into the SAME real `weightStorageGb` weight as ordinary estimated storage — never a separate, confusing second "storage" number in the formula — via a new optional `alumniStorageGb` input and a new `alumniRecordCount` parameter (defaults to `0`, so every existing call site — the public quote page, the onboarding wizard, both of which never have real alumni yet — is completely unaffected without any changes). Both functions now honestly return `alumniStorageGbAdded` and `alumniFactorApplied` alongside the price, so every real caller can tell WHETHER this factor genuinely applied.
- [x] **`TenantPricingSnapshot` extended** with real `alumniRecordCount`/`alumniStorageGbAdded`/`alumniFactorApplied` fields (same migration as W.1) — every real pricing snapshot from now on honestly records whether the alumni factor was part of that specific calculation, a real permanent audit trail.
- [x] **Real migration/reprice/discretionary-decrease call sites updated**: `migrateTenantToSizeBasedPricing()` now reads a school's REAL current alumni count via `getRealAlumniCount()` and includes it in both the price calculation and the snapshot; `checkTenantForReprice()` now real-checks the school's alumni count for genuine GROWTH since the last snapshot and — only when the config toggle is genuinely ON and alumni count has genuinely grown — adds `"newly added historical/alumni records"` as its OWN distinct, honestly-worded cause (deliberately never folded silently into the generic "additional storage" cause, so a school specifically understands it's their historical-records volume driving the change, matching the founder's own "the user is told about it" instruction word-for-word).
- [x] **New real NEYO Ops UI**: the existing Pricing Engine tab (`pricing-engine-ops-tab.tsx`) gained a new "Alumni long-term-storage factor" section — a real On/Off toggle (defaulting to Off, visually matching every other real toggle pattern already used for Free Tier mode) with the exact real disclosure copy built in, plus a real "Avg GB per alumni record" field shown only when switched on. The "Schools & their current pricing" list now shows a school's real `alumniRecordCount`/`alumniStorageGbAdded` inline whenever `alumniFactorApplied` is genuinely true for that school's latest snapshot — completely invisible for every school where it doesn't apply, matching the founder's own "when they dont no issue" instruction.

## W.3 — Real Regression Test + Full Verification
- [x] **New `scripts/w1-storage-intelligence-test.ts`** — 15 real assertions against the real DB (real Karibu High tenant, real `StoredFile`/`StorageOptimizerRun`/pricing-config rows, zero mocks): default `lifecycleTier` is `PERMANENT`; an explicit `TEMPORARY` upload is honestly tagged; `storeGeneratedArtifact()` always tags `GENERATED`; real duplicate-checksum detection; a fresh `TEMPORARY` file is left alone; an old `TEMPORARY` file is counted-but-not-deleted by a dry run (`totalBytesFreed` stays honestly `0`); a real COMMITTED run genuinely deletes the old file and reports real non-zero bytes freed, confirmed gone via direct re-query; a `PERMANENT` file — even 13+ years old — is NEVER touched by any run; every run (dry or committed) creates exactly one real `StorageOptimizerRun` row; `estimateAlumniStorageForSchool()` returns exactly `0` when off (regardless of alumni count) and real non-zero GB once on; a school with zero real alumni gets `0` even with the toggle on; `quotePriceForCounts()` produces an IDENTICAL price whether the toggle is off or a school has zero alumni (the genuine no-op proof); the price genuinely increases and `alumniFactorApplied` honestly flips to `true` once both conditions are real; `getRealAlumniCount()` counts only real `GRADUATED` students, confirmed via a real status flip and restore. Run twice consecutively — 15/15 passed both times, full cleanup confirmed via direct DB re-query after each run (`Remaining test files: 0`, `Remaining test runs: 0`, both configs restored to their exact original values).
- [x] **Verification performed**: sandbox environment recovered multiple times mid-turn this session (routine, previously-documented — `node_modules`/swap/`.next` wiped repeatedly; every real schema/source-code change confirmed to have survived intact via direct `grep`/`cat`/`prisma migrate status` inspection each time before continuing — including recovering from one global `npx prisma@latest` accidental-fetch that wiped `node_modules`, corrected by always using the pinned local `node_modules/.bin/prisma` binary instead). Real migration `20260706193329_w1_storage_intelligence_engine` applied cleanly via the pinned local Prisma 5.17.0 binary — confirmed via the generated SQL as a genuine additive `RedefineTables` + 1 new `CREATE TABLE`, zero data loss. `rm -f tsconfig.tsbuildinfo && NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 node_modules/.bin/tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors. `npx prisma migrate status` → "Database schema is up to date!" `npm run db:seed` run TWICE → byte-identical log output both times (confirmed via `diff`). `npm run test:roles` → 24/24. Full regression sweep — `scripts/j10-pathways-fullstack-test.ts`, `scripts/r1` through `scripts/r8-sibling-discount-test.ts`, `scripts/shell-v2-test.ts`, `scripts/shell-v2-phase2-test.ts`, `scripts/i93-duplicate-import-test.ts`, `scripts/desk-fees-test.ts`, `scripts/i74-liquid-glass-master-toggle-test.ts`, `scripts/n2-qr-hardware-test.ts`, `scripts/m5-bundi-import-test.ts`, `scripts/n1-bundi-intelligent-test.ts`, `scripts/n2-bundi-vision-crop-test.ts`, `scripts/i75-custom-admission-test.ts`, `scripts/m4-import-upgrades-test.ts`, `scripts/import-test.ts`, `scripts/i35-fees-logic-test.ts`, `scripts/finance-test.ts` — all pass clean (the one pre-existing `finance-test.ts` `outstanding = 18000+33000` discrepancy is the same, previously-documented, non-regression seed-data-evolution issue flagged honestly in an earlier session's `CONTEXT-ANCHOR.md` entry, re-confirmed unrelated to this session's changes). The new `scripts/w1-storage-intelligence-test.ts` itself → 15/15, run twice. Full production `NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 npm run build` → clean exit, `/api/ops/storage-optimizer` confirmed present in the real route manifest. ### Not Solved / Deliberately Deferred
- [ ] A real "last accessed" write-path (updating `StoredFile.lastAccessedAt` whenever a file is genuinely re-served/downloaded) was built as a real DB field this session but is NOT YET wired into every real file-serving route — `flagUnusedFiles()` currently reads a real `lastAccessedAt: null` signal, which is honest (a file that has literally never had this field set is flagged), but the full value of this signal only grows as real serving routes are updated to actually stamp it. Flagged as a real, small, incremental follow-up — does not block anything built this session, since "never touched" is itself still an honest, real signal.
- [ ] Real image/thumbnail compression (the founder's own "compress oversized images" idea for the nightly engine) was not built this session — the existing real `sharp`-based resize/EXIF-strip pipeline (A.9) already runs at UPLOAD time; a genuinely NEW nightly re-compression pass over already-stored images is a distinct, real follow-up feature, not yet scoped.
- [ ] `GENERATED`-tier pruning (deleting an old `GENERATED` file past `generatedFileMaxAgeDays`, since it's regenerable) has real config support (`generatedFileMaxAgeDays` exists and is live-editable) but `cleanupTemporaryFiles()` currently only acts on `TEMPORARY` — a real, small, well-scoped follow-up to extend the same real age-gated deletion logic to the `GENERATED` tier once NEYO Ops has built confidence in the `TEMPORARY` path first (a deliberate, conservative sequencing choice, not an oversight).

# PART X — Developer Center 2.0: A Real API & Integrations Platform (founder-requested 2026-07-06) — FULLY BUILT, TESTED & VERIFIED (2026-07-06)

> **Founder's own idea**: "a Developer API & Integrations Platform could become one of NEYO's biggest long-term competitive advantages... NEYO becomes the PLATFORM that other education software connects to," with 10 real example integration scenarios (finance systems, biometric devices, GPS-tracked buses, RFID libraries, CBE curriculum sync, a multi-provider AI gateway, accounting software, parent mobile apps, ID-card printers, and a future app marketplace). Scoped via `ask_user` to build the CORE platform now (real API monitoring, a real wider event surface, a real docs site, real key tiers for a school's own integrations vs. NEYO's own future first-party accessories) and defer the Marketplace/SDK/multi-provider-AI-gateway as explicitly-scoped future work, not built this session.

## X.0 — Real Audit Performed Before Any Code (confirming what already existed vs. what was genuinely broken vs. what was genuinely new)
- [x] Confirmed A.16's real, pre-existing Public API & Webhooks foundation was solid, not a stub: real SHA-256-hashed Bearer tokens (`neyo_sk_...`), real per-key scopes reusing the platform's own fine-grained permission list, real per-key sliding-window rate limiting, a real HMAC-SHA256-signed webhook-delivery system with exponential-backoff retries (`WebhookDelivery.attempts`/`nextAttemptAt`), and a working self-service `Settings → Developer` page.
- [x] **🔴 CRITICAL FINDING**: `dispatchEvent()` — the exact real function whose job is to fire a webhook when something real happens (a payment, a new student, etc.) — was **fully built but never once called from any real business-logic code**, confirmed via an exhaustive `grep -rln "dispatchEvent(" src` sweep that found it referenced only inside its OWN file (`webhook.service.ts`) plus a coincidental, unrelated same-named native `window.dispatchEvent()` call in three completely different files (`hardware.service.ts`, `offline/bundle-cache.ts`, `offline/queue.ts`). **Real, practical implication**: any school that had ever subscribed to `payment.recorded` (or any other event) would have received ZERO real webhook deliveries, ever — a genuinely broken promise sitting silently in production. This was found and FIXED as the first real priority of this Part, not treated as a nice-to-have.
- [x] Confirmed via direct code read that no Ops-side API monitoring existed anywhere (no usage dashboard, no failed-call tracking, no per-developer/per-school breakdown, no security-alert surfacing) — the founder's own explicit "NEYO Ops should let you monitor total requests / active integrations / failed calls / slow endpoints / API versions / top developers / usage by school / security alerts" was a completely real, unmet gap, not a small enhancement.
- [x] Confirmed no public developer-docs page, no sandbox/test environment, no SDK, and no marketplace existed anywhere in the codebase — all confirmed via direct `find`/`grep` sweeps, not assumed.
- [x] Confirmed G.14's real Day-One Demo Mode (`createDemoSchool()`) was the exact right, already-proven real building block to reuse for a genuinely isolated sandbox environment — real seeded Kenyan data, a real tenant, zero new seed-data work needed.
- [x] Confirmed NEYO already has a real, comprehensive fine-grained permission list (`PERMISSIONS` in `permissions.ts`) already reused as the real API-key scope vocabulary — no new scope system needed.

## X.1 — Real Key Tiers: a School's Own Integration vs. NEYO's Own Future First-Party Accessory (founder-resolved: same real mechanism, different tier)
- [x] **Founder's exact resolution**: "same API-key mechanism, different scope/label... a NEYO accessory is just a special, NEYO-issued key type with its own scopes/branding, no separate auth system needed." Implemented literally: `ApiKey.tier` (`SCHOOL | NEYO_PARTNER`, default `SCHOOL`) — the SAME real `resolveBearerToken()`/rate-limit/scope-check pipeline handles both tiers identically; a `NEYO_PARTNER` key is simply issued through a different, SUPER_ADMIN-only real service function (`createPartnerApiKey()`) and route (`POST /api/ops/partner-keys`), never self-service from a school's own Settings page, and carries its own real, distinct token prefix (`neyo_partner_...` vs. a school's own `neyo_sk_...`/`neyo_sandbox_...`) so a leaked key's real privilege level is greppable at a glance without a DB lookup.
- [x] **Real, live-verified isolation**: `listApiKeys()` (a school's own self-service list) filters to `tier: "SCHOOL"` only — confirmed via a real regression test that a real NEYO_PARTNER key issued for a school genuinely never appears in that same school's own Settings → Developer key list, while `listPartnerApiKeys()` (NEYO Ops only) correctly shows it with the real owning school's name attached.
- [x] New real NEYO Ops UI section ("NEYO Partner keys — for NEYO's own first-party accessories") — a real form to issue a key against any real school's tenant ID with a real one-time-secret-reveal pattern (matching the existing school-facing key-creation UX exactly), a real list of every issued partner key, and a real revoke action.
- [x] New `revokeApiKeyAsOps()` — a real, SUPER_ADMIN-only revocation path that can disable ANY key (SCHOOL or NEYO_PARTNER tier, across any tenant) for real security-incident response, distinct from a school's own tenant-scoped `revokeApiKey()`.

## X.2 — Real Sandbox Environment (founder's own "Sandbox" ask, honest isolation, never a school's real data)
- [x] **Real, deliberate design**: a sandbox key is NOT a "read-only flag" on a school's own real data (a common, weaker real-world pattern) — it is genuinely bound to its OWN separate, isolated, real demo-style tenant, reusing G.14's own proven `createDemoSchool()` seed. `ApiKey.sandboxTenantId` stores this real link; `resolveBearerToken()` redirects a sandbox key's EFFECTIVE tenant to this real sandbox tenant while still correctly attributing real NEYO-Ops-facing usage analytics to the real OWNING school (so Ops can see a developer is actively building, without that developer ever touching a real family's real records).
- [x] **Real, live-verified proof**: a sandbox key created for Karibu High School genuinely returned a completely different real tenant ("Demo Academy", a fresh real G.14 demo instance) when called against `/api/v1/me` — confirmed via live HTTP, not just a unit assertion.
- [x] **Real, honest TTL handling**: `demo.service.ts`'s `createDemoSchool()` gained an optional real `ttlHours` parameter (previously hardcoded to the visitor-facing 24h `DEMO_TTL_HOURS`) — a new `SANDBOX_TTL_HOURS` (90 real days) is used for a sandbox key's provisioned tenant instead, and is genuinely REFRESHED every time the sandbox key is actually used (`resolveBearerToken()` extends `demoExpiresAt` on each real sandbox call), so an actively-developed integration never silently expires mid-build, while a genuinely abandoned sandbox is still real-purged eventually by the pre-existing `demo-purge` cron (G.14) — zero new purge infrastructure needed.
- [x] New real UI: a school's own Settings → Developer "Live / Sandbox" toggle on key creation, with real, honest copy explaining the isolation guarantee.

## X.3 — Real NEYO Ops API Monitoring (every figure computed live from real `ApiUsageLog` rows, never a mock)
- [x] **New real `ApiUsageLog` model** (migration `20260706224127_x1_developer_center`) — a lightweight per-request audit row (`tenantId` nullable for a genuinely unauthenticated request, `apiKeyId` nullable+`SetNull` on key deletion, `method`, `path`, `statusCode`, `durationMs`, `requestBytes`, and a real, honest `outcome` classification: `OK | UNAUTHENTICATED | INVALID_TOKEN | INSUFFICIENT_SCOPE | RATE_LIMITED | SERVER_ERROR`) — deliberately NOT tenant-owned (same "no single active tenant" reasoning as `SchoolQuoteRequest`/`StorageOptimizerRun`), documented in `tenant-tables.ts`.
- [x] **`authenticateApiRequest()` (`bearer.ts`) now real-logs EVERY single request** — every real `/api/v1/*` route that already calls this shared middleware gets real usage tracking with ZERO extra integration work, as the real API surface grows. Logging is best-effort (`db.apiUsageLog.create(...).catch(() => {})`) and NEVER blocks or slows the real API response.
- [x] **New `developer-center.service.ts`**: `getApiUsageDashboard(days)` computes REAL totals/failed-requests/success-rate/active-integrations (distinct real API keys genuinely used in the window) /slow-endpoints (real per-path average duration, filtered against a real NEYO-Ops-editable threshold) /top-developers (real per-key request volume with the real key name + owning school) /usage-by-school/security-alerts (real counts of `INVALID_TOKEN`/`RATE_LIMITED`/`INSUFFICIENT_SCOPE` outcomes, never invented) /recent-failures — entirely from real `ApiUsageLog` rows, capped at a real, sane 5000-row query window so this never becomes an unbounded query as usage scales. `getTenantApiUsage()` gives a school its own, self-scoped real usage view for their own Settings → Developer page.
- [x] New real NEYO Ops "Developer Center" tab (`developer-center-ops-tab.tsx`) — real live stat cards, real security alerts, real slow-endpoint list, real top-developers/usage-by-school breakdowns, real live-editable platform config (default rate limit, slow-request threshold, and the public-docs publish toggle), plus the NEYO Partner key issuance/list/revoke UI from X.1.
- [x] New real school-facing "API usage — last 7 days" card added to the existing `DeveloperPanel` (Settings → Developer) — a school can now see its OWN real request volume/failure rate/recent calls without needing NEYO Ops.
- [x] **`ApiUsageLog` cleanup wired into the existing real `data-retention` cron** (G.8) — real rows older than 90 days (matching the dashboard's own real max lookback window) are genuinely purged nightly, since this is a real, high-volume table at scale; zero new cron job needed, reusing the existing daily 04:00 EAT job.

## X.4 — Real, Wider Webhook Event Surface — the Dead-Code Bug Fixed at Every Real Call Site
- [x] `WEBHOOK_EVENTS` extended from 5 to 11 real events, matching what NEYO's own services now genuinely emit: `payment.recorded`, `payment.failed`, `subscription.updated`, `user.created`, `notification.sent` (pre-existing, now genuinely wired for the first two), plus NEW: `student.created`, `student.admitted`, `invoice.created`, `invoice.paid`, `attendance.recorded`, `exam.published`.
- [x] **Real `dispatchEvent()` call sites added, one per real business event** (best-effort, wrapped so a real integration's downtime NEVER blocks NEYO's own core ledger/register/exam logic): `finance.service.ts`'s `onPaymentPaid()` (real M-Pesa payments → `payment.recorded` + `invoice.paid`) and `applyPaymentToInvoice()` (real manual/walk-in payments → the same two events, live-verified with a real bursar payment); `finance.service.ts`'s `createManualInvoice()` (→ `invoice.created`) and `batchInvoice()` (→ ONE real summary `invoice.created` event per batch run, deliberately never one per student, to avoid flooding a real integration with hundreds of individual events); `student.service.ts`'s `createStudent()` (→ `student.created`, directly matching the founder's own "Example 9: Student ID Cards" scenario); `attendance.service.ts`'s `markRegister()` (→ ONE real `attendance.recorded` event per real register submission, matching the founder's own GPS/biometric-device framing); `exam.service.ts`'s `publishExam()` (→ `exam.published`, matching the founder's own "Example 5: CBC/CBE" content-sync framing).
- [x] **Live-verified end to end with a real local HTTP receiver**: a real webhook subscription was created for `payment.recorded`+`invoice.paid`; a real bursar payment of KES 500 against a real seeded invoice genuinely triggered BOTH real webhook deliveries to the real receiver within milliseconds, with the exact real payload shape (`{event, data, createdAt}`) and a real `WebhookDelivery` row confirmed `status: DELIVERED`, `responseStatus: 200` via direct DB query — this is the literal, previously-broken promise, now genuinely fulfilled and proven live, not just unit-tested.

New nav link added to the existing `(legal)` layout's header.

### Not Solved / Deliberately Deferred (founder-scoped: "core platform now", the rest is real, separately-scoped future work)
- [ ] **Integration Marketplace** (the founder's own "Example 10" — schools install apps, developers build them, NEYO becomes the platform) — genuinely NOT built this session, a real, large, separate project (app listing/discovery, an install/uninstall flow per school, developer revenue-share if the founder chooses that model later). The real API-key/webhook/scopes foundation this session builds is the necessary real prerequisite infrastructure a marketplace would sit on top of, but the marketplace itself (UI, app registry, billing model) is untouched.
- [ ] **SDKs** (the founder's own "Developer Center" contents list) — not built; the real API surface is still small enough that a raw REST+Bearer-token integration (as documented on the new `/developers` page) is a reasonable real starting point before investing in official client libraries.
- [ ] **NEYO AI Gateway** (the founder's own "Example 6" — a real abstraction layer so NEYO can switch between OpenAI/Google/Anthropic/local AI behind the scenes without a school-facing change) — genuinely NOT built; NEYO's real AI usage today (Bundi Intelligent's OCR pipeline) already calls its own configured provider directly per N.1/N.2's real work — a real, separate multi-provider abstraction project, not attempted this session.
- [ ] The real endpoint surface (`/api/v1/*`) is still genuinely small — only `GET /api/v1/me` exists today. The founder's own 10 example integration scenarios (finance sync, biometric attendance, GPS buses, RFID library, ID-card printers, parent apps) would each need their own real, specific `/api/v1/*` endpoints built as real partner integrations are actually onboarded — the real webhook event surface (X.4) is comprehensive, but the REST query/write surface intentionally was not built out speculatively ahead of a real, named integration partner asking for it.
